






























































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Ibbuku lyabansiku ba Jesu Kkilisito, mwana wakwe Devidi, mwana wakwe Abbulahamu.
Abbulahamu wakali wisi wa Ayizeki, alakwe Ayizeki wisi wa Jakobu, alakwe Jakobo wisi wa Juda abakulana bakwe.
Juda wakali wisi wa Pelezi a Zela kuli Tamala, Pelezi wisi Hezelani alakwe Hezelani wisi wa Lamu.
Lamu wakali wisi wa Aminadabbu, Aminadabbu wisi wa Nasoni, alakwe Nasoni wisi wa Salumoni.
Salumoni wakali wisi wa Bbowazi kuli Lahabbu, Bbowazi wisi wa Obbedi kuli Lute, Obbedi wisi wa Jese.
Jese wakali wisi wa Mwami Devidi Mwami, Devidi wisi wa Solomoni kuli muka Uliya.
Solomoni wakali wisi wa Lehobbowamu, Lehobbowamu wisi wa Abbija, Abbija wisi wa Asa.
Asa wakali wisi wa Jehosiafati, Jehosiafati wisi wa Jolamu, alakwe Jolamu ngusikale wa Uziya.
Uziya wakali wisi wa Jotamu, Jotamu wisi wa Ahazi, Ahazi wisi wa Hezekkiya.
Hezekkiya wakali wisi wa Manase, Manase wisi wa Amoni, alakwe Amoni wisi wa Josiya.
Josiya wakali sikale wa Jekoniya antomwe abakulana bakwe kuchindi chakutolwa kubuzike ku Bbabbiloni.
Musule lyakulonzegwa kutolwa ku Bbabbiloni, Jekoniya wakali wisi wa Sialitiyeli, Sialitiyeli wakali sikale wa Zelubbabbeli.
Zelubbabbeli wakali wisi wa Abbiyudi, Abbiyudi wisi wa Eliyakkimu, alakwe Eliyakkimu wisi wa Azola.
Azola wakali wisi wa Zadoki, Zadoki wisi wa Akkimu, alakwe Akkimu wisi wa Eliyudi.
Eliyudi wakali wisi wa Eliyazali wisi wa Matani, alakwe Matani wisi wa Jakobo.
Jakobo wakali wisi wa Josefa mulumi wa Meli, oyo wakazyala Jesu ooyo utegwa Kkilisito.
Woonse mazyalani kuzwa kuli Abbulahamu kusika kuli Devidi akali mazyalane ali ikkumi aane, kuzwa kuli Devidi kusika kukulonzegwa kwabo kutolwa ku Bbabiloni mazyalane ali ikkumi aane, alimwi kuzwa kukulonzegwa kutolwa ku Bbabbiloni kusikila kuli Kkilisito mazyalane ali kkumi aane.
Kuzyalwa kwa Jesu Kkilisito kwaka chitika munzila itobela. Banyina, Meli bakatangilwakuti bakwatwe a Jozefu, pesi kabatana kuswanana, wakajanika kuti wakali mintide kumuuya uusalala.
Pesi Jozefu, mulumi wakwe, wakali mwalumi ululeme alimwi tewakayanda kumufwisya bweeme pe chaantanganana, aboobo wakayeya kumuleka chuumunizi akusiya chizuminano chabo.
Awo mpakali kuyeeya ezi zintu, mungelo wa Mwami wakaboneka kulinguwe muchiloto, waamba kuti, “Jozefu mwana wa Devidi, utayowi pe kubweza Meli kuti abe mwanakazi wako, nkambo oyo umintidwe mulinguwe umintidwe a Muuya Uusalala.
Uyozyala mwana mulombe, alimwi uyomuzika izina lyakuti ngu Jesu, nkambo uyofutula bantu bakwe kuzwa kuzibi zyabo.”
Zyonseezi zyakachitika kuzuzikizya zyakaambwa a Mwami kwinda kubasinsiimi, wamba wati,
“Amubone, ooyo musimbi uzominta uzotumbuka mwana mulombe, mpawo izina lyakwe bazomuzika kuti ngu Imanuwele” - elyo lipandululwa kutegwa, “Leza ulandiswe.
Jozefu wakabuka kuzwa kukoona kwakwe wachita mbuli mungelo wa Mwami mbakamulayilila, mpawo wakamubweza waba mwanakazi wakwe.
Pesi takwepe nakamuziba kusika watumbuka mwana mulombe. Elyo wakamuzika izina kuti ngu Jesu.
Nikwakamana kuzyalwa kwa Jesu muBbetelehemu waku Judiya mumazuba a Mwami Helodi, balumi bayiide bazwa kujwe bakasika mu Jelusalema kabamba kuti
“ulikuli ooyo wakazyalwa kali Mwami waba Juda? Twakabona nyenyezi yakwe kujwe alimwi twaza kuzomukomba.”
Awo Helodi Mwami nakamvwa eechi, zyakamukatazya abantu boonse mbakali abo mu Jelusalemu.
Helodi wakabeta amwi boonse bapaizi bapati alimwi abalembi babantu, mpawo wakababuzya, “Nkukuli Kkilisito nkwayozyalilwa?”
Bakaamba kuti kulinguwe, “Mu Bbetelehemu wa Judiya, nkambo oobu mbubo mbukwakalembwa amusinsiimi,
Pesi iwebo, Bbetelehemu, chisi cha Judiya tamuli banini pe akati kabendelezi baJuda, nkambo kuzwa kulinduwe kuyozwa uyowendelezya, uyoyembela bantu bangu Izilayeli.”
Mpawo Helodi chakusisikizya wakiita baalumi bayiide kuti abuzye kuti nchiindinzi loko inyenyezi niyakaboneka.
Wakabatuma kuBbetelehemu, wati, “kamuya mukamulangule chabusongo, mwana munini. kuti naa mwakumujana, mundetele mazembe ambebo inga ndilabola kuzomukomba.
Nibakamaninsya kumvwa Mwami, bakeenda anzila yabo, alimwi inyenyezi njibakalibwene kujwe yakabazulwida kusikila yayimikila awo mwana munini mpakalibede.
Aboobo nibakabona inyenyezi, bakabotelwa alukondo lupati.
Bakanjila mung'anda bamubona mwana munini antomwe a Meli banyina. Bakawidaansi akumukomba. Bakavununa buvubi bwabo mpawo bamupa izipo zyangolida, tununkilizyo atwa mili.
Leza wakabachenjezya kumaloto kuti batajokeli pe kuli Helodi, aboobo bakajoka kunyika yabo anzila imbi.
Nibakabuka akwenda, mu ngelo wa Mwami wakalibonia kuli Jozefu muchiloto wamba wati, “Buka, bweza mwana munini abanyina, uchijile ku Ijipita. Ukkale mumo kusikila ndikwambile, nkambno Helodi uyomulanguula mwana munini kuti amuzimaazye.”
Mansiku ngawo aayo Jozefu wakabuka wamubweza mwana munini antomwe abanyina mpawo wanyampuka winka ku Ijipita.
Wakakkala nkukoko kusikila lufu lwa Helodi. Eechi chakazuzikizya eecho chakaambwa a Mwami kwiinda kumusinsiimi, “Kuzwa mu Ijipita ndamwiita mwana wangu.”
Mpawo Helodi, naakabona kuti weenwa abalumi bayiide, wakanyema kapati. Wakatumina akujaya boonse bana balombe bakali mu Bbetelehemu azisi zyoonse zizyungulukide bakaala minyaka ibiili kaziya ansi yakuzyalwa kakwendelana a chiindi mbuuli mbwakaziba kubaalumi bayiide.
Lino chakazuzikizya chakaambwa kwiinda kumusinsiimi Jelemiya.
“Ijwi lyakamvwigwa mu Lama, kulila a koomoka, Lakkeli ukwilila bana bakwe, alimwi wakkaka kumbulizigwa, nkambo tabachiwo.”
Elyo Helodi nakaafwa, langa mungelo wa-Leza wakaboneka muchiloto kuli Jozefu mu Ijiputi akwamba kuti,
“Buka akubweza mwana a banyina akuya kunyika ya Izilayeli, nkambo abo bakalikuvwima buumi bwamwana bakafwa.”
Jozefu wakabuka, wakabweza mwana a banyina, akuboola munyika ya Izilayeli.
Pesi nakamvwa kuti Achelawusi wakali kwendelezya atala a Judiya abusena bwawisi Helodi, wakayoowa kwiinka nkuko. Nakamana kumuchenjezya Leza muchiloto, wakazwa wayakuchisi chaba Gilili
alimwi wakinka wakukkala mudolopo pati litegwa Nazaleta. Echi chakazuzikizigwa chakaambidwe kwinda kubasinsimi, kuti uyoyitwa kutegwa mu Nazaleta.
Mumazubayo Joni mubbabbatizyi wakasika kakambawuka munkanda yaku Judiya kawamba kuti,
“Amusanduke, nkambo Bwami bwakujulu bwaba afwifwi.”
Nkambo oyu ngonguwe iwakambwa amusinsimi Isaya kuti, “Ijwi lyayooyo uwompoolola mulusaka munkanda, Ámululamike inzila ya Mwami, muchite kuti nzila zyakwe zilulame.”
Lino Joni wakalikusama boya bwa nkamela abbanti lyachikumba muchibuno chakwe. Kulya kwakwe zyakali nsozi abuchi bwamulusaka.
Mpawo Jelusalema, Judiya yonse, azilikiti zyoonse zizyungulukide mulonga wa Jolodani zyakayinka kulinguwe.
Bakabbabbatizigwa anguwe mumulonga wa Jolodani, kabalyamba izibi zyabo.
Pesi nakabona kuti ba Falisi bayingi abasimulawu kabeza kulinguwe kuti ababbabbatizye, wakabambila kuti, “Inywe nizyalani lyabachipile, ngwani wakamuchenjezya kuchija bukali buza.
Amuzyale michelo yelela kusanduka.
Mutayeyi kamwamba kuti akati kanu, 'Tula Abbulahamu wamataatesu. Nkambo ndamwambila kuti Leza ulakonzya kubusya bana ba Abbulahamu nikuba kuzwa kumabwe.
Kabikwa kale kaleba kumiyanda yaminsamu itazyali michelo mibotu ulagonkwa akuwalilwa mumulilo.
Ndamubbabbatizya amanzi kuti musanduke. Pesi oyo uuza musule lyangu ulenguzu kwiinda ndime, alimwi tandelede nikuba kunyampula manyatela akwe. Uyomubbabbatizya a Muuya Uusalala amulilo.
Ipanga lyakwe lilimumanza akwe kuti akukule lubuwa lwakwe akubungania witi mungánda yachiyobwedo. Pesi uyowumpa buungu amulilo kuti obo butakonzeki kubikwa anze.”
Mpawo Jesu wakasika kuzwa ku Galili akuya kumulonga wa Jolodani kuti akabbabbatizigwe a Joni.
Pesi Joni wakasyezye kumukasya, kaamba kuti, “Ndiyanda kubbabbatizigwa anduwe, ani wasika kulindime biyeni?”
Jesu wakamuvwiila wati, “chizuminine lino, nkambo kulelede kuti swebo tuzuzikizye bululamiboonse. Mpawo Joni wakamuzumizya.
Nakamana kubbabbatizigwa Jesu wakazwa mpawawo mumeenda, amulange, majulu akajulilwa nguwe. Wakabona Muuya wa Leza kuuseluka ansi mbuli inziba akukkala alinguwe.
Amulange, ijwi lyakazwa kuzwa kumajulu kalyamba kuti, “Oyu ngu Mwana wangu ngundiyandisya. Ndilabotelwa anguwe.
Mpawo Jesu wakazulwidwa a Muuya kuya munkanda kuti akasunkwe asimwaba.
Lino nakalyimya mazuba makumi aane amansiku ali makumi aane, wakaba enzala.
Sikusunka wakasika akwamba kuti kulinguwe, “kuti koli mwana wa Leza, layilila mabwe aya kuti abe chinkwa.”
Pesi Jesu wakasandula akwamba kuti kulinguwe, “Kulilembedwe kuti Muntu takoyopona achinkwa luzutu, pes ajwi lyoonse lizwa kumulomo wa Leza.”
Mpawo simwaba wakamutola kuchisi chisalala akumukkazika aatala ansonge yangánda ya Leza,
akwamba kuti kulinguwe, “Na koli mwana a Leza, liwalile aansi, nkambo kulilembedwe kuti uyolayilila bangelobakwe kuti bakubambe; alimwi, bayokubaka mumaanza abo, kuti utakalyumpuni abbwe.”
Jesu wakabambila kuti, “Alubo kulilembedwe kuti, utasunki Mwami Leza wako.”
Alubo simwaba wakamutola kukalundu kalamfu akumutondezya Bwami boonse bwanyika abulemu bwayo bonse.
Wakamwambila kuti, “zyonse zintu eezi ndiyokupa, kuti wandivundamina akundikomba.”
Mpawo Jesu wakamwambila kuti, zwaawa, siluuni! Nkambo kulilembedwe kuti, uyokomba Mwami Leza wako, akukutawukila nguwe luzutu.”
Mpawo simwaba wakayinka, Amubone bangelo bakaza akumukutawukila.
Lino Jesu nakamvwa kuti Joni wakaabwa wakazwa waya ku Galili.
Wakazwa mu Nazaleta akwinka kuyokkala muKkapenawuma, ilikumbali lyalwizi lwa Galili mumasena a Zebbuluni a Nafutali.
Eezi zyakachitika kuti kuzuzikizigwe zyakaambwa amusinsiimi Isaya kuti,
“Chisi cha Zebbuluni achisi cha Nafutali kaziya kulwizi, luli kunembo lya Jolodani, Galili wabamasi!
Bantu bakalikkede mumudima babona mumuuni mupati, akulibaabo bakalikkede muchilikiti amumwenzule walufu, alimbabo kwanyamuka mumuuni.”
Kuzwa kulecho chindi Jesu wakatalika kukambawuka akuti, “Amusanduke, nkambo Bwami bwakujulu bwasika afwifwi.”
Nakali kwenda ambali lyalwizi lwaGalili, wakabona bana bakwabo babili, Sayimoni utegwa Pita, a Endulo mukulana wakwe, bakali kuwala tuzamba mulwizi, nkambo bakali bazubi babaswi.
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “amuze, munditobele, alimwi ndiyomuchita kuba bazubi babantu.”
Mpawawo bakasiya tuzamba bamutobela.
Jesu nakali kuyabwenda kuzwa mpawawo wakabona bambi bana bakwabo babili, Jemusi mwana a Zebbedi, a Joni mukulanakwe. Bakali mubwato awisi Zebbedi kabali kusuma tuzamba twabo. Wakabayita,
Alimwi mpawawo bakasiya bwato awisi akumutobela.
Jesu wakiinka mu Galili yoonse, kayobuyiisya muzikombelo, kakambawuka makani mabotu a Bwami akusilika misyobo yamalwazi amachise akali mubantu.
Impuwo atala anguwe yakamwayika mu Siliya yoonse, alimwi bantu bakeeta boonse bakali kuchiswa misyobo-misyobo yamalwazi amachise, abaabo bakanjidwemyuuya mibi, basimasuntu, abayuminide mibili, Jesu wakabasilika.
Makamu makamu abantu akamutobela kuzwa kuGalili, Ba Dekkapolisi, Jelusalemu, aku Judiya, akuzwa kunembo lya Jolodani.
Jesu naakabona makamu makamu aabantu wakatanta aatala aachilundu. Akkale biyo, baskwiiya bakwe bakaswena kulinguwe,
eelyo wakabbanuna mulomo wakwe, wakabayiisya kuti,
“Bali achoolwe bachete mumuuya, nkaambo bwami bwakujulu mbubwabo.
Bali achoolwe aabo balila, nkaambo bazowuuzigwa.
Bali achoolwe aabo balibombya, nkaambo bazoovuba nyika.
Bali achoolwe aabo bafwa nzala yabululami anyota yambubo, nkaambo bazookkuta.
Bali achoolwe beetelezi, nkaambo mbobonya bazooyetelelwa.
Bali achoolwe aabo basalala mumoyo, nkaambo bazoobona Leza.
Bali achoolwe basikutontozya, nkaambo bazootegwa bana ba Leza.
Bali achoolwe aabo bapenzegwa nkaambo kubululami, nkaambo bwami bwakujulu mbubwabo.
Inywe muli achoolwe nibazoomutukila akumupenzya akumutamikizya zintu zibi zyoonse zyakubeja nkaambo kandime.
Amukombe akusekelela, nkaambo bulumbu bwanu bwakujulu mbupati, nkaambo mbubonya oobo mbubakapenzya basinsimibakali kunembo lyanu.
Ndinywe munyo wanyika, pesi munyo kuti, wasampuka ulungwe buti tuuchikwe mulimo pesi kuswewegwa buyo akulyatawilwa abantu.
Ndinywe mumuni wanyika. Muunzi uyakidwe aatala achilundu tukonzyi kusisigwa.
Alimwi bantu nibamunikalampi tabalibiki munsi lyalusuwo, pesi balalibika aachibikilo kuti limunikile boonse bali mung'anda.
Mbubonya oobo mumuni wanu umunike kunembo lyabantu kuti babone milimo yanu mibotu, balemeke wuso wanu ulikujulu.
Mutayeeyi kuti ndeza kuzoojaya mulawu nibaba basinsimi. Teensi kiujaya nkuzidide pe, ndizide kukulondola.
Nkaambo ndamwaambila chakusinizya kuti julu anyika zyoonse zilakonzya kumana, pesi tachikonzeki kuti kamane kabala nikaba komwe nikaba kazila komwe kamumulawu mane lumwi zintu zyoonse zikachitwe.
kaako umwi awumwi usotoka nikaba kanini akati kamilazyo eeyi, alimwi ulayiisya bantu mbubonya oobo, ooyo uzotegwa muniini mubwami bwakujulu, pesi umwi awumwi uyiilomya, alimwi ulayiisya ooyo uzootegwa mupati mubwami bwakujul.
Nkaambo, ndamwaambila kuti, bululami bwanu kabutayindi bululami bwabalembi abwaba Falisi, tamukanjili mubwami bwakujulu.
bantu bakalekale mbubakaambilwa kuti, utajayi, umwi amwumwi uujaya uleede kubetekwa.
Pesi mebo ndamwaambila kuti, umwi awumwi uukalalila munyina uleede uleelde kubetekwa. Alimwi umwi awumwi uusampawula munyina uleelede lubeta lupati, pesi umwi awumwi utukila uleelede mulilo wa Gehena.
kaako kuti kuli mukutuula chipo chako nkukonya ooko kunembo lyachipayiliilo, uye ukasangune kuyanzaana amunyoko,
kosiya chipo chako kunembo lyachipayililo, akwiinka kunzila yako. Lutaanzi koyanzaana amunyoko, mpawo usike akuzootuula chipo chako.
Fwambaana kuzuminana asinkondo nyokwe nochili aawe munzila, kuti sinkondo nyokwe atakutoli kumubetesi, alkwe mubetesi atakutoli kumupolis, alakwe mupolisa atakubiki muntolongo.
Kasimpe ndamwaambila kuti tokoozwa oomo mane ukaliye nikaba kasyaalizi
Mwakamvwa mbukwaambwa kuti, 'utachiti bumambi.'
Pesi mebo ndamwaambila kuti, umwi awumwi weemuuzya mwanakazi wamuchitya kale bumambi mumoyo wakwe.
Na liso lyako lyalulyo lyakulebya, uligwisye ulisowe nkaambo kulakubotela kuti ufwidwe chipanzi chomwe kwiinda kusowelwa mu Gehena mubili wako woonse.
Alimwi kuti jaanza lyako lyalulyo lyakulebya, ulikosole ulisowe, nkaambo kulakubotela kuti ufwidwe chipanzi chomwe kwiinda kusowelwa mu Gehena mubili wako woonse.
Alimwi kwakaambwa kuti, umwi awumwi uuleka mukakwe amupe lugwalo lwakulekana.
Pesi mebo ndamwaambila kuti, umwi awumwi ulekede mukakwe kutaamba kuti nkaambo kakuvuulakuluumbi, wamuchitya bumambi alimwi umwi awumwi ooyo mwanakazi uleledwe wamuchitya bumambi.
Mwakamvwa bantu bakalekale mbubakaambilwa kuti, utakombi chakubeja uchitile Jehova mbubonya oobo mbuwakakonkezya.
Mebo ndamwaambila kuti, utakonki pe nikuba bunini, nikuba kujulu nkaambo nchichuuno chabwami bwa Leza.
Nikuba kunyika nkaambo nchichuuno chamawulu aakwe, nikuba ku Jelusalemu, nkaambo ngumuunzi wamwami mupati.
Alimwi utakonki kumutwe wako, nkaambo tokonzyi kusandula kasusu nikaba komwe kati katube na kasiye.
Kwaamba kwanu akube, Ii ii, na pe, nkaambo nzyoonse ziyungizigwa zilazwa kumubi.
Mwakamvwa mbukwakaambwa kuti, liso kuliso lino kulino,
mebo ndamwaambila kuti utamutontekki muntu mubi pesi muntu umwi awumwi ukuuma seya lyalulyo
Alimwi uuli buti uyanda kukubika kaambo akunyanzya chikobela chako, mulekele achalo chibaki chako.
Alimwi ukusungilizya kuyumuna musinzo omwe, musindikile musinzo yobile.
Umwi awumwi ukumbila kwako umupe, mpawo umwi awumwi kukolota kwako utamufutatili pe.
Mwakamvwa mbukakaambwa kuti yanda mweenzinyokwe, pesi sinkondo nyokwe umusule.
Mebo ndamwaambila kuti amuyande basinkonyokwe mubakombele bamupenzya,
kuti mube bana bakwe uso wanu uli kujulu nkaambo ulapusuzya zuba lyakwe kubabi akubabotu, ulawisizya mvulakuli boonse baluleme abataluleme.
Kuti kamuyanda aabo bamuyanda ino mbulumbuunzi mbumujisi? sa abalo basimutelo tabachiti mbubonya oobo?
Na mwazuminina bakwanu, muchita buti ziinda kulibamwi? Sena abalabo bamasi tabachiti mbubonya?
Nkaambo kaako amulondoke mbuli uso wanu uli kujuliu mbwalondokede
Amuchenjele kuti mutachiti milimo yanu iluleme kumeso abantu kuti mwebelwe ambabo. Mwachita obo, tamukwe bulumbu kuli Uuso wanu uulikujulu.
Nkambo kaako chindi nchowabila bantu izipo utasibi imwembo kubusyu bwabo mbuli mbubachita basikuupawupa ameso muzikombelo amumigwagwa, kuti batembawulwe kubantu. Nchobeni ndamwambila kuti balijene kale bulumbu bwabo.
Pesi webo, ichindi nchowabila bantu zipo ijanza lyako lyakululyo litazibi mbulichita lyakuchimwensi.
Kuti zipo zyako zibe kumbali, lino Uuso ubonena kumbali uzokulumbula.
Alimwi chindi nchomukomba mutabi mbuli basikupawupa amenso nkambo balayanda kukomba bwimvwi muzikombelo amuzyooko zyamigwagwa mipati kuti babonwe kubantu. Nchobeni ndamwambila kuti balijene kale bulumbu bwabo.
Iwebo chindi nchokomba njila muchimpetu chako ulijalile kumulyango ukkombe kuli Uuso uubonena kumbali uzokulumbula.
Alimwi mukukomba kwenu mutayindululi mbuli mbubachita bamaasi, nkambo balayeya kuti balaswililwa kukubwanta kwabo.
Nkinkaako, mutakozyani abo nkambo Uuso wanu ulikujulu ulizi zintu zyonse nzimubula kamutana kumubuzya
mbuboobu mbumwelede kukomba: 'Taata wesu ooli kujulu, alilemekwe izina lyako, abuze bwami bwako.
Aluchitwe luyando lwako, ansi aano mbubonya mbuli kujulu.
Utupe sunu zilyo zitwelede.
Utulekelele milandu yesu, mbubonya mbuli mbutu balakelela aswe bali amilandu kuli ndiswe.
Utatwenzyi mukutempawulwa. Utuvune kumubi, nkambo bwami mbubwako anguzu, abulemu, mane kukabe kutamani. Ameni.
Nkambo mwalekelela bantu milandu yabo alakwe Uusowanu ulikujulu ulamulekelela anywebo.
Pele mwatabalekelela bantu milandu yabo anywebo tamukoyolekelelwa.
Alimwi chindi nchomulyiimya kulya mutabi mbuli basikuwupawupa amenso, nkambo balo balawungumana, balabisya masyu aabo, kuti baboneke kubantu mbubalyimya kulya. Nchobeni ndamwambila kuti balijene kale bulumbu bwabo.
Pele chiindi ncholyimya kulya webo, ubotye mutwe wako akusamba kumenso aako.
Kuti kulyiimya kwako kutaboneki kubantu pele kuli Uuso uuli kumbali lino Uuso uubonena kumbali uzokulumbula.
Mutaliyobwedi lubono aansi ano mpaabisya mapempe ankalaya ababbi mpobatulula kuti babbe.
Amuliyobwede lubono lwakujulu nkwatabisyi mapempe ankalaya, ababbi nkubatatululi kuti babbe.
Nkambo lubono lwako nkulubede nkukonya oko nkubede moyo wako.
Ilampi lyamubili ndinso nkambo kaako linso lyako kuti kalili sibuuya mubili wako woonse ulazula mumuni.
Anukuti linso lyako kalili abutavu mubili wako woonse lino mumuni mulinduwe wakali mudima. Mudima wayo ulasiya mbi.
Takwe muntu ukonzya kumanina baami bobile milimo nkambo ulasula umwi ulayanda umwi na ulakakilila umwi akusampawula umwi. Tamukonzyi kubelekela Leza antomwe alubono.
Nkambo kaako ndamwambila kuti, mutalibilikili kubuumi bwanu kuti tukalyeenzi? Nikuba kumibili yenu kuti, tukasamenzi? Buumi bwenu tabwiindi zilyo awalo mubili sa tuyindi zyakusama?
Amulange bayuni bakujulu nkambo tababyali tabatebuli, tabayoboli mumatala, nekuba boobo Uusowanu ulikujulu ulabasanina. Sa inywe tamuyandiki kwinda mbabo?
Ngwani akati kenu ulibilika ukonzya kukomezya chiimo chakwe nikuba kakokola komwe?
Alimwi nkamboonzi mulalibilikila zyakusama? Amuyeye masamu amusokwe mbwamena, tabeleki, takonzyi kuluka,
pele ndamwambila kuti naba Solomoni mubulemu bwakwe boonse takakonzya kusama mbuli limwi akati kanzizyo.
Lino kuti Leza kasamika boobo maani amusokwe, aaliko sunu pele ijunza alasowelwa muchikko, sa takayindi loko kumusamika anywebo nobasilusyomo lunini.
Nkambo kaako mutalibiliki akaamba kuti tukalyeenzi? Tukanyweenzi? Tukasamenzi?'
Nkambo kazeezi zyoonseni nzibayandula bamaasi, alimwi Uusowanu ulikujulu ulizi kuti eezi zyonse zilayandwa kulindinywe.
Pele amusangune kuyandula bwami bwa Leza abululami bwakwe eelyo zintu ezi zyoonse mulaziyungizizigwa azyalo.
Nkambo kaako mutalibilikili zyejunza, nkambo bwejunza bula lilibilikila bwini. Buzuba bwasunu bulizulide mapenzi abo bwalo.
Mutabeteki, nkambo muzobetekwa.
Alubeta ndomutakabeteke alo muyobetekwa aandulo, achelesyo nchimuyoyelesya, muyokuyelesezegwa anchicho.
Nkambonzi nulanga katanda kali mulinso lyamukulana wako, pele wasiya itanda lili mulinso lyako?
Chilakonzeka na kuti utedi kumukulana, leka ndikugusye katanda kali mulinso lyako; kakuli tanda mulinso lyako?
Inywe nobasikuupaupa! Tanguna kugusya itanda lilimulinso lyako, alubo ulakonzya kubona kabotu katanda kalimulinso lyamukulana wako.
Mutapi zisalala kubankala, alubo mutasoweli zibi kumpela angulube. Ulabona zyalyatuulwa aansi amawulu, alubo zilasanduka akumudabula mutu fwapufwapu.
Amukumbile, alubo muyopegwa. Amuyandawule, mulajana. Amukonkomone mulajulilwa.
Nkambo umwi awumwi ukumbila ulatambula, alakwe uyanduula ulajana alakwe uukonkomona ulajulilwa.
Nguli muntu akati kenu uupa mwanaakwe ibbwe, amukumbila insima?
Alimwi, kuti wakumbila imuswi, sa ulamupa inzoka?
Lino mbuli bmumuzi kupa bana benu zintu zibotu, inywe nobabi, alakwe Wuso wenu ulikujulu sa tazoyindi loko kupa zintu zibotu kulibaabo bamukumbila?
Nkaambo kaako zintu zyoonse zili buti nzimuyanda kuti bantu bamuchitile, anywebo amubachitile nzizyoonya, nkambo mbuboobo mbuwamba mulawo abasinsimi.
Amunjile mumulyango umanikide, nkambo mulyango ukwazamukide anzila impati njiitola kukunyoonyoka, nkabela abo banjila mulinjiyo mbanji banji.
Pesi mulyango umanikide anzila ipatide njiitola kubuumi, nkabela abo banjila mbache.
Amuchenjelele basinsimi babeji beeza kulindinywe basamide zyakusama zyambelele, anukuti mukati lyabo mbawumpe babutambo.
Michelo yabo njiiti muzibye mbubabede. Sa kulachelwa masansa kumuunga niziba inkuyu kumutubatuba?
Mbubonya obo musamu umwi awumwi mubotu ulazyala michelo mibotu, alimwi musamu usampawukide ulazyala michelo mibi.
Musamu mubotu tukonzyi kuzyala michelo mibi, alimwi musamu usampawukide tukonzyi kuzyala michelo mibotu,
Musamu umwi awumwi utazyali michelo mibotu ulatemwa akusowelwa mumulilo.
Aboobo michelo yabo njita muzibye mbubabede.
Boonse bandambila kuti, Mwami, Mwami, teensi mbabo bayonjila mubwami bwakujulu, ngooyo uuchita luyando lwa-Taata uli kujulu.
Kubuzuba obo banji banji bayondambila njako alimwi sa teensi kuzina lyako nkutwakatanda madayimona Sa teensi kuzina lyako nkotwakachita milimo mipati myiingi?'
Lino nzobaambila kuti, nsimuzi pe, amuzwe kulindime inywe nubamuchita zibi!'
Nkambo kaako umwi awumwi uuswilila majwi aangu aya akwachita uzokozyanisigwa amuntu uchenjede iwakayaka ing'anda yakwe atala amwaala.
Lino imvula yakawa nyingi, milonga yakeeta, amyuuwo yakawunga, yakawuma ang'anda eyo, nekuba boobo teyakawa pe, nkambo yakatalikilidwe aamwala.
Pele umwi awumwi uuswilila majwi aangu aya akutachita uzokozyanisigwa amuntu mufuba fuba iwakayaka ing'anda yakwe amusele,
lino niyakawa imvula milonga yakeeta, myuuwo yakawunga, yakawuma ang'anda eyo, elyo yakawa, nkabela buwe bwayo bwakakomena.
Lino Jesu nakamana kwamba majwi aya oonse, makamu makamu abantu aka kankabala kukuyiisya kwakwe,
nkambo wakali kubayiisya chabwami kutakozyenie abalembi babo pe.
Chiindi Jesu nakaseluka kuzwa muchilundu makamu mingi akamutobela.
Eelyo, sichinsenda wakasika kulinguwe alimw wakamufugamina, wakati, “Mwami na kuzumina ulakonzya kundisalazya.
Jesu wakatambika kuboko kwakwe alimwi wakamwampa, wakati, “Ndilazumina. Salala.” Mpawawo wakasalazigwa kuchipele.
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Utakambili muntu naba umwi” Ulitondezye kumupayizi, alimwi ukape chipo kuli Mozesi nchakakulayilila, kuti bukabe bukamboni kulimbabo.”
Awo Jesu nakanjila mu Kapenawuma, silutwe wempi wakaza kulinguwe, wakamulombela.
alimwi wakati, “Mwami, mubelesi wangu ulilede kungánda, uliyuminide akumvwa machise mapati.”
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Ndilasika alimwi ndizomuponye.”
Silutwe wankamu wakasandula alimwi wakati, “Mwami, tandeelede kuti unjile mungánda yangu pesi amba ijwi alimwi mubelesi ulapona.
Ngambulindime lubo ndili muntu usalidwe mubwendelezi, alimwi ndilabasilumamba balimunsi lyangu. Ngandati kuloyu, 'Koya' alimwi ulenda, alimwi akulumwi, ngandati, 'Sika' alimwi ngawaza, akulumbi mubelesi, ngandati, 'chita echi; alimwi ulachichita.”
Chindi Jesu nakamvwa ezi, wakagamba alimwi wakati kuli abo bakali kumutobela, “Nchobeni ndamwambila kuti takwe pe ngundakali ndajana ulalusyomo luli obu mu Izilayeli.
Ndamwambila, bingi bayozwa kumbo alimwi akujwe, alimwi bayolya atebuli a Abbulahamu, Ayizeki, a Jakobo, mubwami bwakujulu.
Pesi baana babaami bayotandilwa anze mumudima, chindi nikunoli kulila akuluma ntwino.”
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Enda! mbuli mbuwasyoma, aboobo achichitwe kulinduwe.” Alimwi mubelesi wakapona mu hola ndilelyo.
Chindi Jesu nakasika mungánda ya Pita, wakabona banyinazyala a Pita kabachisidwe ntuntumanzi.
Jesu wakajata kuboko kwabo, mpawo ntuntumanzi yakamana mpawo bakabuka alimwi bakatalika kumukutawukila.
Elyo nikwakaba mangolezya bantu bakamwetela Jesu bakanjidwe amadimoni. Wakitanda myuuya mibi ajwi alimwi wakaponisya boonse bakali kuchiswa.
Munzila eyi zyakazuzikizigwa ezyo zyakambidwe amusinsimi Isaya, wakati, “Nguwelwakwe ubweza machise esu akunyampula malwazi esu oonse.”
Lino Jesu nakabona makamu kamuzyungulukide, wakabalayilila kuti bazubukile mutala eliya lyalwizi lwa Galilaya.
Mpoonyawo mulembi wakasika kulinguwe alimwi wakati, “Mwiiyi, Ndiyokutobela kufumbwa nkoya.”
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Bamwaba balijisi mapako, alimwi tuyuni twakujulu tulazizumbo, pesi Mwana a Muntu takwe ampalazika mutwe wakwe.”
Umwi wabasikwiiya wakati kulinguwe, “Mwami, ndizumizye saansi kuti njiinke alimwi ndikavwikke ndeende.”
Pesi Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Nditobele alimwi usiye bafwide bazikkane lwabo.”
Lino Jesu nakanjila mubwato, basikwiya bakwe bakamutobela alimwi.
Elyo kwakaba iguwo ipati mulwizi, lumwi bwato bwavumbwa amayuwe. Pesi Jesu wakali winkilila koona.
Basikwiya bakaza kulinguwe alimwi bakamubusya, bakati, “Tugwasye, Mwami; twamba kumana kufwa!”
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Nkamboonzi nomuyowa, inywe nobalusyomo lunini? Mpawo wakabuka alimwi wakawumuzya iguwo alimwi alwizi. Mpoonya kwakaba kumuuna kupati.
Bantu bakagamba alimwi bakati, “musyobonzi wamuntu ulibobu, kuti nikuba iguwo alimwi alwizi zilamulemeka?”
Lino Jesu nakasika kulubazu lumbi alimwi kubantu bakkala kuchisi chitegwa Gadala bantu babili bakanjidwe madimoni bakaswanana anguwe. Bakali kuzwa kuzibunda alimwi bakali abukali alubo tebakali kuyanda muntu winda munzila eyo.
Elyo, bakoompolola bakati, “uyandaanzi kulindiswe Mwana wa Leza? Wasika okuno kuti uzotufwabye nkachitanasika chiindi chibambidwe.
Lino sikwembela wabutanga bwangulube wakaliwo kalikucheezya, katali kule loko ambabo.
Madimoni akaliswini kukombelezya Jesu alimwi kati, 'Na watutanda, tutumine kubutanga bwangulube.”
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Kamuya! Madimoni akazwa akiya mungulube, alimwi zyoonse ngulube zyakafwambana kukunkulikila mujenga zyanjila akufwida mumanzi.
Abo bakali kwembela butanga bwengulube bakachija alimwi bakaya mudolopo alimwi bakamba zyoonse, kapati loko azyakachitika kumuntu wakanjidwe dimoni.
Mpawo, Lyoonse dolopo lyakasika kuti baswanane a Jesu. Nibakamubona bakamukombelezya kuti azwe muchisi chabo.
Jesu nakanjila mubwaato, wakazubuka, alimwi wakasika kudolopo lyakulimbaabo.
Amubone, bata kulinguwe muntu ulebukide kaleede aabulo. Nakabona lusyomo lwabo, Jesu wakati kumuntu ulebukide, “Mwana mulombe, sungwazigwa zibi zyako zyalekelelwa.”
Amubone, bamwi balembi bakati kulilwabo beni,” “Imuntu oyu ulatukila.”
Nkabela Jesu wakaziba miyeeyo yabo, elyo wakati, “Nkambonzi nimuyeeya buubi mumyoyo yenu?
Nkambo nchichili chuuba kwamba kuti, Ízibi zyanu zyalakelelwa, na kwamba kuti, Nyampuka alimwi uyende'? Pesi mulelede kuziba kuti Mwana a Muntu ulanguzu ansi zyakulekelela izibi,...”Nyampuka, bweeza bulo bwako,
alimwi uyinke kungánda yako” Mpawo mwalumi wakanyampuka alimwi wakeenda kungánda yakwe.”
Mpawo mwalumi wakanyampuka alimwi wakeenda kungánda yakwe.
Chiindi makamu makamu nakabona eechi, bakayoowa alimwi bakatalika kulumbayizya Leza, wakapede inguzu ziliboobu kubantu.
Mbubonya Jesu nakayinda kuzwa awo, wakabona mwalumi utegwa Mateyo kakkede aziyako zyabasimutelo wasikuti kulinguwe, “Nditobela.” Wakanyampuka alimwi wakamutobela.
Mbubonya Jesu wakakkala ansi kuti alye mungánda, amubone, basimutelo biingi abasizibi bakasika alimwi bakasusula a Jesu abasikwiiya bakwe.
Lino baFalisi nibakachibona echi bakati kuli basikwiya bakwe, “Nkambonzi muyisi wenu ulalya abasimutelo alimwi abasizibi?”
Eelyo Jesu nakamvwa echi, wakati, bantu basimide mubili tabayandi musilisi, pesi abo bachisidwe.
Mulelede kwinka akuyoyiiya kuti ezi zyambayi. Ndilombozya luzyalo alimwi zitali zipayizyo.' Mbulikuti ndakasika, kuti nditazoyiti balulami kuti musanduke, pesi basizibi.”
Eelyo basikwiya ba John bakasika kulinguwe alimwi bakati, “Nkambonzi iswe antomwe abaFalisi nitulyiimya, pesi basikwiya bako tabalyiimyi pe?”
Jesu wakati kuli mbabo, “Ani bana basimusa balakonzya na kulila nibachili asibwinga? Pesi mazuba ayosika elyo sibwinga nayobwezegwa kuzwa kuli mbabo, alimwi bayolyimya.
Takwe muntu ubika chisamo chipya atala a jansi kkulukulu, nkambo chigamba chiladeluka kuzwa kujansi, alimwi ibbanga elyo lilayindilila kukomena.
Nekuba kuti bantu babika wayini mupya muzibikilo zikulukulu zyewayini. Na bachita boobo zibikilo zilakwamuka. Wayini ulatika alimwi zibikilo zyawayini zilanyonyonwa. Anukuti, babika wayini mupya muchibikilo chipya cha wayini, alimwi zyoonse zilalondokeka.”
Alimwi Jesu nakali kwamba eezi kulimbabo, amubone, mwendelezi wakasika alimwi wakkkotama aansi kulinguwe wakati, “Mwana wangu musimbi wafwa lino, pesi sika alimwi uzobike ijanza lyako alinguwe, alimwi uyopona.”
Mpawo Jesu wakabuka akumutobela, alimwi mbubakachita basikwiiya bakwe.
Amubone, mwanakazi wakali kufwabisigwa akalobola kwaminyaka ili kkumi ayibili wakeza musule lya Jesu alimwi wakajata moombe wejansi lyakwe.
Nkambo wakali walyambila lwakwe mwini, “kuti na nkajate chisamo, ndiyopona.”
Pesi Jesu wakachebuka mpawo wakamubona, alimwi wakati, “Musimbi, koba mukozu, lusyomo lwako lwakuponya. Mpawo mwanakazi wakapona muchindi ncicheecho.
Chiindi Jesu nakeza kungánda yamwendelezi, wakabona bakali kusobana mutetele alimwi makamu makamu akali kuyowela.
Wakati, “Muzwe awa, nkambo musimbi tafwide pe, pesi ulilede. “Pesi bakamuseka chakumuniaka.
Kuchindi makamu nakazwa anze, wakanjila mungánda alimwi wakamubweza akuboko, alimwi musimbi wakanyampuka.
Makani atala azezi akazulila munyika yoonse.
Mbubonya Jesu nakayinda kuzwa oko, bantu babili boofu bakamutobela. Bakali koompolola alimwi kabati, “Tufwide luzyalo Mwana wa Devidi.
Chiindi Jesu nakeza mungánda. bantu boofu bakasika kulinguwe. Jesu wakati kuli mbabo, mulasyoma na kuti nga ndilachichita eechi? Bakati kuli nguwe, “Iyii, Mwami.”
Mpawo Jesu wakajata menso abo akwamba kuti, “achichitike kulindinywe mbuli lusyomo lwenu,”
alimwi meso abo akajulika. Mpawo Jesu wakabalayilila akwamba kuti, “mubone kuti takwe uumbi utakazibe atala azezi.”
Pesi bantu babili bakeenda biinka alimwi makani akakuzulila munyika yoonse.
Mbubnya bantu abo babili nibakayobwenda, muntu uutambuli kazwide muuya wadimoni wakeetwa kuli Jesu.
Dimoni nilyakagwisigwa, muntu utaambuli wakaambula. Makamu makamu akagamba, akaamba kuti, “eezi tazinakuboneka mu Izilayeli!”
Pesi ba Falisi bakali kuti, “Mubwendelezi bulama dimoni, ulagwisya dimoni.”
Jesu wakenda kumadolopo woonse akumagunzi wakendelela anembo kayobuyiisya muzikombelo zyabo kakambawuka makani mabotu abwami, akuyobuponia zilwazi zyonse zyamisyobo misyobo amachise woonse amisyobo misyobo.
Lino nakabona makamu makamu, wakaba aluzyalo kuli mbabo, nkambo bakali kupeekezezegwa akunyansigwa. Bakali mbuli mbelele zitakwe mweembeli.
Wakati kuli basikwiiya bakwe, “Butebuzi bwavula, pesi batebuzi mbache.
Nkabela amukombe chakufwambana ku Mwami wabutebuzi, kuchitila kuti atuume batebuzi mubutebuzi bwakwe.
Jesu wakayita basikwiiya bakwe boonse ibali kkumi ababili alimwi wabapa inguzu aatala amyuuya mibi, kuti bayitande. Akuponia zilwazi zyamisyobo isiyene amachise amisyobo isiyene.
Lino mazina abatumwa balikkumi ababili ngaya. Wakusanguna, Sayimoni (oyo ngwakiita kuti Pita), a Endulo mukulana; Jemusi mwana wa Zebbedi, a Joni mukulana wakwe;
Filipu, a Bbatolomyu; Tomasi, a Mateyo simutelo; Jemusi mwana wa Alufiyasi, a Tediyasi;
Sayimoni mu Ziloti, a Judasi Sikaliyoti, oyo wakali sikuyomwaba.
Aaba bali kkumi ababili Jesu mbakatuma wakabalayilila akwamba kuti, “Mutakayinki kunyoika kukkala bamaasi alimwi mutakanjili kufumbwa dolopo lyaba Samaliya.
Kamuya kumbelele ziswekede zyang'anda ya Izilayeli.
Alimwi nimuyoyinka, mukakambawuke akwamba kuti, “Bwami bwakujulu bwaba afwifwi.
Mukaponie bachiswa, mukabusye bafwide, musanzye basizinsenda, akuyotanda madimoni. Mwatambula kakutakwe muliyo, anywebo amukape katakwe muliyo.
Mutakabwezi ingolida, nsiliva, nikuba kkopa muzibbeeke zyenu.
Mutakabwezi zibbeeke zyamulwendo mukwenda kwenu, nikuba zibaki zibili na insangu, na inkoli, nkambo simulimu uyolijanina chakulya.
Kufumbwa muunzi ngumuyonjila, mukalange kuti ngwani uyelede, kuti mukkale alinguwe manedo mukeende.
Mbubonya mwakunjila mung'anda, mukiijuzye.
Kuti ing'anda kiyelela, akube kuti luumuno lwenu lukabe mulinjiyo. Pele na kitelede lumuno, luumuno lwenu ngalubwede kulindinywe.
Kuli abo batakabule kumutambula nikuba kumutelela kumajwi enu, nimutakazwe mung'anda na mudolopo, mukakunkumune lusuko kumawulu enu.
Nchooncyo ndamwambila kuti, kuyoba kulansya moyo kunyika ye Sodomu a Gomola mubuzuba bwalubeta kwinda kwamudolopo elyo.
Amulange, Ndamutuma mbuli imbelele akati kabawumpe, nkenkaako amuchenjele mbuli inzoka alimwi mube basalali mbuli inziba.
Amukabalangisisye bantu! bayomutola kumbeta alimwi bayomutanda muzikombelo zyabo.
Mpoonya bayomweta kunembo lyabendelezi akubaami nkambo kangu, bukabe bukamboni kuli mbabo akuli bamaasi.
Kuchindi nibayomujata akumwaba, mutakalikatazyi kuti mbobuli nakuti tuyowambula katutyeni, nkambo izyakuyowamba muyozipegwa nywebo muchiindi echo.
Nkambo teensi ndinywe nimuyowambula, pesi kuti Muuya wa Wuso ngutakaambule mulindinywe.
Mukwesu uyowaba munyina kulufu, alimwi wisi uyowaba mwana. Bana bayobukila bazyali baabo alimwi akuchita kuti bajayigwe.
Muyosuligwa abantu boonse akambo kezina lyangu. Pesi oyo ukakatila kuyosika kumamanino, imuntu oyo uyofutulwa.
Chindi nibayomupenzya mudolopo elyo, mukachijile kuli liimbi, nkambo zyamasimpe ndamwambila, tamukoyo yenda mukati kamadolopo a Izilayeli Mwana a Muntu katanakusika.
Sikwiiya temupati kwiinda muyiisyi wakwe, nikuba mulanda talimupati kwiinda simalelo wakwe.
Zilelede mbuli sikwiiya kuti aabe mbuli muyiisyi, alimwi mulanda mbuli simalelo wakwe. Na bayita mulanda wang'anda ya Bbeluzebbulu, zilaba kazyindilila byeni mbuli mazina ngibayita bamwi babeleki bang'anda yakwe!
Nkinkakako mutakabayoowi, mbulikuti takwe chisisikene chitakaleke kuzwa entanganana alimwi takwe chisisikene chitakaleke kuyozibinkana.
Nzendikumubuzya mumudima, muzyambe mumumuuni, alimwi nzimumvwa kanonono mumatwi enu, mukaziluule aziluli zyamaanda.
Mutayoowi abo bajaya, mibili pesi kabakachilwa kujaya muuya. Anukuti mwelede kuyowa oyo ukonzya kujaya muuya a nyama mugehena.
Sena tuyuni tobile tatuulwi a kkobili? Takwe naba omwe wabo uuwa aansi katakwe luzibo lwa Wuso.
Pesi nikuba masusu mumutwe yenu woonse alibalidwe.
Mutayowi. Mulayandika kwinda tuyuni twiingi.
Nkinkakako kuliwoonse ulisola kulindime kunembo lyabantu, andime ndiyolisola kuli Taata ulikujulu.
Pesi oyo undikkaka kunembo lyabantu, Ambebo ndiyomukkaka kunembo lya Taata uli kujulu.
Mutayeeyi kuti ndakeza kuzoyeta lumuno ansi aano. Tindakazida kuzoyeta luumuno, pesi ikafulo.
Mbulikuti ndakazida kuzokazyanisya mwana awisi, alakwe mwana musimbi abanyina, alakwe mukamwana abanyinazyala.
Nkabela basinkondonyina bamwalumi mbimbabo beng'anda yakwe.
Oyo uyanda wisi na banyina kwinda ndimeteelede kulindime, oyo uyanda mwanakwe mulombe na musimbi kwinda ndime teelede kulindime.
Oyo utabwezi chiingano chakwe alimwi atobelele musule lyangu telede kulindime.
Oyo uyanda buumi bwakwe uyobuswekelwa. Pesi oyo uswekelwa buumi bwakwe akambo kangu uyobujana.
“Oyo ukutambula utambula ndime, alimwi oyo unditambula alimwi watambula ayoyo iwakandituma.
Oyo utambula musinsimi muzina lyamusinsiimi uyojana mpindu yamusinsiimi, alimwi oyo utambula bululami bwamuntu muzina lyabululami bwamuntu uyojana mpindu yabululami bwamuntu.
Kufumbwa uupa kulumwi wabaaba banini, nikaba kanywido kamaanzi atontola kuti banywe, nkambo ngusikwiiya, chamasimpe ndamwambila, takwepe nayobula impindu yakwe.”
Nichakaba kuti Jesu wamaninsya kulayilila basikwiya bakwe balikkumi ababili, wakazwa nkukonya oko wakuyisya akukambawuka mumadolopo aabo.
Lino Joni nakamvwa muntolongo atala anchito zya Kkilisito, wakatuma basikwiya bakwe
ajwi elyo bakati kulinguwe, “Nduwe na ulokuza, na kuti tuchilangilila uumbi?”
Jesu wakasandula akwamba kulimbabo, “Mwinke mukaambe kuli Joni nzimwabona akumvwa.
Bataboni balikutambula kubona, zilema zilenda, balezipele balokusalazigwa, batamvwi balokumvwa lubo, bafwide balokubusigwa lubo kubawumi, amakani mabotu alokukambawukwa kubachete.
Alubo ngusicholwe kufumbwa utabilizigwi andime.”
Lino aba bantu nibakeenda munzila yabo Jesu wakatalika kwamba kumakamu atala a Joni, “Mwakayinka kuya kunkanda kuyobonanzi - ityetye lizunganisigwa aguuwo?
Pesi mwakayinka kuya kuyobonanzi - muntu usamide ziteete? Mbukubede, abo basama zisamo ziteetete bakkala mumaanda abami.
Pesi mwakainka kunze kuyobonanzi - musinsimi? Iyi, ndati kulindinywe, akwinda musinsimi.
Echi nchenchicho nguchakali kulembeledwe obu. 'Bona, ndinokutuma mutumwa wangu kunembo lyabusyu bwako, uyokubambila nzila kunembo lyako.
“Ndamba kulindinye nkasimpe, takukwe nikwakabukide akati kabaabo bazyalwa abanakazi unga ulaba mupati kwinda Joni mubbabbatizyi. Nekubaboobo, munini muntu mukolondo kubwami bwakujulu mupati kwinda nguwe.
Kuzwa kumazuba a Joni mubbabbtizyi kusikila lino, bwami bwakujulubulokufwabisigwa alupyopyongano, lino bantu balupyopyongana balalubweza changuzu.
Mbukunga boonse basinsimi amulawu wakali kusinsima kusikila kuli Joni.
Elyo nawayanda kuzumina kuchitambula, oyu ngu Elija, nguwe wakali kuzosika.
Kuliyoyo ulamatwi akumvwa, ngamvwe.
Kuli chili nchindinga ndilayezyanisya azyalane lyasunu? Chili mbuli bana basobana kuchisambalilo, bakkala akwita umwi awumwi,
akwamba, 'twakakulizizya muteetele, aboobo tewakazyana pe. Twakayeema, pele tewakalila.
Aboobo Joni wakasika katalyi chinkwa nanka kunywa masansa, elyo bakati, Uladimoni.
Mwana amuntu wakasika akulya akunywa elyo bakati, Langa, mwalumi sindya amukolwi, muzolwani abasimutelo abasizibi!' Pesi busongo bulalulamikwa anchito zyakwe.”
Elyo Jesu wakatalika kukalalila madolopo omo mwakachita malele akwe manji, nkambo tebakeempwa.
“Maawe kulinduwe, Kkolazini! Mawe kulinduwe, Bbetisayida! Kansinga malele akachitwa ku Taya a Sidoni akachitwa kulindinywe, ninga bakeempwa kale kuchindi chakayinda muzisamo zyamasaka amudyota.
Pesi kulakuyandika chakwindilila kubuzuba bwalubeta kwinda nduwe.
Webo, Kapenawumu, uyeeya kuti uzosumpulwa kujulu? Peepe, unoyoyetwa ansi kumulindi utagoli [Hadesi]. Nikwali kuti mu Sodomu mwakachitwa malele akachitwa mulinduwe, ninga mwachili asunu.
Pele ndati kulinduwe chiyobachubila kunyika ya Sodomu mubuzuba bwalubeta kwinda nduwe.”
Kuchindi echo Jesu wakati, “Ndilikutembawula Taata, Mwami, wakujulu anyika, nkambo wasisila basongo abamvwisya, akuyubunwida bana banini:
Iyii, Taata, Eechi chakalikubotezya kumeso ako.
Zintu zyonse zyakapegwa ndime kuzwa kuli Taata. Elyo takwe umwi uzi mwana kunze kwa Taata, mpawo, takwe uzi Taata kunze kwamwana aboobo kuloyo mwana ngwasala kuti amuyubunune.
Amuze kulindime, moonse nimukatede animulemenwa ndiyomupa kulyokezya.
Amubweze ijokwe lyangu lili alindime akwiiya kulindime, nkambo ndilimubombe akuba mutete moyo, eelyo muyojana kulyokezya kwmyuuya yanu.
Nkambo ijokwe lyangu niteete alubo ndiguba amukuli wangu tulemi pe.”
Kuchindi echo Jesu wakayinka mubuzuba bwakulyokezya wayinda mumyunda yazilyo. Basikwiya bakwe bakafwa anzala eelyo bakasanguna kukulula mayila nkwalikumpela akwalya mituutu.
Pesi baFalisi nibakabona oobo bakati kuli Jesu, “Bona, basikwiya bako bachita zitali mumulawu kuchitwa mubuzuba bwakulyokezya.”
Pesi Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Takwe nimwakabalide Devidi mbakachita nakaba anzala, abaabo balumi mbakali aabo?
Wakanjila mungánda ya-Leza akulya chinkwa chakutwa, chitensi kumulawu kuti alye alubo chitali kumulawu akulabo mbakali abo, pesi kazili kumuawu kupela kubapayizi.
Tamubalide mulawu kuti mubuzuba bwakulyokezya bapayizi muchikombelo balataluka mulawu wabuzuba bwakulyokezya pesi tabakwe mulandu?
Pele ndati kulindinywe umwi mupati kwinda ngánda yaLeza ulaano.
Namwakalizi echi nchichalikwamba, 'mebo ndiyanda luse pepe chipayizyo; temwalikubapa kambo batakwe mulandu.
Eelyo mwana amuntu ngu Mwami wazuba lyakulyokezya.”
Mpawo Jesu wakazwa oko akwinka kuchikombelo.
Amubone, kwakali muntu wakalinyanide kuboko. Bafalisi bakabuzya Jesu, bakati, “sena chililuleme kusikila mubuzuba bwakulyokezya?” Ikuti bamutamikizye kubisya.
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Inga ulaba mwalumi biyeni akati kanu, ngwani, na wali ambelele imwi, aboobo, na imbelele eyi yawida mudindi mubuzuba bwakulyokezya, takonga ulijata na akwigusya aanze?
Chiinda bulemu biyeni, eelyo kumuntu nekuba kumbelele! Aboobo chililuleme kuchita chibotu mubuzuba bwakulyokezya.”
Mpawo Jesu wakati kumuntu, 'Tandabika kuboko kwako.” Wakatandabika, alubo lwakabwedezegwa mukupona, mbuli kwenzinyina kuboko.
Pesi ba Falisi bakayinka bakubamba mbubonya kabalikumuvwiya. Bakali kuyandula mbubanga balamujaya.
Mbuli mbwakaziba Jesu, wakazwa oko. Bantu banji bakamutobela, lino wakabasilika boonse.
Wakabalayilila kuti batachiti kuti azibinkane kulibamwi,
zikazuzikizigwe, zyakambwa muli Isaya musinsimi, kuti,
“Bona, mulanda wangu ngundakasala; Muyandwi wangu umwi, oyo muuya wangu ngundibotelwa. Ndiyobika muuya wangu alinguwe, eelyo uyobakambawukila bululami kulibamasi.
Takoyojana buyumuyumu na kukulililisya; nikuba umwi kumumvwa ijwi lyakwe mumigwagwa.
Takwe nayotyola limwi ityetye lyakapwayulwa; takwepe nayozima kamuni kasuka kamulilo, kusikila wendelezya bululami mukuzunda,
Abalabo bamasi bayoba bulangizi muzina lyakwe.”
Eelyo umwi muntu utakuboni katambuli, wakanjidwe adimoni, wakeetwa kuli Jesu. Wakamusilika, azezyo zyakazwa kuti utambuli muntu wambula akubona.
Makamu wonse akagamba akwamba, “ooyu muntu ngaulaba mwana wa Devidi na?”
Pesi baFalisi nibakamvwa malele aaya bakati, “Ooyu muntu tatandi madimoni kunze kwa Bbelezebbulu, mupati wamadimoni.”
Pele Jesu walizi miyeyo yabo mpawo wakati kulimbabo, “Bwami boonse bukazyania lwabo, buyomwayisigwa, alubo kufumbwa dolopo niba ng'anda ikazyania lwayo tikayimikili pe.
Ikuti satani watanda satani, unoli ulikulikazya lwakwe. Bwami bwakwe nga bulimikila byeni?
Lino na ndilatanda madimoni a Bbelizebbulu, ani batobezi banu batandyanzi? Nkambo kachechi, bayoba babetesi banu.
Pesi do katwatanda madimoni a muuya wa Leza, mpawo bwami bwa Leza bwasika akati alindinywe?
Alubo kulibiyeni kuti umwi anjile mung'anda yamuntu usimide akubba makwebo akwe katamusungide muntu usimide chakusanguna? Elyo uyobba makwebo akwe kuzwa mungánda yakwe.
Umwi utali andime ukazyanya andime, alubo ayoyo utabungani andime ulamwayula.
Aboobo ndati kulinduwe, chibi choonse akusampawuula bantu bayolekelelwa, pesi kutukila muuya takukwe kulekelelwa pe.
Kufumbwa uwambula ijwi atala amwana muntu, ooyo uyolekelelwa. Pesi kufumbwa uwambula bubi atala a Muuya Uusalala, oyo takoyolekelelwa, na munyika eyi, na kuleeyo ichizosika.
Chita musamu ubote ayala michelo yawo ibote, na kuchita musamu kuba mubi, amuchelo wayo ubije, mbuli kuti musamu uboneka amichelo yawo.
Nywebo nubana banzoka, mbomunga muli babi, ngamulamba buti izintu zibotu? Kuzwa mumoyo mulizinji mulomo nzuwambula.
Muntu mubotu kuzwa kuzintu zibotu zyamoyo wakwe ulagusya nzizyonya, pele muntu mubi wakuzintu zibi zyamoyo wakwe mulazwa bubi kupela.
Ndati kulinduwe mubuzuba bwalubeta bantu balakupa bupandanuzi kuli alimwi ijwi litali kabotu ndibakaamba.
Kuzwa kumajwi ako uyolulamikwa, akumajwi ako uyopegwa mulandu.”
Elyo balembi bamulawu bamwi, abaFalisi bakasandula akut, “Muyiisi tuyanda kubona chitondezyo kuzwa kulinduwe.”
Pesi Jesu wakasandula akuti kulimbabo, kufumbwa bubi abumambi kuzukulu lyasunu lyabayandula chitondezyo. Pesi tokwe chitondezyo pe chiyopegwa kunze kwachitondezyo cha Jona musinsiimi.
Mbanga Jona wakali amazuba atatu mubula bwamuswi mupati, alakwe Mwana Muntu uyoba amazuba atatu amansiku atatu mumoyo wanyika.
Bantu baku Ninivu bayoyimikila kunembo lyalubeta azukulu eli lyabantu aboobo liyopegwa mulandu. Nkambo bakeempwa mukukambawuka kwa Jona, lino amubone, umwi mupati kwinda Jona uli aano.
Mwami mwanakazi wakumusama uyobuka kulubeta abantu bakwe bazukulu eli lyabantu akulipa mulandu. Wakazwa kumajinkilo anyika kuti azomvwe busongo bwa Solomoni, alubo bona, umwi mupati kwinda Solomoni ulaano.
Na muuya mubi wazwa kumuntu, wakwinda mukati kamasena atakwe maanzi akuyandula kulyokezya, pesi tawubujani pe.
Mpawo lyakat, “Ndiyobweda kungánda yangu nkundakazwa; Nilyakabwed, lyakujana ng'anda eyo yakakukulwa akubambwa obotu.
Elyo lilayinka akubweza bweza imbi myuuya ili musanu ayibili mibi kwinda nguwo, lino ilasika kuzokkala omo. Abobo bubi bwamuntu kumamanino bwakabisisisya kwinda kumatalikilo. Mbukuyoba mbubobo kuzukulu lyabubi eli.”
Nakachili kwambula Jesu kumakamumakamu, amubone, banyina abakulana bakwe bakayimikila aanze, kabayandula kuti bambule anguwe,
Umwi wakati kulinguwe, “Bona banyoko abanike bako balimvwi aanze bayanda kwambula anduwe.”
Pesi Jesu wakasandula kuliyoyo wakamwambila, “Mbani baama bangu alubo mbaani banike bangu?”
Eelyo wakatandabika kuboko kwakwe akutondeka basikwiya bakwe mpawo wakati, “Bona, mbabo baama abanike bangu!
Nkambo kufumbwa uchita luyando lwa Taata ulikujulu, muntu oyo mukulana wangu, muchizi wangu, mbebaaba bangu.”
Mubuzuba obo Jesu wakazwa aanze ang'anda akukkala ambali alwizi.
Inkamu mpati yakamubunganina achakumuzyunguluka, lino wakanjila mubwato akukkala mukati, inkamu yoonse niyakachimvwi kunkomwe.
Elyo wakamba zintu zyiingi kulimbabo muzikozyanio. Wakati, “Amubone, mulimi wakaya kunze kukuyobyala imbuto.
Nakayobubyala, Imwi imbuto zyakawida ambali lyamugwagwa, mpawo bayuni bakasika akuzilya.
Imwi imbuto yakawida anyika ilamabwe, kwakati kwakatali muse mwingi. Mpawo mpawo zyakamena nkambo imuse tewakali abulamfu kukuyaansi.
Pesi izuba nilyakatenta, zyakawuumpwa, nkambo tezyakali amiyanda, aboobo zyakayuma.
Imbuto zimwi zyakawida mumaamvwa. Maamvwa akakomena mpawo akazisyanikizya.
Zimwi imbuto zyakawida mumuse mubotu mpawo zyakazyala zilyo, zimwi mwanda umwi windulwidwe chakuvula, zimwi makumi musanu alimwi, mpawo zimwi makumi aatatu.
Ooyo ulamatwi muleke amvwe.”
Basikwiya bakasika mpawo bakati kuli Jesu, “Nkambonzi nowambula makani aya muzikozyanio?”
Jesu wakasandula akwamba kuti kuli mbabo, “mulipedwe mwenya wakumvwisisya zisisidwe zyabwami bwakujulu, pesi kulimbabo tabapedwe pe.
Nkambo kufumbwa ujisi uyopegwa zyingi, alimwi uyoba azyindilide zyingi. Pesi utakwe, nekuba anchalacho chiyobwezegwa kuzwa kulinguwe.
Nchenchicho nchingambulaabo muzikozyanio: nekuba banokubona, pesi tababonesesyi pe; alubo nekuba balamvwa, pesi tabamvwisisisyi, nekuba kumvwisisisya.
Kulimbabo chisinsimicha Isaya chili zuzikizizigwe, echo chamba kuti, “Nekuba kumvwa mulamvwa, pesi takwe abunini nimuyomvwisisya; nekuba kubona muyobona, pesi takwepe nimuyobonesesya.
Nkambo myoyo yabantu aaba yaba mifubafuba mpawo miyumu kukumvwa, alubo bakajala meso aabo, kuti bataboni ameso aabo, nekuba kumvwa amatwi aabo, nikuba kumvwisisisya amyoyo yabo, kuti basanduke lubo, alubo ndikabaponesye.'
Pesi alongezegwe meso anu, nkambo alabona.
Nkasimpe ndati kulindinywe kuti basinsimi bayingi abantu baluleme bakayandisya kubona zintu ezyo nzimubona pesi tebakazibona. Bakayandisya kuzimvwa zintu nzimumvwa alimwi tebakazimvwa.
Lino ngamuswilile kuchikozyanyo chamulimi wakabyala imbutozyakwe.
Na umwi wamvwa ijwi lyabwami bwakujulu pesi talimvwisisisya, mubi umwi wasika akubweza chakabyalwa mumoyo wakwe. Eyi nimbuto yakabyalilwa ambali lyamugwagwa.
Chakabyalwa anyika ilamabwe muntu umvwa ijwi elyo mpawo mpawo wakalitambula akukondwa,
nekubabobo takwe miyanda mulinguwe nkambo mpawo ulakakatila chabunini. Nikuba makatazyo akupenzegwa kaabuka ankambo kajwi, ulafwambana kuwa.
Chakabyalwa mumuse ulamamvwa, oyu muntu umvwa ijwi, pesi misaalo yenyika abongelezyi bwabuvubi bwasyanikizya ijwi, elyo ulaba utachizyali michelo.
Imbuto yakaminzwa mumuse mubotu, ooyu muntu uumvwa ijwi akulimvwisisisya. Ulazyala michelo akuleta zilyo, kakutebulwa uumwi myanda, amuli umwi makumi musanu alimwi, amuli umwi makumi aatatu akayindululwa mbubonya mbozyakabyalwa.
Jesu wakababikila chimbi chikozyanyo kuli mbabo. Wakati, “Bwami bwakujulu bulimbuli mwalumi wakabyala imbuto imbotu mumuunda wakwe.
Pesi ibantu nibakachili koona, sinkondonyina wakasika elyo mpawo wakabyala masokwe akati ka wiiti mpawo wakiinka.
Mpawo masoonso nakazwa akuzyala bana balamuseke, aboobo isokwe lyakaboneka alyalo.
Babelesi bamukamuunda nibakasika mpawo bakati kulinguwe, 'Taa,' temwakabyala imbuto mbotu na mumuunda wenu? Nkambonzi nikwaba masokwe?'
Wakati kulimbabo, 'Sinkondoma nguwakachita echi.' Babelesi bakati kulinguwe, 'Mpo mulayanda na kuti twinke tukazinonkole?'
Mwini muunda wakati, 'Pee. Nkambo mwanoli kamunonkola masokwe, ngamuyononkokezya a wiiti.
Muleke zikule antomwe kusikila kukutebula. Elyo kuchiindi chakutebula ndizoti kubatebuzi, “Chakusanguna amunonkoole masokwe akwawanga misunta kuti akawumpwe, pesi mubunganisye wiiti mubutala bwangu.”
Elyo Jesu wakabika chikozyanisyo chiimbi kulimbaabo. Wakati, “Bwami bwakujulu buli mbuli inseeke yalubangulamuntu njakabweza akwiibyala mumuunda wakwe.
Inseke eyi nindini loko kunseke zyoonse. Pesi na yakomena, inga yabampati kwinda misamu yamuchilili. Ngayakomena kwinda ziziki zyamuchilili, ngayaba musamu wakuti bayuni bawuluka basike akuyaka zizumbo mumitabi yayo?”
Alimwi Jesu wakabambila chimbi chikozyanyo. “Bwami bwakujulu buli mbuli bumena bwamwanakazi bwakabweza akuswanizya zimpanzi zitaatu zyabusu bwa wiiti kusikila zyafufumuka.”
Zyoonse ezi zintu Jesu wakazyaamba muzikozyanio kumakamu; aboobo takwe nchakamba katambide muchikozyanio.
Echi chakalibobo kuchitila kuti chakambwa kwinda mumusinsimi chizuzikizigwe, Awo mpakamba kuti, “Ndiyojula mulomo muzikozyanisyo. Ndiyowamba zintu zyakasisikene kuzwa kumatangunino anyika..”
Jesu wakasiya makamu makamu akuya mungánda. Basikwiya bakwe bakeza kulinguwe akwamba kuti, “Tupandulwide chikozyanio chamasokwe amumuunda.”
Jesu wakabasandula wamba elyo wakati, “Ooyo ubyala imbuto mbotu Mwana a Muntu.
Muunda ninyika; mpawo imbuto mbotu, aba mbana baLeza bamubwami. Imasokwe mbana bamubi umwi.
Lino sinkondo wakabyala ngudyabulosi. Butebuzi ngimamanino achiindi, mpawo batebuzi mbaangelo.
Nkinkako mbuli masokwe mbabunganigwa akuumpwa amulilo, aboobo mbukuyooba kumamanino achiindi.
Mwana amuntu uyotuma baangelo bakwe, elyo bayobunganisya aanze abwami bwakwe zintu zyoonse zyakali kuchita kuti kube ababo bakachita zitelede.
Bayobawalila mumabanga banga amulilo, nkubanoli kabakwila akuyoluma intwino.
Elyo kuyoba bantu balume kabamweka mbuli zuba mubwami bwa Wisi. Ulamatwi, ngamvwe
Ibwami bwakujulu buli mbuli buvubi busisidwe mumuunda. Muntu wakabona akubusisa. Mukukondwa kwakwe wakinka, wakawuzya zintu zyoonse nzyakali azyo, akuyowula munda oyo.
Alubo, Bwami bwakujulu bulimbuli muntu musambali uyandula ngale imbotu.
Nakijana imwi ngale imbotu, wakeenda akuzya zyoonse nzyakalazyo zintu akuyoyiwula.
Alubo bwami bwakujulu buli mbuli kazamba kakawalwa mulwizi, mpawo kabungania baswi bamisyobo yoonse.
Nikakazula, bazubi bakakabweza, bazubi bakakakwelela aanze kunkomwe. Elyo bakakkala ansi akubungania imbotu muzibikilo, pesi zyakatali kabotu bakazisowa.
Kuyoba obo kumamanino achindi. Baangelo bayosika akuyowandanya babi kuzwa kubaluleme.
Bayobawalila mumabangabanga oko nkubayokwila akuyoluma intwino zyameno.
“Mwazimvwa na zintu eezi zyoonse?” Basikwiiya bakati kulinguwe, “Iyii.”
Mpawo Jesu wakamba kuti kulimbabo, “Aboobo woonse mulembi wamulawu waba sikwiya kubwami bwakujulu ulimbuli muntu mwiningánda, ugwisya aanze zintu zyakwe zikulukulu ezipya kuzwa muzibikilo zyakwe.”
Abobo nichakaba kuti Jesu wamaninsya zikozyanio ezi, wakazwa kubusena oobo.
Eelyo Jesu nakanjila kuchisi chakwe akuyiisya bantu muchikombelo chabo. Chakazwa chakuti bakagamba akwamba kuti, “Muntu oyu ubujana kuli busongo bwakwe anguzu zyamalele aaya?
Oyu muntu teensi mwana wamubezi na? Sena banyina tabitwi kuti Meli? Sena bana bakwabo tabali ba Jemusi, Jozefu, Sayimoni a Judasi?
Sena bachizi bakwe, tabali akkati kesu? Uzijana kuli zintu zyoonse ezi?”
Bakalimvwa kabali amulandu anguwe. Pesi Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Musinsimi takwe bulemu kunze akuchisi chakulimbabo amumpuli yakwe.”
Alubo takwe pe nakachita malele miingi nkuko akambo kakutamusyoma kwabo.
Kuchindi echo, Mwami Helodi watamvwa makani atala a Jesu.
Wakamba kuti kubazike bakwe, “ooyu ngu Joni mubbabbatizyi; wabuka kuzwa kubafu. Nkinkaako nguzu eezi zilikubeleka mulinguwe.”
Nkambo Helodi wakali wajata Joni, wamwanga akumubika muntolongo nkambo ka Helodiyasi, mukamwanike wakwe Filipu.
Nkambo Joni wakambide kuti kulingu, “Tachili mumulawu pe kuti umukwate.”
Helodi wakali kukonzya kumujaya pesi wakayoowa bantu, nkambo bakali kumuyeyela kuti musinsiimi.
Pesi buzuba bwakuzyalwa kwa Helodi nibwakasika, mwana musimbi wa Helodiyasi wakazyana aakati kabo akubotezya Helodi.
Mukusandula wakasyomezya aachikonke chakuti uyomupa kufumbwa nchayokumbila.
Musule akulayililwa abanyina, wakamba kuti, “Mundipe aano, mundyido, mutwe wa Joni mu Bbabbatizyi.”
Mwami wakawusa kuchikumbizyo chakwe, pesi nkambo kachikonke chakwe alimwi akambo kabaabo mbakali kususula aabo, wakalayilila kuti kuchitwobo.
Wakatumina kuyodunsulwa kwamutwe wa Joni muntolongo.
Mpawo mutwe wakwe wakaletwa mundyido akupegwa kumwana musimbi oyo wakutola kuli banyina.
Mpawo basikwiya bakwe bakasika, babweza mutunta akuyowuzikka. Kwinda kwachechi, bakiinka akuyowambila Jesu.
Lino Jesu nakamvwa eechi, wakazwa mpawo awo, wakunjila mubwato kubusena buli kumbali. Makamu nakamvwa aanchicho, akamutobela amawulu kuzwa kumyunzi.
Mpawo Jesu wakasika musule lyabo akubona makamu mapati. Wakabaluzyalo kulimbabo eelyo wakaponya bachiswa babo.
Nilyakaba goko, basikwiya bakasika kulinguwe akwamba kuti, “Oobu busena mbwankanda, alimwi chiindi chamana. Mwayisya makamu kuti bayinke kumyuunzi mpawo bakalyulile chakulya kwabo.”
Lino Jesu wakabambila kuti, “Tabelede kumwayika. Amubape chimwi nchibatalye.”
Bakamba kuti kulinguwe, “Aano tuli aazinkwa zili musanu biyo answii zyobile.
Jesu wakati, “Amuzilete kulindime.”
Mpawo Jesu wakalayilila makamu abantu kuti akkale aansi mubwizu. Wakabweza zinkwa zili musanu answi zyobile. Walanga kujulu, wazilongezya akukwamuna zinkwa mpawo wazipa kuli basikwiya, alimwi basikwiiya bakapa makamu.
Boonse bakalya akukkuta. Mpawo bakabwezelela bufwefwelenga bwakachaala bwechakulya - nsangwa zizwide zili kkumi azibili.
Aabo bakalya bakali zyuulu zili musanu zyabaalumi, kutaamba abanakazi abaana.
Mpawo mpawo wakachita kuti basikwiya banjile mubwaato akwinka kunembo lyakwe kuli bumwi busena, mbubonya mbwakachili kumwayisya makamu makamu.
Nakamana kumwayisya makamu, wakatanta achilundu kuyokoomba. Nilyakaba goko wakali aalikke.
Pesi lino bwato bwakali bwabakule aanyika. Kabuchundwa amayuwe, nkambo muuwo wakali kuunga kuubakachizya.
Muchiindi chane mansiku Jesu wakabasikila, keenda aatala aalwizi.
Basikwiya nibakamubona kayobwenda ataala alwizi, bakakatazika akwamba kuti, “Musangu,” mpawo bakalila chakuyowa.
Pesi Jesu wakaamba kuli mbabo aawo akuti, “Amube bakozu ndime! Mutayowi.”
Pita wakamusandula akwamba kuti, “Mwami, na nduwe, ndilayilile kuti ndize kulinduwe atala amaanzi.”
Jesu wakati, “Kweza.” Mpawo Pita wakazwa mubwato akweenda aatala aamanzi kayinka kuli Jesu.
Pesi Pita nakabona muuwo mupati, wakayoowa. Mbwakatalika kubbila biyo, wakalila akwamba kuti, “Mwami ndifutule.”
Mpawo mpawo Jesu wakatandabika kuboko kwakwe, wajata Pita, akwamba kuti kulinguwe, “Nusilusyomo luniini, nkambonzi nodoneeka?”
Mpawo Jesu aa Pita nibakanjila mubwato, muuwo wakiimikila kuunga.
Mpawo basikwiiya bakali mubwato bakakomba Jesu akwaamba kuti, “Nkasimpe uli Mwana wa Leza.”
Nibakazubuka bakasika kunyika yaku Genesaleti.
Bantu bakubusena oobo nibakaziba kuti ngu Jesu, bakatumina makani konse muchisi choonse chizyungulukide, alimwi bakaleta kulinguwe woonse wakali kuchiswa.
Bakamukumbila kuti bajate moombe wajansi lyakwe, alimwi biingi bakuujata bakapona.
Mpawo bamwi ba Falisi abalembi bakasika kuli Jesu kabazwa ku Jelusalema. Bakaamba kuti,
“Nkamboonzi basikwiya bako nibakazyania aziyanza zyabapati? Nkambo tabasambi pe mumaboko nibalya chinkwa.”
Wakasandula akwamba kuti kulimbabo, “Alimwi nywebo - nkambonzi nimukazyania amulawu wa Leza nkambo kaziyanza zyanu?
Nkambo Leza wakamba kuti, “Lemeka wuso abanyoko, alimwi ooyo wambula bubi kuli wisi na banyina nkasimpe uyoofwa.
Pesi mwamba kuti, kufumbwa lugwasyondunoli watambula kuzwa kuli ndime lino nchipo chipegwa kuli Leza,”
Ooyo muntu telede kulemeka wisi. Munzila eyi mwawubula ijwi lya Leza. Malembe mabotu aachindi ali aajwi lya Leza aamwi malembe aachindi ali aamulawu. Nkuyumu kusalula chibalo chibotu. Nkambo kachiyanza chenu.
Nywebo nobasikuwupawupa! Isaya wakachita kabotu nakasinsiima aatala andinywe nakamba kuti,
'Bantu aba balandilemya amilomo yabo, pesi myoyo yabo ilikule andime.
Balandikomba chabuyo, nkambo balayiisya milawo yabantu mbuli njiisyo zyabo.”
Mpawo wakiita makamu kulinguwe mwini akwamba kuti kuli mbabo, “Amuswilile akumvwisya -
Tachiwo chinjila mukanwa chisofwazya muntu. Pesi echo chizwa mukanwa, eechi ncheenchicho chisofwazya muntu.”
Mpawo basikwiya bakasika akwamba kuti kuli Jesu, “Ulizi na kuti ba Falisi bakalebwa nibakamvwa makani aaya?”
Jesu wakasandula akwamba kuti, “Zizikki zyoonse ezyo Taata wakujulu nzyakatazikila ziyononkolwa.
Amubaleke aabalike, mbeenzyi boofu. Na moofu weenzya moofunyina, boonse bayowida mukkomba.”
Pita wakasandula akwamba kuti kuli Jesu, “Pandulula kalabiko aaka kulindiswe.”
Jesu wakaamba kuti, “Anywebo aambuli sunu tamumvwisisyi na?
Tamumvwisisisyi na kuti kufumbwa echo chinjila mukanwa chilayinda mwida mpawo chilazwa aanze mpawo chilasowegwa mukkomba?
Pesi izintu ezyo zizwa mukanwa zilazwa mumoyo. Nzenzizyo ezyo zisofwazya muntu.
Nkambo kumoyo kulazwa miyeyo mibi, bujayi, bumambi, bwamu, kubba, bukamboni bwakubeja, akulengelela.
Eezi nzenzizyo eezyo zisofwazya muntu. Pesi kulya amaboko atasambie pe takusofwazyi muntu pe.”
Mpawo kuzwa awo Jesu wakazwa ooko akwinka kuzisi zyakumyunzi yaku Taya aku Sidoni.
Amubone, mwanakazi mu Kkenani wakazwa kuchisi echo. Wakoompolola akwamba kuti, “Ndifwide luzyalo, Mwami, Mwana wa Devidi! Mwana wangu musimbi ulijisi loko dimoni.
Pesi Jesu taakwe jwi ndyakamusandula pe. Basikwiiya bakwe bakeza akumukumbila, bakati, “Mutande, nkambo uli koompolola musule lyesu.”
Pesi Jesu wakasandula akwamba kuti, “Nsitumidwe nikuba kuli umwi pesi kumbelele ziswekede zyakungánda ya Izilayeli.”
Pesi wakeza akuvundama aansi kunembo lyakwe, wati, “Mwami, ndigwasye.”
Wakasandula akwamba kuti, “Tachili kabotu pe kubweza chinkwa chabana akuchisowela tunkala.”
Wakati, “Mbukubede, Mwami, pesi aatulato tunkala tulalya tumwi twatufwefwelenga ooto tuuwa kumatebule abasimalelo aato.”
Mpawo Jesu wakasandula akwamba kuti kulinguwe, “Yo mwanakazi, lusyomo lwako ndupati; akuchitwe kulinduwe mbubonya mbuli mboyanda.” Mwana wakwe musimbi wakaponesegwa kuzwa kuchindi echo.
Jesu wakazwa kubusena oobo akwinka kumbali aalwizi lwaku Galili. Mpawo wakatanta akukkala nkuko.
Makamu makamu abantu mapati akeza kulinguwe. Bakaza abalema, boofu, basyataambi, abantu batyokede, abamwi bayingi bakali kuchiswa. Bakababika kumawulu aa Jesu, mpawo wakabasilika.
Eelyo makamu makamu akagamba nakabona bantu batambuli kabambula, batyokede kababakabotu, balemene kabeenda, aboofu kababona. Bakalumbayizya Leza wa Izilayeli.
Jesu wakaiita basikwiya bakwe akwamba kuti, “Ndafwaluzyalo kumakamu nkambo bakkala aandime kwamazuba ataatu kale mpawo tabakwe achakulya. Tandiyandi kubamwayisya kabatalyide, nkambo ngabayowizuka munzila.”
Basikwiya bakati kulinguwe, “Nkukuli nkotunga tulajana zinkwa zizulila kubusena bwankanda buliboobu kuti zikkutye makamu makamu mapati aalibobu?”
Jesu wakati, “Mujisi zinkwa zyongane?” Bakati, “musanu azibili, atuswi tuchebiyo.”
Mpawo Jesu wakalayilila makamu kuti akkale aansi aanyika.
Wakabweza zinkwa zili musanu azibili answi, mpawo nakamana kulumba, wakakwamuna zinkwa akuzipa kuli basikwiya.
Basikwiya bakazipa kumakamu. Bantu boonse bakalya mpawo bakakkuta. Mpawo bakabunganisya nsangwa zili musanu azibili zyabu fwefwelenga bwakachaala.
Aabo bakazilya bakali zyuulu zyone zyabaalumi, kutabala abanakazi abaana.
Mpawo Jesu wakamwayisya makamu makamu abantu akunjila mubwato mpawo wakaya kuchisi chaku Magadani.
Ba Falisi aba Sadusi bakeza mpawo bamusunka akumubuzya kuti abatondezye chitondezyo chizwa kujulu.
Pesi wakasandula akwamba kuti kuli mbabo, “Nikwasiya, mwamba kuti, 'Kuyoba kunze kubotu, nkambo ijulu lilasalala.'
Nikuba chifuma, mwamba kuti, 'Kunze kunoli kubi, nkambo ijulu lilasalala alimwi lilivumbidwe. Mulizi kupandulula bwime bwakujulu, pesi tamukonzyi kupandulula zitondezyo zyazyiindi.
Izyalane ibbi abwamu lilangula chitondezyo, pesi takwe chitondezyo chiyopegwa kulindilyo kutaamba chitondezyo cha Jona.” Mpawo, Jesu wakabasiya akutozya kumbi.
Basikwiya nibakasika mutala, bakalubide kubweza chinkwa.
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Amubone akuchenjela kubumena bwaba Falisi aba Sadusi.”
Elyo basikwiya bakabuzyanya akwamba kuti, nkambo tetwabweza pe chinkwa.”
Jesu wakaziba achechi mpawo wakati, “Nywebo nubasilusyomo lunini, nkambonzi mulabuzyania lwanu mpawo mulati nkambo tetwabweza pe chinkwa?
Tamuna kuziba na kwibaluka zinkwa zili musanu kulibali zyuulu zili musanu, alimwi kuti mwakabungika nsangwa zyongane?
Na zinkwa zili musanu aazibili kuzyuulu zine, alimwi kuti ninsangwa zyongane nzimwakabungika?
Ino nkambonzi kuti tamumvwisisyi kuti tendakalikwamba kulindinywe aatala achinkwa? Aamubone akuchenjela kubumena bwaba Falisi aba Sadusi.”
Mpawo bakamvwisya kuti takali kubambila kuti bachenjele bumena bwakali bwachinkwa pe, pesi kuti bachenjelele injisyo zyaba Falisi aba Sadusi.
Lino Jesu nakasika kuzisi zili kufwifwi aa Kkayisaliya Filipi, wakabuzya basikwiya bakwe, wati, “Ino bantu bati Mwana aa Muntu ngwani?
Bakati, “Bamwi bakwamba kuti nduwe Joni mubbabbatizyi; bamwi bati, Elayija; alimwi bamwi bakuti, Jelemiya, na umbi wabasinsimi.”
Wakati kulimbabo, “Pesi nywebo mundamba kuti ndimeni?”
Sayimoni Pita wakasandula wati, “Nduwe Kkilisito Mwana wa Leza uupona.”
Jesu wakasandula akwamba kuti kulinguwe, “Uli aacholwe, Sayimoni mwana a Jona, nkambo nyama abulowa teensi nzizyo zyakuyubunwida eezi, pesi Taata wangu uli kujulu.
Alimwi ambebo ndamba kuti kulinduwe nduwe Pita, mpawo aatala amwaala ooyu ndiyoyaka mbungano yangu. Milyango yazibunda tikozokuzunda.
Ndiyokupa zijaluzyo zyabwami bwakujulu. Kufumbwa nchotakaange aansi chiyosungwa akujulu, alimwikufumbwa nchotakangunune aansi chiyosungununwa aakujulu.”
Mpawo Jesu wakalayilila basikwiya kuti batakaambili naba umwi kuti wakali Kkilisito.
Kuzwa kuchindi echo Jesu wakatalika kwambila basikwiya bakwe kuti welede kwinka ku Jelusalema, kuyopengela zinti zyingi kumaanza abapati abapayizi bapati abalembi, kujayigwa, akubusigilwa kubuumi kubuzuba bwatatu.
Mpawo Pita wakamubweza akumutola kiumbali akumuchibula, wati, “Eezi azibe kule anduwe, Mwami; eezi zitazochitiki kulinduwe.”
Pesi Jesu wakachebuka akwamba kuli Pita kuti, “Zwaawa kusule lyangu, Satani! Uli chilebyo kulindime, nkambo toyeeyi atala azintu zya Leza, pesi ataala aazintu zyabantu.”
Mpawo Jesu wakati kuli basikwiya bakwe, “Na muntu kayanda kunditobela, aalilube lwakwe, abweze chiingano chakwe mpawo anditobele.
Nkambo kufumbwa uyanda kufutula buumi bwakwe uyobuswekelwa, alimwi kufumbwa uswekelwa buumi bwakwe nkambo kandime uyobujana.
Nkambo chigwasyanzi kumuntu kuvuba nyika yoonse pesi akaswekelwe buumi? Ninzi nchakonzya kupa muntu muchibaka chabuumi bwakwe?
Nkambo Mwana muntu uyoboola mubulemju bwa Wisi abangelo bakwe. Mpawo uyolumbula muntu umwi awumwi mbuli milimo yakwe.
Chakasimpe ndamwambila kuti, mpubali bamwi benu bayiimvwi ano batakwe nibayolabila lufu mane lumwi bakabone Mwana aa Muntu kaboola mubwami bwakwe.”
Nikwakayinda mazuba aali musanu abumwi Jesu wakabweza Pita, Jemusi a Joni mwanike wakwe, akubatola atala achilundu chilamfu abalikke.
Wakasanduka kunembo lyabo. Busyu bwakwe bwakabalama mbuli zuba, azisamo zyakwe zyakaba mbuli mumuuni.
Amubone kwakaboneka Mozesi a Elija balaambula awe.
Pita wakasandula akwamba kuti kuli Jesu, “Mwami, nchibotu kuli ndiswe kuti tube aano. Kuti koyanda, ndilakuchita matumba aatatu - chimwi chibe chako, achimwi chibe cha Mozesi, achimwi chibe cha Elayija.”
Elyo kachili mukwambula, amubone, ijoba libalaama lyakabavumba, mpawo amubone, kwakazwa ijwi mujoba, lyakati, “Ngoyu Mwanangu ngundiyandisya, muli nguwe mundibotelwa. Amuswilile nguwe.”
Lino basikwiya nibakalimvbwa, bakavundaama aansi, akuyowa loko.
Mpawo Jesu wakaza, akubaguma akwamba kuti, “Mubuke mutayowi.”
Mpawo bakalanga kujulu pesi takwe ngubakabona kunze kwa Jesu luzutu.
Lino nibakali kuseluka achilundu, Jesu wakabalayilila, wati, mutambili muntu chilengano eechi kusikila mwana amuntu akabuke kubafu.”
Basikwiya bakwe bakamubuzya, bati, ino nkamboonzi balembi bamulawu balaamba kuti Elija welede kusanguna kuza?”
Jesu wakasandula wati, “Elayija nchoonzyo uleza akubukulusya zintu zyoonse.
Lino ndamwambil, Elayija wakasika kale, pesi tebakamuziba pe. Kwinda kuchita nchibakali kuyanda kuli nguwe. Munzila njiiyo, Mwana amuntu uyofwaba mumaboko aabo.”
Mpawo basikwiya bakamvwa kuti wakalikwambambuula ambabo atala a Joni Mubbabbatizyi.
Eelyo nibakasika kunkamu, mwalumi wakaza kulinguwe, wafugama kunembo lyakwe akwamba,
“Mwami, komufwida luzyalo mwanawangu, mbuli mbwali sichisuntu ulokufwaba loko. Nkambo ukkala kawida mumulilo na mumaanzi.
Ndali mwetede kuli basikwiya bako, pesi tebamuponia pe.”
Jesu wakavwiila akwamba kuti, “Izyalane litasyomi akukakatila, ndiyooba achiindi chilamfu biyeni kandikkede andinywe? Ndiyoba andinywe kusika lili? Mumweete okuno kuli ndime.”
Jesu wakalayilila dimoni, mpawo lyakazwa mulinguwe, amulombe wakaponesegwa kuzwa muhola eelyo.
Mpawo basikwiiya bakeza kuli Jesu kumbali akwaamb, Nkaambonzi nitwakachilwa kulitandila aanze?”
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Nkambo kalusyomo lwenu lunini. Nkambo ndamwambila kasimpe, kansyonga mulijisi lusyomo niluba lunini mbuli nseke yembuto yamusitada, nga ulambila chilundu eechi, Eenda kuzwa ano kuya okiiya, alimwi chiyoyeenda, takukwe chiyokachizya kuli nduwe.”
Malembe mabotu achindi tajisi pe. Pesi oyu musyobo wadimoni tuyendi akuzwa kunze kwakukomba akulyiimya.
Kabachikede mu Galili, Jesu wakati kuli basikwiiya bakwe, “Mwana amuntu uyopegwa mumanza abantu,
alimwi bayomujaya, amubuzuba bwatatu uyobusigwa.” Basikwiya bakawusa kapati.
Elyo nibakasika ku Kapenawuma, ibalumi ibakabweza zipanzi zibili zyamali yamutelo bakaza kuli Pita akwamba, “Sa muyiisi wanu tagwisyi zipanzi zyamali yamutelo?
Wakati, “Iyii ulatela.” Pesi Pita nakanjila mungánda Jesu wakaamba wati kuli nguwe chakusanguna akuti, “Uyeyaanzi, Sayimoni? Kuzwa kuliini bami baansi nkubabweza mutelo na bulumbu? Kuzwa kubana baabo na nkubeenzu?”
Pita mpaakati, “kuzwa kubeenzu,” Jesu wakati kulinguwe, Pita wakasandula. “Lino bana bangununwa,” Jesu wakaamba.
Pesi kuti tutachiti basimutelo kuti bachite chibi, koya kulwizi, mukawaale kalobyo, akugwisya aanze inswi eyo itakazwe kutanguna. Na wajula mulomo wayo, ulajana Ishekkeli. Wibweze akwiipa basimutelo njiyangu ayako.
Kuchiindi eecho basikiiya bakaza kuli Jesu akwaamba kuti, “Ngwani mupati mubwami bwakujulu?”
Jesu wakayiita kana kanini kulinguwe wakakkazika aakati kabo,
akwaamba kuti kasimpe ndamwaambilamkuti ado musanduke akuba mbuli kana kaniini takukwe nimunga muyoonjila mubwami.
Nkaambo kakaako, kufumbwa ulibombya mbuli mwana muniini nguumupati mubwami bwakujulu.
Kufumbwa utambula kana kaniini mbuli oobu muzina lyangu wambula ndime.
Pesi kufumbwa utuka umwi wabaaba baniini bamusyoma ulabalebya, chilabota mbubo kulinguwe kuti aangwe ndomba lyabbwe munsingo yakwe, akubbizigwa aakati kalwizi.
“Maawe kunyika nkaambo kazilebyo! Aboobo kuleelede kuti zilebyo zibe, pesi maawe kuli yooyo muntu weeta zilebyo!
Kuti luboko lwakp na chituta chako chikupa chilebyo, chigonke ukuwaalila kule anduwe, kuli mbubo, kunjila mubuumi koli chilema na kotyokede kwiinda kuowelwa mumulilo utamani koli aamaboko aabili na mawuulu aabili.
Na liso lyko likuchita kuba chilebyo, ulidadule ulisowele kule aanduwe. Kuli mbubo kuti unjle mubuumi aliso limwi kwiinda kusowelwa mubbila lyamulilo koli ameso aabili.
Amuchenjele kuti utasmpawuuli umwi wabaaba baniini. Mbuli mbundaamba kulindinywe kuti kujulu kuli baangelo lyoonse balanga kubusyu bwa Taata uli kujulu.
Malembe mabotu achi Giliki taajisi munchali ooyo ulaabupanduliuzi bujanika muli bumwi, nkaambo Mwana aamuntu wakaza kuzoofutula eecho chakasweekede.
Uyeeyanzi? Kuti umwi uli aambelele mwaanda, mpawo iimwi yasweek, takonzyi kusiya zili makumi aali musanu aane azili musanu azine aatala aakalundu akuya kuyooyanduula eeyo isweekede?
Na wayijana, ndamwaambila kasimpe, ulabotelwa kwiinda eezyo zitasweekede.
