Munzila ikozyene, teesi kuyanda kwa Taata uli kujuliu kuti umwi wabaaba baniini kuti batafwidilili.
Kuti munyoko wakubisizya, koya ukamutapatile aakati kako anguwe luzutu. Na wakuswiilila, ulajana munyoko.
Pesi na takuswiilili, bweza umwi na bambi babili kuti milomo yababili na baka, mboni batatu lyoonse jwi lilazuminika.
Lino kuti wakaka kubaswiila, ambila mbungano, kuti wakaka alimwi kuswiilila mbungano, muleke aabe mbuli muhedeni akuba mbuli simutelo.
Ndamwaambila kasimpe, kufumbwa zintu nzimwaanga ansi zilaangwa akuju; lu, akufumbwa zyaangununwa ansi zilaanguununwa akujuliu.
Alubo ndamwaambila na babili bazuninana atala achimwi nchibakumbila balachichitilwa a Taata uli kukulu
. Aawa ali kobile na kotatu mpubabungene aamwi muzina lyangu, akooko ndinooli aakati kabo.
Eelyo Pita waza akwaamba wati kuli Jesu, “Mwamio tungee mukwesu kandisizya nzyentimulekelele? Kusikila tuli musanu atubili!
Jesu wakati kuli nguwe, “Tandimwaambili tuli musanu atubili, kusikila kumakumi musanu aabili katupetedwe kusika kumusanu atubili.
Nkaambo kaako bwami Bwakujulu bulikozyene awumwi Mwami wakayanda kubamba makani aababelesi bakwe.
Mbuli mbwakasanguna kubamba, umwi wababelesi wakaletwa kuli nguwe iwakapedwe kkumi lyazyuulu zyamataalenta.
Pesi mbwatakajisi chakuliya, Mwami wakwe wakamulayilila kuti awuzigwe, antoomwe amwanakazi wakwe abana azyoonse nzyakaliya kuchitwe.
Mpawo mubelesi wakawida ansi, wavundama akwaamba wati, “Mwami ndikkazike moyo, lino ndilakuya yoonse.
Lino Mwami wamubelesi mbukunga wamufwida wamufwida luzyalo wamwaangwida mpawo wamulekelela chikoloto.
Pesi mubesi ooyo wakeenda akujana umwi mubelesi wamunyina wakalijisi madinali mwaanda, wakamubweza, watalika kumusina akwaamba kuti ndiliye nzwakabweza kuli ndime.
Mpawo mubelesinyina wakawida ansio wamukumbila wati, “Ndikkazikile moyo, ndilakuliya.
Pesi mubelesi mutaanzi wakakaka. kwiinda, wakaya wakuya kuyoomuwalila muntolongo kusika akaliye nzyakali mupede.
Lino babelesinyina nibakabona zyakachika, bakawusa loko. Bakasika akwaambila mwami wabo zyoonse zyachitika.
Mpawo mwami wamubelesi wakamwiita wati kulinguwe, iwe numubesi mubi, ndakakulekelela chikoloto choonse nkaambo wakandikumbila.
Waleleede kumufwida luzyalo mubelesinyokwe, mbuli mbundakakufwida luzyalo?
Mwami wakwe wakanyema akumupeda kuli basintolongo kusikila akaliye zyoonse nzyakabwezede.
Mbuboobo alakwe Taata wakujulu mbwayoomuchitila na temwalekelela munyoko kuzwa mumoyo.
Kwakaba kuti Jesu amane majwi ay, wakazwa ku Galili waya kuchisi cha Judiya mutala amulonga wa Jodani.
Makamu makamu akamutobela, mpawo wakabaponia nkukoko.
Ba Falisi bakaza kuli nguwe, bamusunka, baamba kuli nguwe, “chili mumulawu kuti mwalumi aleke mwanakazi wakwe, katakwe kaambo.
Jesu wakasandula akwaamba, “sa temwakabala kuti oyo wakabalenga kuzwa kumatalikilo wakabalenga baalumi a abanakazi?”
Alubo oyo iwakabelnga wakati, 'Nkambo kaako Mwalumi uyosiiya wisi abanyina akukakatila kumwanakazi wakwe, aba bobile babe nyama imwi.
Lino tabachili babili, pesi nyama imwi. Nkinkaako echo Leza nchakaswaniizya, kutabi muntu uchipambukanya.”
Bakati kulinguwe, “Nkaambonzi elyo Mozesi wakatulayilila kuti apegwe lugwalo lwakulekana mpawo amuleke?”
Wakati kuli mbabo, “Nkaambo kabuyumu bwamyooyo yenu, Mozesi wakamuzumizya kuleka banakazi benu, pesi kumatalikilo tekwakali munzila eyo pe.
Ndamwambila, kufumbwa uleka mwanakazi wakwe, kunze kwamakani abuvule, akuyo kwata uumbi, wachita bumambi; amwalumi ukwata mwanakazi wakalekwa wachita bumambi.”
Basikwiiya bakati kuli Jesu, “Na kuti ntwaambo twamwalumi amwanakazi wakwe, tachili chibotu kukwata.”
Pesi Jesu wakati kuli mbabo, “Teensi bonse batambula kaambo aka, pesi kuli baabo luzutu bapedwe.
Nkambo nkubali bazibe bakachitwa bazibe abantu, alimwi mpubali bazibe bakalichita bazibe lwabo beni nkambo ka Bwami bwakujulu kuli ooyo ukonzya kutambula injiisyo eyi, muleke ayitambule.”
Lino bana baniini bakaletwa kuli nguwenkuti abaampe amaboko akukomba, pesi basikwiiya bakwe bakabakasya babakalalila.
Pesi Jesu wakaamba wati, “Amuzumizye bana banini, mutabakasyi kuti baze kuli ndime, nkambo Bwami bwakujulu mbubwabo bali boobu.”
Wakabika maboko aakwe alimbabo mpawo wakabasiya.
Amubona, mwalumi wakaza kuli Jesu akwamba kuti, “Muyiisi, nchichili chintu chibotu nchindinga ndilachita kuti ndibe abuumi ibutamani?”
Jesu wakati kuli nguwe, Nkamboonzi niwandibuzya atala chitegwa nchibotu? Kunze kwachintu chimwi, pesi na koyanda kunjila mubuumi, baamba milayizyo.”
Oyu mwalumi wakati kuli nguwe, milayizyo nzi?” Utajayi, utachiti bumambi, utabbi, utapi bukamboni bwakubeja,
lemeka wuuso abanyoko akuyanda ngoyakilene anguwe mbuli lwako omwini.”
Mwalumi mukubusi wakati kuli nguwe, “Zyoonse ezi zintu ndakazilemeka. Ndichiyanaanzi?”
Jesu wakamwambila wati, “Na koyanda kuti ulondoke, koya, ukawuzye lubono lwako, akuyopa bachete, mpawo uyooba abuvubi kujulu, lino uboole, unditobele.”
Pesi eelyo mwalumi mukubusi nakamvwa Jesu nzyakaamba, wakayinka kawuside, nkambo wakalijisi imbono nyiingi.
Jesu wakaambila basikwiiya bakwe, “Kasimpe ndamwambila, nchiyumu kumuvubi kuti akanjile kubwami bwakujulu.
Alimwi ndamwambila kuti, nkutete kunkamela kunjila muliso lyaneleti kwinda kuti muvubi anjile mubwami bwa Leza.”
Lino basikwiiya nibakamvwa oobo, bakagambilwa loko, akwaamba kuti, “Ino ngwani ukoonzya kuyofutulwa?”
Jesu wakabalanga akwaamba kuti, 'kubantu tachikonzeki, pesi kuli Leza zintu zyoonse zilakonzeka.”
Mpawo Pita wakavwiila akwamba kuti “Langa, twasiya zintu zyesu zyoonse twatobela nduwe. Ani mpawo tukajanenzi?”
Jesu wakati kuli mbabo, “Ndamwambila kasimpe kuti, muchiindi chiza Mwana a Muntu nayokkala achuno chakwe chabulemu, inywe nimwakanditobela muzokkala azyuno zilikkumi azibili, mukabeteke misyobo ili kkumi ayibili ya Izilayeli.
Woonse oyo iwakasiide maanda, babunyiina, bachizi, wisi, banyina niiba myuunda nkambo kazina lyangu uyotambula tuli mbuli mwanda umwi akukona buumi ibutamani.
Pesi bataanzi baanji bayoba bakumamanino, abakumamanino bayoba batanzi.
“Nkambo bwami bwakujulu buli mbuli mwanimunda wakazwa kuseni loko kuyotamba basikubeleka mumuunda wakwe wamasansa.
Nikwakamana kuzuminana abasimulimu kudinali lyomwe abuzuba, wakabatuma kumunda wamasansa wakwe.
Alubo wakenda chindi chamahola atatu mpawo wakabona bamwi basimilimu kabayimvwi kabatakwe nchibachita kubusena bwakuuzizya.
Kuli mbabo wakati, 'Anywebo, kamuya mumuunda wamasansa alubo ndilakumupa zilikabotu.' Nkako bakayinka kumulimu.
Alimwi wakiinka kunze muhola lyamusanu alimwi amuhola lyamusanu aane, akuyochita chikozyenie.
Limbi lubo kusika kuhola lyakkumi alimwi wakazwa alimwi wakujana bamwi balimvwi katakwe nchibalikuchita.
Wakati kulimbabo, 'nkambonzi nimwimvwi awa kamutakwe nchimulikuchita zuba lyoonse?' “Kulinguwe bakamba kuti, 'nkambo takwe pe watutambila mulimo.' “kulimbabo wakati, ánywebo lubo mwinke mumunda wamasansa.”
Lino nilyakaba golezya, mwani muunda wakati kumupati wamulimo, 'Yita basikubeleka alubo ubape bulumbu bwabo, utangune abasyalizi umane akumutaanzi.'
Eelyo basimilimo bakanjila ahola lyakkumi alimwi bakeza, awumwi wabo wakatambula dinali.
Nibakeza basimulimo batanzi, bakalikuyeya kuti balatambula zyiingi, pesi abalabo bakatambula dinali lyomwe awumwi.
Nibakatambula bulumbu bwabo, bakasyoloka atala mwanimunda.
Bakati, 'Aba basimulimo basyalizi babeleka biyo hola lyomwe, pesi mwabachitila bvukozyenie andiswe, iswebo nitwaminwa buzuba bonse alubo muzuba lyuumpa obu.'
“Pesi mwanimunda wakavwiila umwi wabo wati, 'mwenzuma, takwe chibi nchindamuchitila. Temwazuminene andime na ku dinali lyomwe?
Amubweze zyanu mwende enzila yanu. Ndasala kupa basimulimo basyalizi zikozyenie azyenu.
Tazili mumulawu na kuchita mbuli m bwenjanda achintu changu? Wabasibbivwe na nkambo ndimwabi?'
Nkinkako musyalizi uyoba mutanzi, amutaanzi uyoba musyalizi.” Malembe aansiku mabotu takwe banji bayitidwe, pesi basalidwe mbache.
Lino Jesu nakalikuya ku Jelusalema, wakabweza abalikkumi ababili kumbali, alubo munzila wakati kulimbabo,
“Amubone, tuyobuya ku Jelusalema, alubo Mwana Muntu nkwayowabwa mumaboko abapayizi bapati abalembi basimulawu. Bayomutama kusikila kulufu
alubo bayomutola kuli bamasi kuti bamuniake, akumuuma, akuyomubambula. Pesi mubuzuba bwatatu uyobusigwa.”
Mpawo banyina babana balombe ba Zebbediya bakaza kuli Jesu abana babo. Wakafugama aansi kunembo lyakwe alubo wakakumbila chimwi chintu kulinguwe.
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Niinzi ncholombozya?” wakati kulinguwe, “Layila bana bangu aba kuti bakkale, umwi kululyo umwi kulumwensi lwaluboko, mubwami bwako.”
Pesi Jesi wakasandula wati, “Tochizi nchokumbila. Ulakonzyana kunywa mukanywido nkindaamba kunywa?” Kulinguwe bakamba kuti, “Tulakonzya.”
Wakamba kuti kulimbabo, “Kanywido kangu mulakonzya kunywa. Pesi kukkala kululyo lwangu akuchimweensi tendime uupa pe, pesi nzizyabaabo bakabambilwa a Taata.”
Elyo basikwiya bamwi balikkumi nibakachimvwa echi bakanyema kapati abaaba babunyina babili.
Pesi Jesu wakabita kulinguwe akwamba kuti, “mulizi kuti bendelezi babamaasi balabendelezya, abalabo bapati baabo babulemu bezyanisya nguzu zyabo alimbabo.
Pesi tazyelede kuti kube anzila eyo akati kenu. Anukuti, kufumbwa ulomboozya kuba mupati akati kenu abe mulanda wenu,
alubo kufumbwa ulombozya kuba mutanzi akati kenu welede kuba mulanda wenu,
mbuli Mwana Muntu mbatakazidide kukutawukilwa, pesi kukutawuka, akupa buumi bwakwe mbuli muulo wabingi.”
Nibakazwa ku Jelikko, inkamu mpati yakamutobela.
Kwakali balumi babili boofu bakakkede kumbali lyamugwagwa. Elyo nibakamvwa kuti Jesu walikwiinda, bakompolola, “Mwami, Mwana Davida, ba aluzyalo andiswe.”
Mbungano yakaba kalalila, bababuzya kuti bawumune, pesi bakakwila chakwindilila, “Mwami, Mwana Davida, ba luzyalo kulindiswe.”
Mpawo Jesu wakayima alubo wakita kulimbabo wati, “ninzi nchimulombozya kuti ndimuchitile?”
Bakaamba kuti kulinguwe, “Mwami, kuti meso esu ajulike.”
Mpawo Jesu, kali wasungilizigwa aluzyalo, wakabaguma meso aabo, mpoonya awo bakatambula kubona akumutobela.
Awo Jesu abasikwiya bakwe nibakasika ku Jelusalema alubo bakakusika ku Bbetipegi, kukalundu ka Olivusi, mpawo Jesu wakatuma basikwiya bakwe bobile,
wakati kuli mbao, “Kamuya kumunzi ulikunembo, alimwi muyofwambana kubona donki lyangidwe nkuko, alubo akana kelyo. Mwawangunune mwalete kulindime.
Kuti kwaba utabe achakwamba atala angawo, mukambe kuti, 'Mwami ulayanda,'alimwi oyo muntu uyofwambana kumupa ngawo.
'Lino kwakaba kuti ezyo zyakali zyambwa kwinda kumusinsimi zizuzikizigwe. Wakati,
“Ambila mwana musimbi we Zioni, 'Langa, Mwami wanu ulaza kulindinywe, Ulibombede alimwi ulitantide a donki, Akukana ka donki, mwana we donki.”
Mpawo basikwiya bakinka bakuchita mbunya Jesu mbwakabalayililide.
Bakakuleta donki akana alubo bakabika zikobela zyabo a donki, alimwi Jesu Jesu wakakkala ajulu azikobela.
Makamumakamu manji akayala zikobela zyabo mumugwagwa, alimwi bamwi bakagonka ntabi zyamisamu akuyobuyala mumugwagwa.
Mpawo makamu akenda kunembo lya Jesu alubo abaabo bakali kuyobutobela kabayobompolola, “Hosana kumwana wa Davida!” Ulongezezegwe ngoyo uuza muzina lya Mwami! Hosana kuli simajulu!”
Elyo Jesu nakasika ku Jelusalema, idolopo lyoonse lyakali lyanyonganisigwa akwamba kuti, “Ngwani oyu?”
Makamumakamu akasandula, “Oyu ngu Jesu musinsimi uzwa waku Nazaleta mu Galili.”
Mpwo Jesu wakanjila mungánda ya Leza. Wakaandilanze boonse abo bakali kuula akuuzya mungánda ya Leza, alubo wakasandamuna matafula abasikuzizya mali alubo azikkalo zyababo bakali kuzya nziba.
Wakati kulimbabo, “Kulilembedwe, 'Ngánda yangu iyowambwa kuti ngánda yakukambya; pesi mwayichita kuti ibe chikkalilo chababb.”
Mpawo mofu achilima bakeza kulinguwe mungánda ya Leza, alubo wakabaponya.
Pesi elyo bapayiza bapati alubo abalembi bamulawu nibakabona zintu nzyakachita, alubo elyo nibakamvwa bana balompolola mungánda yaLeza alubo balamba, “Hosana kumwana a Davida, “bakaba akunyema kupati.
Bakati kulinguwe, “Ulibamvwide na kuti balikutyeni Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Iyii! Pesi takwe nimwakabalide, 'kuzwa kumilomo yabana banini atunyonka wakabamba intembawuzyo'?”
Mpawo Jesu wakabasiya alubo akuzwa mudolopo lya Bbetani akumana busiku nkuko.
Lino kuseni wakayinka nakali kujokela kudolopo, wakali waba anzala.
Nakabona mukuyu munsi lyamugwagwa, wakayinka kulinguwo akujana kakutakwe chintu kuli nguwo kunze kwamatu. Wakaamba kuti kulinguwo, “Kutakabi kuti kukabe michelo lubo kuzwa kulinduwe alimbi,” alubo mponya awo mukuyu wakapusama.
Elyo basikwiya nibakawubona, bakagamba akwamba bati, “Ibiyeni mukuyu wapusama mpawonyaawa?”
Jesu wakasandula akwamba kulimbabo, “Masimpe ndamba kulindinywe, na mulijisi lusyomo alubo kamutadoneki, tamukwe nimuyochita zyakachitwa amukuyu biyo pe, pesi muyowamba nikuba kuchilundu echi, 'Zyukuka akuwalwa mulwizi; alubo ziyochitika.
Kufumbwa nchimuyolomba munkombyo, chakuzumina, muyozitambula.”
Elyo Jesu nakasika mungánda yaLeza. Bapayizi bapati antomwe abapati babantu bakasika kulinguwe kali mukuyisya basikuti, “Anguzu nzi nzyochitya zintu ezi, alubo ngwani wakakupa nguzu ezi?”
Jesu wakasandula akwamba kulimbabo, “Ambebo ndilamubuzya mubuzyo umwi. Na mwandambila, ndiyomwambila kuti nkunguzunzi nzindichitya ezi.
Lubbabbatizyo lwaJoni - nkukuli nkulwakazwa? Lwakazwa kujulu na kuti nkubantu?” Bakambuzyania akati kabo, bakati,
“Na tutedi, Luzwa kujulu,' Ulamba kuti kulindiswe, 'Nkambonzi mpo nimwakatamusyoma?'Pesi na tutedi nkubantu,'tuyowa nkamu yabantu nkambo boonse babona Joni mbuli musinsimi.”
Mpawo bakasandula Jesu alubo bati, “Tatuzi pe.” Wakamba alimwi kulimbabo, “Nsikwe nensikamwambile ambebo kuti ninguzunzi nzindichitya azyozintu ezi.
Pesi muyeyaanzi mwalumi wakali abana balombe babili. Wakaya kumutanzi alubo wakati, “mwanangu, koya ukabeleke sunu mumunda wamasansa.
“Mwana wakasandula wati, “Tandiinki, pesi mukuya kwachiindi wakasandula mizezo yakwe wakinka.
Mpawo mwalumi wakaya kumwana wachibili akwamba chintu chikozyenie. Wakasandula wati, 'Ndilayinka, 'Ta; pesi takwe nakinka pe.
Nguuli mubana babili aba wakachita kuyanda kwawisi?” Bakati, “Mutanzi.” Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Masimpe ndaamba kulindinywe, basimutelo abasimamambe bayonjila mubwami bwa Leza kamutana kunjila.
Nkambo Joni wakeza kulindinywe minzila yabululami, pesitemwakamusyoma pe. Pesi basimutelo abasimamambe bakamusyoma. Pesi nywebo, nikuba elyo mwakazibona ezi, temwakeempwa mukuya kwachindi alubo temwakamusyoma.
“Amuswilile kuli ambi mambilambali. Kwakali umwi mwalumi, mukamwini munda wakabyala masansa, wakayaka lubaya alinguwo; wasikusya chikandilo mukati kawo, wayaka ngánda yamujulu, alubo wakayiboleka kuli basikulima masansa. Mpawo wakaya kulichimwi chisi
Elyo chiindi chakutebulwa kwamasansa nichakasika, wakatuma bamwi babelesi kuli basikulimina masansa kuti bakabweze michelo yakwe.
Pesi basikulimina masansa bakabweza babelesi bakwe bawuma umwi, bajaya awumwi, alubo bamutulula mabwe.
Alubo, mwanimunda wakatuma bambi babelesi bayingi kwinda batanzi, pesi basikulimina masansa bakabajata zikozyenie.
Kwiinda awo, mwanimunda wakazotuma mwanakwe kulimbabo, kuti, 'Bayo mulemeka mwanangu.
“Pesi elyo balimi bamasansa nibakabona mwana, bakati akati kabo, 'Ngoyu sikukona. Mubole, muleke tumujaye akubweza lukono.
'Nkinkako bakamubweza, bamusowela kunze amuunda akumujaya.
Lino elyo mwanimunda asika, ninzi nchayochita abo balimi bamasansa?”
Bakati kulinguwe, “Uyonyonyona abo baalumi babuyo muli imwi nzila njumu, alubo uyobatandila aanze amuunda akubika bambi basikulimina masansa, bantu bayomupa chabilo chazilimwa kuchiindi chakuyebula.”
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Sena temwakabala mumalembe, Íbbwe bayaki ndibakakaka lyakachitwa munsemo. Echi chakazwa ku Mwami, alubo zilagambya mumeso esu'?
Nkinkako ndamba kuti kulindinywe, bwami bwa Leza buyobwezwa kuzwa kulindinywe akuyopegwa kuchisi chiyopanga michelo yacho.
Kufumbwa uwida atala abbwe eli ulakutyoka kuba tumpanzi, pesi umwi ngulitawide atala ulakupwasuka.”
Elyo bapayizi bapati aba Falisi nibakamvwa mambilambali akwe, bakamvwisisisya kuti wakalikwamba ataala ambabo.
Bakayandula kumwanga, pesi bakayoowa makamu abantu, nkambo bantu bakali mujisi mbuli musinsiimi.
Jesu wakambula lubo kulimbabo mumambila mbali wakati,
“Bwami bwakujulu buli mbuli umwi mwami wakabambila ipobwe lyakukwatana lyamwanakwe.
Wakatuma babelesi bakwe kuyoyita abo bakatambidwe kuti baze kupobwe pesi tebakasika.
Alimwi mwami wakatuma bambi babelesi, kuti, bambile aabo batambidwe, “Mulange, ndabambilila chisusulo chabasune bangu angómbe zyangu zinenede zyajayigwa, alubo zintu zyoonse zyabizwa. Muze kupobwe lyalukwatano.”
Pesi tebakaswilila pe alimwi bakainka, umwu kumunda wakwe mupati, awumwi kumakwebo akwe.
Bamwi bakajata babelesi ba Mwami, bakabajata enzila ifwisya nsoni, akubajaya.
Mwami wakanyema, akutuma basilumamba bakwe akuyonyonyona aabo bajayi akubawumpila dolopo lyabo.
Mpawo wakati kubabelesi bakwe, kuswanizigwa kwazulila, pesi abo bakatambidwe tebakali kwelela.
Aboobo kamuya mumanzanino anzila akuyotamba bantu banji kupobwe lyakukwatana mbuli mbimutajane.'
Babelesi bakayinka enzila akubunganya antomwe bantu boonse mbibakajana, bonse babi ababotu. Nkinkako ngánda yepobwe lyakukwatana yakazozula abantu.
Pesi Mwami nakasika mukati kuzolanga batambidwe, wakabona kakuli mwalumi wakatazwete zizwato zyapobwe lyalukwatano.
Mwami wakati kulinguwe, Mwenzuma, wanjila byeni omuno kotasamide zizwato zyapobwe lyalukwatano?'Pesi mwalumi wakabula alyakwamba.
Mpawo mwami wakati kubabelesi, 'mumwange mwalumi oyu kumaboko akumawulu, alubo mumusowele aanze mumudima, oko kunoli kulila akuluma ntwino.'
Nkambo mbingi bantu batambidwe, pesi mbache biyo basalidwe.”
Mpawo baFalisi bakinka akuyobamba mbubatamuche Jesu kuzwa kungambwido yakwe.
Mpawo bakatuma kulinguwe basikwiya babo, antomwe abaka Helodiya. Bakati kuli Jesu, 'Ómuyisyi, tulizi kuti uli wakasimpe, alubo kuti uyiisya nzila yaLeza mubwini. Tomvwi miyeyo yawumwi pe alubo totondezya kusiyanisya pe akati kabantu.
Mpo kotwambila, uyeyanzi? Zili mumulawu na kubbadala mutelo kuli Siza na pe?”
Pesi Jesu wakamvwisisisya bubi bwabo wakati, “Nkambonzi nimundisunka, nywebo nobasikuupawupa?
Munditondezye mali yabbwe yamutelo.” Mpawo bakamwetela dinali kulinguwe.
Jesu wakati k ulimbabo, “Ngwani ulachechi chikozyanisyo e zina?”
Bakasandula kuti, “nzizya Siza.” Mpawo Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “alimwi amupe Siza zintu zya Siza, alubo kuli Leza zintu zya Leza.”
Elyo nibakazimvwa, bakagamba. Mpawo bakamusiya akwenda.
Mubuzuba oobo bamwi ba Sadusi, abo baamba kuti takwepe bubuke bwabafu, bakeza kulinguwe. Bakamubuzya,
kabati, 'Muyisyi, Mozesi wakatedi, “Na mwalumi wafwa, kataside bana, mukulana wakwe welede kukwata banakwe akumujanina bana mukulana wakwe.
Kwakali bakulana bali musanu ababili. Mutanzi wakakwata mpawo wakafwa katasiide bana, wakasiya mwanakazi wakwe kumwanike wakwe.
Alimwi alakwe mwanike wachibili wakachita chintu chikozyania, mpawo awatatu, mulongo woonse kusikila kuli wamusanu ababili.
Kwinda kwabo boonse, mwanakazi wakazofwa.
Lino kububuke bwabafu, ngwani utakabe mwani mwanakazi mubakulana bali musanu ababili? Nkambo boonse bakali mukwete.”
Pesi Jesu wakbasandula akuti kulimbabo, “Nywebo muliswekede, nkambo tamuzi malembe naa inguzu zya Leza.
Nkambo mububuke bwabo takwe nekuba kukwata nikuba kukwatisigwa. Anukuti, bayoba mbuli baangelo bali kujulu.
Pesi atala abubuke bwabafu, temwakabala na zyakaambwa kulindinywe a Leza, kuti
Ndime Leza wa Abbulahamu, Leza wa Ayizeki, alimwi Leza wa Jakobo'? Leza teensi Leza wabafwide, pesi waba pona.”
Eelyo makamu nakamvwa eezi, bakagamba kunjiisyo zyakwe.
Pesi ba Falisi nibakamvwa kuti Jesu wakawumuzya ba Saduki, bakalibungania lwabo beni antomwe.
Umwi wabo, uyiide zyamulawu, wakamubuzya mubuzyo, kumusunka -
“Muyiisi, nguuli mulayizyo mupati mumulawu?”
Jesu wakati kulinguwe “Yanda Mwami Leza wako a moyo woonse, alubo amiyeyo yako yoonse.'
Oyu ngomulazyo mupati alubo ngomutanzi.
Alimwi awabili mulayizyo ulimbuli oyu - Ýanda mwenzinyokwe mbuli mboliyanda lwako.'
Amilawu eyi ibili mpokuzulila mulawu woonse abasinsimi.”
Lino ba Falisi nibakachibungene antomwe, Jesu wakababuzya mubuzyo.
Wakati, “muyeeyanzi aatala a Kkilisito? Mwana wani?” Bakamusandula, “mwana wa Devidi.”
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Biyeni mpo Devidi mumuuya ulamwiita kuti Mwami, kaamba,
'Mwami wakati ku Mwami wangu. “Kkala kuluboko lwangu lwachilisyo, kusikila ndayita basinkonyokwe chikkalilo chamawulu ako”?
Kuti Devidi wakiita Kkilisito kuti 'Mwami,' nkambonzi nali mwana wa Devidi?”
Takwe wakakonzya kumusandula jwilyomwe, alubo takukwe wakachili kuyanda kumubuzya imbi mibuzyo kuzwa elyo zuba.
Mpawo Jesu wakambuula kubbunga lyabantu alimwi akuli basikwiiya bakwe.
Wakati, “Balembi aba Falisi bakkala muchuno cha Mozesi.
Nkiinkako kufumbwa nchibamulayilila kuchita amuchite nzizyo akuzibeleka. Pesi mutakatobelezyi inchito zyabo pe, nkambo baambula zintu nzibatachiti pe.
Iyii, balabamba mitolo miyumu kukwinyampula, alimwi balabikkala amakkuko aabantu. Pesi bo lwabo tabanyampuli pe kanwe kabo kuti banyampule.
Balachita zyoonse nzibachita kuti babonwe abantu. Balalichitila zipati alimwi balakomezya myoombe yezibaki zyabo.
Bayanda zyuuno zyabapati kumapobwe alimwi azyuuno ezyuuno zyabapati muzikombelo,
alimwi bayanda injuzyo zilikabotu muzisambalilo, alimwi akwiitwa kuti 'Mwami'abantu.
Pesi inywebo tamwelede pe kwitwa kuti 'Mwami' nkambo mulijisi umwi alimwi nywebo moonse mulibabunyina.
Alimwi mutayiti muntu anyika ansi aano kuti Taata, nkambo mulawe omwe Taata, alimwi ulikujulu.
Nikuba kuti ngamulategwa muyiisi, nkambo mulijisi muyisi umwi luzutu, Kkilisitu.
Pesi oyo mupati akati kenu uyoba mulanda wenu.
Nikuba nabaani ulisumpula uyofwinsigwa, alimwi nikubaani ulifwinsya uyosumpulwa.
Pesi maawe kuli ndinywe, nobalembi alimwi abaFalisi, nobasikuupawupa! mulajala abwami bwakujulu kubantu.
Nkambo tamunjili pe nywebo, alimwi tamukwe nimubazumizya aabo abayanda kunjila kuti banjile.
Maawe kulindinywe, nobalembi alimwi nobaFalisi, basikuupawupa! nkaambo muulya zintu zili mumaanda abamukabafu kamukomba nkombyo ndamfu. Muyotambula mulandu mupati. Maawe kulindinywe, nobalembi alimwi nobaFalisi, basikuupawupa! Nkambo mulayinka akulwizi alimwi akunyika kuti mukasandule muntu umwi, alimwi na waba oyo umwi, ngamwamuchita tubili kuba mwana wegehena mbuli ndinywe.
“Maawe kuli ndinywe, nobeenzyi baboofu, inywe nimuti, “Ooyo ukonka antempele takwe pe. Pesi ooyo ukonka angolida zyantempeli, ulangidwe kuchizuminano chakwe.
Inywe noboofu bafubafuba! Niinzi chipati, ingolida nikuba ntempeli eyo ichita ngolida kuti isalale?
Alimwi, óyo ukonka kuchipayililo, takukwepe. Pesi ooyo ukonka echo chili achipayililo, ulaangidwe kuchizuminano chakwe.
Inywe nobantu boofu, Niinzi chipati, ichipo nikuba chipayililo eecho chichita kuti ichipo chisalale?
Eelyo, ooyo ukonka kuchipayililo ukonka nchiicho alimwi azyoonse ezyo zili alinchicho.
Ooyo ukonka kuntempeli ukonka njiiyo alimwi ayooyo ukkala mukati.
Alimwi ayooyo ukonka akujulu ukonka achuuno chabulemu bwa Leza alimwi ayooyo ukkala alinchiicho.
Maawe kulindinywe nobalembi alimwi anoba Falisi basikuupawupa! Nkambo mulapayizya chakumi chazisyu zyachinsyungwa abbonko akanyansya, pesi mwasiya akutachita zintu zipati ezyo zyaamba mulawu- bwendelezi bubotu alimwi aluzyalo mpawo alusyomo. Pesi eezi mwalelede kuti naka mwazichita alimwi akutasiya nikuba chimwi chanzizyo.
Inywebo nobasikwenzya boofu, mulatingwa akawuka pesi mumena inkamela!
Maawe kulindinywe, nobalembi alimwi aba Falisi, basikuupawupa! Nkaambo musanzya inkomeki kunze kwayo mpawo andyido, pesi muzili mukati zilizwide kutangala akutayendelezegwa kabotu.
Inywe noba Falisi boofu! Musanzye muzili mukati nkomeki sansina amukati kandyido, kuchitila kuti kunze kusambe akulako.
Maawe kulindinywe, nobalembi aba Falisi basikuupawupa! Nkaambo mulimbuli tubanda tulambidwe amilambo ituuba, eezyo zilangiika kubota anze, pesi mukati zizwide mafuwa abantu bakafwa alimwi azyoonse zyamudima.
Munzila njiyeeyo, anywebo aanze kwanu muli mbuli bantu baluleme kubantu, pesi mukati mulizwide kuupawupa ameso alimwi abubi.
Maawe kulindinywe, nobalembi aba Falisi, basikuupawupa! Nkaambo mulayaka tubanda twabasinsiimi alimwi akubotezya tubanda twabaluleme.
Mwamba kuti, “Kwanoli twakaliko mumazuba abamataata, nikuli tetwakabape mulibaabo bakatila bulowa bwabasinsiimi.'
Nkinkaako mulalyaamba nobeeni kuti muli bana babaabo bakajaya basinsiimi.
Alimwi mwazuzikizya bulemu bwabamawuso.
Inywe nobazooka, inywe nobana bachipile, muyokuchija biyeni kubetekwa kwagehena?
Nkambo kako, amubone, ndamutumina basinsimi abalumi basongo alimwi abalembi. Bamwi babo muyobajaya akubagankamina, alimwi bamwi muyobakwipawula muzikombelo zyenu alimwi muyobatanda kuzwa kumunzi akumunzi.
Impindu njakuti andinywe kuyozwa bulowa boonse bwabataluleme oobo bwakatika enyika, kuzwa kubulowa bwa Abbelu mululami, domane kubulowa bwa Zakkaliya mwana wa Bbelekkiya, ooyo ngumwakajaya akati kantempeli achipayililo.
Kasimpe ndamwambila, zintu eezi zyoonse ziyozida aabo bapona sunu
“Jelusalema, Jelusalema, inywe nimujaya basinsiimi alimwi akudonkola aabo batumwa kuli nduuwe! Ndakaliswini kuyanda kubunganya bana bako antoomwe, mbuli inkuku mbifukatila twana twayo munsi lyamababa ayo, pesi tewakazumina pe!
Amubone, ngánda yenu yachaala kulindinywe yaba mbulitongo.
Alimwi ndamwambila, tamuchizondiboni pe kuzwa lino dokusikila mukaambe kuti, uulachoolwe ooyo uuza muzina lya Mwami.”
Jesu wakazwa aanze achikombelo weenda. Basikwiiya bakwe bakeza kulinguwe kuzomutondezya mayake achikombelo.
Pesi wakabasandula wati kulimbabo, “Tamuzibwene pe zintu eezi zyoonse? Nkasimpe ndamwambila, takukwe ibbwe liyochala atala alimwi litakwe kuyobwalwa aansi.”
Nakachikkede atala lyechilundu cha Olivusi, basikwiiya bakamusikila kumbali bati, “twambile, ndilili nikuyochitika zintu eezi? Ninzi chiyoba chitondezyo chakuboola kwaako alimwi amamanino anyika?”
Jesu wakabasandula wati kulimbabo, “Amuchenjele kuti kutabi umwi umusowa.
Nkaambo kuyozwa bayingi muzina lyangu. Bayowaamba kuti, 'ndindime Kkilisito, álimwi bayosowa bantu bayingi.
'Muyomvwa nkondo azyaambo zyankondo. Amukalange kuti zitakamukatazyi pe, alimwi eezi zintu zyeelede zichitike; pesi mamanino katanakuba pe.
Nkambo inyika iyobukila nyikanyina, alimwi bwami abwaminyina. Kuyoba nzala alimwi amuzuzumina wenyika mumabazu asiyene siyene.
Pesi zintu ezi zyoonse matangunino biyo amachise amuntu sikutumbuka.
Elyo bayomutola kukwezegwa akuyomujaya. Muyosulwa enyika zyoonse akambo kezina lyangu.
Eelyo bantu bayingi bayobukilwa, alimwi akwaba umwi awumwi akusulana umwi awumwi.
Basinsiimi bayingi babeji bayoza akuzosowa bayingi.
Nkambo bupapi buyovula, luyando lwabayiongi luyotontola.
Pesi oyo uyokakatila kusikila kumamanino uyofutulwa.
Ayamakani mabotu abwami ayokawukwa munyika yoonse mbuli bukamboni kumanyika oonse. Eelyo mamanino ayosika.
“Lino, nimuzobona chisesemyo chisisidwe, chaakambwa a Daniyele musinsiimi, kayiimvwi mubusena busalala” ( ooyo ubala amvwisisisye).
Amuchite kuti aabo balimuJudiya bachijile kuzilundu,
ooyo uli achiluli changanda ataseluki aansi kuzobweza nikuba chimwi chintu chilimungánda,
alimwi amuchite ooyo ulimumuunda aleke kujokela kuzobweza chakusama chakwe.
Pesi maawe kubabo bamintide akuli baabo banyonsya bana mumazuba aayo!
Amukombe kuti kuchija kwenu kutakabi muchindi champeyo nikuba mubuzuba bwasabata.
Nkambo kuyoba mapenzi mapati loko, aayo atana kubonwa pe kuzwaida kumasangunino anyika kuzosikila lino, pe, takwe nikuzoba zili mbubobu pe.
Nakuti mazuba aayo pesi afwinsigwa, tekwali kunooba naba muntu walikuzofulwa. Pesi nkambo kabasale aayo mazuba ayofwinsigwa.
Lino kuti umwi muntu wamba kulindinywe kuti, 'Langa, ngoyu Kkilisito!'mutakamuzuminini pe akuzisyoma.
Nkambo baKkilisito bakubeja abasinsimi babeji bayosika akuchita malele mapati azigambyo, kuti baleesye, nikuba, aabo basale.
Amubone, ndamwambila kazitana kuchitika pe.
Lino kuti baamba kuti kulindinywe, 'Mulange, ulimunkanda, 'mutakayinki pe oko kunkanda. Nikuba kuti, 'mulange, mwali mungánda zyamukati, 'mutakasyomi pe.
Mbuli lulabi mbulumweka kuzwa kubuzwezuba alimwi lulamvwikkila koonse kusikila kububbila, oko kuyoba nkuboola kwa Mwana Muntu.
Oko kuli munyama ufwide, nkukubungene makubi.
Pesi mpawawo kwakumana mazuba amapenzi aya izuba liyosiya, mweezi tuchiko kuyopa mumuni pe, inyenyezi ziyoowa kuzwa kujulu, alimwi manguzu ejulu ayotikinisigwa.
Lino chitondezyo cha Mwan a Muntu chiyoboneka mujulu, alimwi misyobo yoonse iyolila. Bayomubona Mwana a Muntu kalikuza atala lyamayoba akujulu anguzu alimwi abulemu bupati.
Uyotuma baangelo bakwe akulila kwamweembo, alimwi bayobunganya antomwe basale bakwe kuzwa kumabazu aane, kuzwa kumpela imwi kuyosika kumpela yomwe yakujulu kusikila kuliimwi.
Amwiiye chiiyo kuzwa kumukuyu. Aawo mutabi nuuba muteete akusyuuka matu, ngamwaziba kuti mayiinza abafwifwi.
Lino zilikozyenie, naa mwabona zintu ezi zyoonse, mweelede kuziba kuti waba afwifwi, amulyango loko.
Nchobeni ndamwambila, izyalani eeli talikoyomana pe kazitanachitika pe zintu eezi.
Ijulu anyika ziyomana, pesi majwi aangu takwe natakamane pe.
Pesi takukwe uuzi buzuba nikuba chiindi niziyochitika eezi, nikuba baangelo bakujulu, nikuba Mwana a Muntu, pesi Taata alike.
Mbuli kumazuba a Nowa, mbukuyooba kubola kwa Mwana a Muntu.
Mbuli kumazuba kakutana boola zambangulwe bakali kulya alimwi akunywa, kabakwatana akukwatanisigwa kusikila kubuzuba Nowa mbwakanjila mubwato.,
alimwi takukwe anchibakalizi pe kusikila izambangulwe lyabatola - lino mbukuyoba kusika kwa Mwana a Muntu.
Eelyo bantu babili banoli mumuunda - umwi akati kabo uyobwezegwa, alimwi umwi uyosiigwa.
Banakazi babili banoli kabaziiya aziiyo - umwi akati kabo uyobwezegwa, alimwi umwi uyosiigwa.
Nkinkaako amuchenjele, nkambo tamuzi pe buzuba Mwami wenu nayoboola.
Pesi amuzizibe eezi, kuti kwanoli mwani ngánda walizi chindi akati kamansiku sikubba namusikila, walikuno lindide alimwi talikunoleka ngánda yakwe pe kuti itululwe.
Nkinkaako anywebo mulelede kulibambila, nkambo Mwana Muntu uyobola muchiindi nchimutalangilide pe.
“Lino nguuli mulanda usyomekede alimwi kalimusongo ooyo wakabikwa asimalelo wakwenkuti abaambe ngánda yakwe kuchitila kuti abape chakulya kuchiindi cheelede?
Uli achoolwe ooyo mulanda uyojanwa kachita oobo.
Nkasimpe, ndamwambila kuti simalelaakwe uyomubika kuti akabambe zintu zyoonse.
Pesi mulanda mubi kuti waamba eezi mumoyo wakwe, 'Simalelaangu wanonoka,
alimwi akatangune kuuma balanda bakwe, alimwi kulya akunywa azidakwa,
lino simalelaakwe ooyo mulanda uyosika mubuzuba ooyo mulanda mpatalibambilide pe alimwi achindi nchatazipe.
Simalelaakwe uzomugonkola goonkola akumwaaba kubusena kuti bakabe aamwi abasikuupawupa, ooko kuyoba kulila akuluma ntwino.
Lino bwami bwakujulu buyokozyanisigwa abasimbi balikkumi bakabweza malampi aabo alimwi bayinka kuyochinga simusa.
Balimusanu baabo bakali bafubafuba alimwi balimusanu bakali basongo.
Aawo basimbi bafubafuba nibakabweza malampi aabo, tebakabweza pe mafuta aabo.
Pesi basimbi basongo bakabweza mafuta aabo muzibikilo.
Lino simusa wakanonoka, boonse bakaguna alimwi bakoona.
Pesi akati kabusiku kwakamvwigwa ikongolola, Ámulange, simusa! Amuzwe aanze alimwi mukamuchinge akumutambula.
Éelyo basimbi boonse bakabuka alimwi bayasya malampi aabo.
Bafubafuba bakaamba kuti kubasongo, 'mutwabile amwi mafuta aanu nkambo malampi esu azima.'
'Pesi bo basongo bakasandula kuti, 'mbokunga takotukwanina swebo andinywe, amwinke kuli baabo basambala alimwi mukalyulile eenu nobeni.
Áawo nubakachili kukuyowula, simusa wakasika, alimwi aabo bakalibambilide bakayinka aawe kupobwe, alimwi imulyango wakajalwa.
“Kumane boobu bamwi basimbi abalabo bakaboola alimwi baamba kuti, “Simalelo wesu, Simalelo wesu, tujulile.'
“Pesi wakabasandula alimwi wakati, 'Nchobeni ndamwambila, tandimuzi pe.
Nkinkaako amuchenjele, nkambo tamulizi izuba nikuba ichindi.
“Zyakozyania amwalumi wakali afwifwi akuya munyika iimbi. Wakayita balanda bakwe alimwi wabaabila buvubi bwakwe.
Umwi wakamupa matalenta alimusanu, mpawo umwi wakamupa aabili, alimwi umbi lubo wakamupa limwi talenta. Umwi awumwi wakatambula eecho chendelana ambuli mbakonzya, mpawo mwalumi ooyo wakeenda mulweendo lwakwe.
Ooyo wakatambula matalenta alimusanu wakeenda wakubuka akwabelesya mpawo wakabbindawuka ambi alimusanu.
Mbuboobo, oyo wakatambwide aabili alakwe wakabbindawuka wajana aambi aabili.
Pesi oyo mulanda wakalalimwi wakeenda, wakusya kkomba mulubuwa, alimwi wakasisa mamali asimalelaakwe.
Lino mumazuba simalelo wabalanda aaba boonse wakaboola wazolangalanga myeelwe yabuvubi antomwe ambabo balanda bakwe.
Mulanda oyo wakatambwide matalenta alimusanu wakaboola alimwi weeta aambi alimusanu. Wakamba kuti, 'Simalelo wangu, Langa, ndakakubbindawuka aambi alimusanu.
“Simalelaakwe wakati kulinguwe, 'wakachita kabotu, iwe nomulanda mubotu alimwi usyomeka! Walikusyomeka muzintu ziche. Ndiyokubika kuti ukeendelezye zintu zyiingi. Njila mubusekelezi bwasimalelaako.'
“Ooyo mulanda wakatambwide matalenta aabili wakaboola waamba kuti, 'Simalelo wangu, wakandipa matallenta aabili. Langa, ndakabbindawuka aambi abili lubo.
“Simalelo wakwe wakati kuli nguwe, 'wakachita kabotu, iwe numulanda mubotu alimwi usyomeka! Walikusyomeka muzintu ziche. Ndiyokubika kuti ukeendelezye zintu zyiingi. Njila mubusekelezi bwasimalelo wako.'
“Eelyo oyo mulanda wakatambwide talenta lyomwe wakasika alakwe wati, 'Simalelo wangu, ndilikwizi kuti ulimwalumi ukalala. Ulatebula mpotabyalide, alimwi ulatebula mpotakwe niwamwaya.
Ndakayoowa, lino ndakeenda mpawo ndakusiisa talenta munyika. Langa ndeeli lyako ndabozya.
“Pesi Simalelaakwe wakamusandula wati kulinguwe, Íwe nomulanda mubi alimwi mutolo, wakaziba kuti ndilatebula aawo mpondatabyalape alimwi ndilatebula aawo mponditamwayide pe.
Nkiinkaako wakeelede kupa mamali kulibasikulondola, alimwi kukuyobola kwangu ndakati kunobweza aangu antoomwe ayaayo alikunozyalwa.
Nkiinkako amumubwezele talenta alimwi mulipe ooyo mulanda ulamatalenta alikkumi.
Mpawo kuli umwi awumwi weeta zyiingi uyopegwa, alimwi uyooba azyiingi. Pesi kuliyooyo utayeti chintu, uyonyanzigwa nikuba eecho nchajisi.
Mumubwale mumudima ooyo mulanda utakwe anchabede, omo mulikulila alimwi akuluma ntwino.'
“Eelyo Mwana a Muntu nayoboola mubulemu alimwi abaangelo bakwe boonse, uyokkala achuuno chakwe chabulemu.
Kuyobunganisigwa misyobo yoonse, alimwi uyopambula bantu umwi akulumwi, mbuli mwembeli mbwapambula imbelele kuzwa kumpongo.
Uyobika mbelele kuchilisyo chakwe, pesi mpongo kuchimweensi chakwe.
Eelyo Mwami uyowamba kuli zeezyo zitanoli kuchilisyo kuti, 'Muze, inywe nimulongezezegwe a Taata, amujane bwami oobo mbumwakabambilidwe kuzwa kumatalikilo anyika.
Nkaambo ndakali enzala alimwi mwakandipa chakulya.' ndakali enyota alimwi mwakandipa chakunywa.' ndakali mwenzu alimwi mwakandinjizya mungánda.'
ndakali chintanda alimwi mwakandisamika.' ndakali kuchiswa alimwi mwakandisilika.' ndakali mujele alimwi mwakandiswaya.'
Éelyo baluleme bayosandula alimwi kabati, 'Mwami, ndilili nitwakakubona koli enzala alimwi twakakusanina? Nikuba nyota alimwi twakakupa meenda?
Ndilili nitwakakubona koli mwenzu alimwi twakakutambula akukunjizya? Nikuba chintaanda alimwi twakakusamika?
Alimwi ndilili nitwakakubona kochiswa nikuba muntolongo alimwi twasika kulinduwe?'
“Eelyo Mwami uyosandula alimwi uyoti kuli mbaabo, 'Nchobeni ndamwambila, nzimwakachitila kumunini wabakwesu, mwakazichitila ndime.'
Eelyo uyoti kuli baabo batanoli kuchimweensi chakwe, 'Muzwe kuli ndime, inywe nimutukidwe, munjile mumulilo utamani ooyo ubambilidwe Satani abaangelo bakwe,
nkambo ndakali enzala, pesi temwakandipa pe chakulya; ndakali enyota, pesi temwakandipa pe meenda;
ndakali mweenzu, pesi temwakandinjizizye pe mungánda; ndakali chintanda, pesi temwakandisamika pe; ndakali kuchiswa alimwi nikuba nindakali muntolongo, pesi takwepe nchimwakayeeya andime.'
“Mpawo abalabo bayosandula alimwi kabati, 'Mwami ndilili nitwakakubona koli enzala, nikuba nyota, nikuba koli mwenzu, nikuba chintanda, nikuba kochiswa, nikuba koli muntolongo, alimwi twakaleka kukubelekela?'
“Eelyo uyobasandula kuti, 'Nchobeni ndamwambila, nzimwakatachitila abo banini babaaba, temwakazichita pe kulindime.'
Aaba bayonjila muchisubulo chitamani, pesi baluleme bayonjila mubuumi ibutamani.”
Lino chakaba kuti Jesu nakamana majwi aya oonse, wakati kuli basikwiya bakwe,
“Mulizi kuti kwayinda mazuba abili pobwe lyakwindilila ngalyasika, e; yo Mwana Muntu waabwa kuti akagankaminwe.”
Mpawo mupayizi mupati abapati bamwi babantu bakali bungene aantomwe mungánda yamuapyizi silutwe, wakalikutegwa ngu Kkayafasi.
Bakalangula inzila isisikene kabali antomwe kuti bamwange Jesu chakumubba akuyomujaya.
Nkambo bakali kwamba kuti, “kutabi chiindi chapobwe litakwe bumena, kuti kutabi kunyongana akati kabantu.”
Lino Jesu nakali mu Bbetani mungánda ya Sayimoni sichinsenda,
Nakalikulya atafula, elyo kwakasika mwanakazi wakajisi cinkuli wamafuta adula, elyo wakatila Jesu amutwe
Pesi basikwiya bakwe nibakaziba, bakabilila alimwi bakati,
“Ninzi chapa kuti aanyonyone obu? Ayaa alikuzigwa amali inyingi akuyopa bachete.”
Pesi Jesu nakaziba echi wakati kulimbabo, “Nkambonzi nimumukatazya mwanakazi ooyu? Nkambo wandichitila chintu chibotu.
Bachete mulaabo chiindi chonse, pesi tamukoyooba andime pe chindi choonse.
Nkambo mpatila mafuta aya amubili wangu, wazichitila kuzikwa kwangu
kasimpe ndamwambila kuti kufumbwa nkwayokambawukwa makani mabotu, munyika yoonse echi nchaachita mwanakazi oyu chinoyowambwa kuti bakamwibaluke.
Mpawo umwi wabali kkumi ababili, wakali kuteghwa Judasi sikaliyoti, wakayinka kumupayizi mupati
Alimwi wakati, “Ninzi nchimuyanda kundipa kuti ndimwabe kulindinywe?” Bakazuminana makumi ataatu ansiliva kuti bamupe.
Kuzwa kuleechochindi wakalangula mwenya wakumwaba kulimbabo.
Lino mubuzuba butaanzibwachinkwa chitakwe bumena basikwiya bakaza kuli Jesu akumwambila kuti, “Nkukuli nkoyanda kuti tukakubambilile kuti ukalye pobwe lyakwindilila?
Wakamba kuti, “Ngamwinke mumyuunzi kuli umwi mwalumi akumwambila kuti, “Muyisi wati, “chindi changu chaba mumaanza. Ndiyobamba ipobwe lyakwindilila kungánda yako abasikwiya bangu.
Basikwiya bakachita mbuli Jesu mbwakabalayilila, alimwi bakakubamba kulya kwapobwe lyakwindilila.
Lino nichakaba chindi chagoko, wakakkala aansi kuti alye abasikwiya balikkumi ababili.
Awo nibakali kulya, wakabambila kuti, “Nkasimpe ndamwambila kuti umwi wanu uyondaaba.”
Bakawusa kapati, elyo umwi wakatalika kumubuzya kuti, “Zyanchonzyo tendime na Mwami?”
Wakasandula kati, “Ngumwi oyo unika kuboko kwakwe andime mukabbavu ngonguwe uyondaaba.
Mwana Muntu uleenda, mbuli mbukulembedwe atala anguwe, pesi maawe kulooyo muntu uwaaba Mwana a Muntu! Chalikubota kuloyo muntu natakazyalwa.”
Judasi oyo wakali wakayanda kuyomuuzya wakati, “Ndime na, Mwami?” wakamwambila kuti, “walyambila olikke.”
Kabalimukulya, Jesu wakabweza chinkwa, wachilongezya, akuchikwamuna. Wakachipa basikwiya akubambila kuti, “Mubweze, mulye. Ooyu ngomubili wangu.”
Wakabweza nkomeki akulumba, alimwi wakabapa akwamba kuti, “Munywe, moonse.
Nkambo obumbulowa bwangu bwachizuminano butililwa bayingi kuti balekelelwe zibi.
Pesi ndimwambila kuti, tandi koyonywa limbi muchelo wamasansa, kusikila mubuzuba obo mbwintakanywe bupya andinywe mu Bwami bwa Taata.”
Lino nibakazwa kwimba lwiimbo, bakayinka kuchilundu chama oliva.
Mpawo Jesu wakabambila kuti, “moonse muyolebwa mansiku aano nkambo kandime, nkambo kuli lembedwe kuti, Ndiyowuma mwembeli alimwi butanga bwambelele buyomwayika.'
Pesi musule ndakubusigwa, ndiyomusangunina kuya mu Galili.”
Pesi Pita wakati kulinguwe, “Nekuba boonse balebwa nkambo kanduwe, mebo andike tandikoyolebwa pe.”
Jesu wakamwambila kuti, “chakasimpe ndakwambila kuti, busiku mbubobuno, mukombwe katana kukokolika, unoli wandikaka tutaatu.”
Pita wakamwambila kuti, “Nikuba kufwa anduwe ndilakonzya, nsikoyokukaka pe. “Boonse basikwiya bakamba chomwe.
Mpawo Jesu wakinkabo kubusena ibutegwa Gesemane alimwi wakati kuli basikwiiya bakwe, “Amukkale aano ninchiya kukukomba.”
Wakabweza Pita abana ba Zebbedi babili antoomwe anguwe alimwi bakatalika kuba amawuse aku katazika.
Mpawo wakati kuli mbabo, “Muuya wangu wawusa kapati, nikuba kusikila akulufu. Amuchale ano alimwi mulindile.”
Wakayinka anembo kulekule, wakakotamika busyu bwakwe, akukomba wakamba kuti, “Taata, na chakonzeka, nkomeki eyi ngindiinde. Pesi, kutabi kuyanda kwangu, pesi kube kuyanda kwako.
Wakaboola kuli basikwiya akubajanabalimukoona, alimwi wakati kuli Pita, “Niinzi, sa tamukonzyi kulindila andime hoola limwi?
Amulindile akukomba kuti mutanjilinmukusunkwa. Nchoonzyo Muuya ulayanda, pesi mubili wezuuka.”
Wakayinka lwachibili akuyokoomba. Wakamba kuti, “Taata, kuti echi tachikonzeki kwinda kumbali kwakuti ndinywe, kuyanda kwako kuchitwe.
Wakaza lubo wazobajana balikoona, nkambo meso aabo akali alema.
Wakabasiya lubo, wakayinka akuyokoomba kachitaatu, kayindulula majwi omwe.
Mpawo Jesu wakeza kuli basikwiya akubambila kuti, “Muchoona na akulyokezya? Amulange, hola lyaba mumaboko, alimwi Mwana Muntu waabwa mumaboko abasizibi
Mubuke, twinkeAmulange, oyo sikundaaba waba afwifwi.”
Nakachili kwambula, Judasi, umwi wabali kkumi awumwi, wakasika, wakaaza amakamu makamu abantu kuzwa kumupayizi mupati abapati babantu. Bakeza amafulo enkoli.
Lino oyo mwalumi wakali kuyanda kuuzya Jesu wakali bapede chitondezyo, chamba kuti, “oyo ngwensikamyonte ngonguwe. Mukamuvumpile.”
Mpawawo wakasika kuli Jesu akwamba kuti, “Wapona, Omuyisi!” akumumyonta.
Jesu wakamwambila kuti, “Mweenzuma, chita echo nchwazida kuzochita.” mpawo bakasika, babika maanza ali Jesu, akumuvuntila.
Amulange, umwi wababo bakali a Jesu wakatandabika janza lyakwe, wasomona kafulo, akuma muzike wamupayizi mupati, akumudyunkula kutwi kwakwe.
Mpawo Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Bwedezya kafulo kako muchibikilo chako, nkambo boonse abo babweza tufulo bayolobesegwa atufulo.
Muyeeye kuti tendali kukonzya na kwiita Taata, alimwi walikunditumina baangelo bayinda myuya mibi ilikkumi ayibili?
Pesi alikuyo zuzikizigwa biyeni malembe, “kuti echi chichitike?”
Kuleecho chindi Jesu wakati kumakamu abantu, “Mwaaza azifulo enkoli kuti muzondivuntile mbotatedi ndimubbi? Mazuba oonse ndakali kuyiisya mungánda ya Leza, alimwi tamwakandaanga pe.
Pesi zyoonse eezi zyachitika kuti malembe amusinsimi azuzikizigwe. “Mpawo basikwiya boonse bakamutakata akuchija.
Abo bakamuvuntila Jesu bakamutola kuli Kkayafasi muapayizi mupati, oko balembi abapati nkabakabungene.
Pesi Pita wakamutobelela kule kule kusikila mulubuwa lwamupayizi mupati. Wakanjila mukati akukkala aansi abasikulinda kuti abone chitachitike.
Lino mupayizi mupati abankuta boonse bakali kulangila bukamboni bwakubeja aatala a Jesu kuti bakonzye kumubika kulufu.
Takwepe nchibakajana, nekuba kuti bakamboni bakubeja bakeza. Pesi nichakaba chiindi babili bakasika.
Akwamba kuti, “Oyu mwalumi wakali kuti, 'Ndilakonzya kumwayula ngánda ya Leza akwiyakulula mumazuba ataatu.”
Mupayizi mupati wakimikila akumwambila kuti, “Tukwe nsandulo na?” Niinzi zyoonse eezi nzibalokukukwambila atala anduwe?”
Pesi Jesu wakawumuna. Mupayizi mupati wakamwambila kuti, “Ndakulayilila muli Leza upona, twambile na nduwe Kkilisito, Mwana a Leza.”
Jesu wakamuvwiila kati, “wamba nduwe omwini. Pesi ndakwambila, kuzwa lino uyoobona Mwan Muntu kakkede kukuboko kwachilisyo kwenguzu, akuyoboola mumayooba akujulu.”
Mpawo mupayizi mupati wakadelula zisamo zyakwe akwamba kuti, “wambula masampu! Nkambonzi nituchiyanda bukamboni? Amulange lino mwamvwa masampu.
Muyeyaanzi? Bakasandula akwamba kuti, “Welede lufu.”
Mpawo bakamuswida kumeso akumuuma, akumuvatula mabbayi,
akwamba kuti, “Tusinsimine, webo Kkilisito. Ngwani wakuuma?”
Lino Pita wakalikkede aanze mukati kalubbaya lwankuta, elyo mulanda musimbi wakasika kulinguwe akumwambila kuti, “wakalawe Jesu mu Galili.”
Pesi wakazikaka kunembo lyabo boonse kaamba kati, “tandizizi pe eezyo nzyolikwamba.”
Lino nakazwa anze amulyango walubaya, awumwi musimbi mulanda wakamubona akwambila abo mbakalabo, “Ooyu mwalumi wakali awe Jesu waku Nazaleta.”
Wakakaka lubo chakukonka, “tandimuzipe me mwalumi ooyu.”
Musule lyakayindi abo bakalimvwi bakasika akwamba kuti kuli Pita, “Nchamasimpe uli umwi wabo, nkambo nzila njowambula ayo ilakwamba.”
Mpawo wakatalika kutukila akukonka, “tandimuzi pe mwalumi oyu,” alimwi mpawawo mukombwe waka kokolika.
Pita wakayeeya majwi Jesu ngakaambide, “mukombwe katana kokolika uyonditama tutatu.” Mpawo wakaya aanze wakutalika kweema.
Lino nikwaba kuseni, boonse bapayizi bapati abapati babantu bakalangula inzila mbubanga balamubika kulufu Jesu.
Bakamwaanga, akumutola aanze, akumusisya kuli Payileti mwendelezi.
Mpawo Judasi, wakamuuzya, nakabona kuti Jesu wapegwa mulandu, wakasanduka akujosya mali yansiliva ili makumi atatu kubapayizi bapati akuzuluzi,
alimwi wakati ndabisya akwaaba bulowa butakwe mulandu. Pesi bakati, “Niinzi echo kulindiswe? Libonene olikke.”
Mpawo wakasowela aansi tumpanzi twansiliva mungánda ya Leza, akwinka, alimwi wakaya anze wakulisina.
Mupayizi mupati wakatubweza tupanzi twansiliva akwamba kuti, “tachili mumulawu pe kuti eechi chibikwe muchiyobwedo nkambo muulo wabulowa.”
Bakambuuzyania antoomwe, alimwi bakawula muunda wamubumbi muzikkilwa beenzu.
Nkambo kacheechi, oyo muunda wakategwa, “Muunda wabulowa.” kusika lino.
Mpawo echo chakambidwe amusinsimi Jelemiya chakazuzikizigwa, chaamba kuti, “Bakabweza tumpanzi tulimakumi ataatu twansiliva, muulo wakabamba abana ba Izilayeli,
alimwi bakawupa kuti muunda wamubumbi, mbuli Mwami mbakandilayilila.
Lino Jesu wakayimikila kunembo lyamwendelezi, alimwi mwendelezi wakamubuzya, “Uli Mwami waba -Juda na?” Jesu wakavwila kuti, “wamba mbubo.”
Pesi nakatamikizigwa amupayizi mupati abapati, takwepe nakasandula.
Mpawo Payileti wakamwambila kuti, “Sa totumvwide twambo ntubalo kukutamikizya?”
Pesi takwe nakasandula niliba ijwi lyomwe, awo mwendelezi wakagamba kapati.
Lino kupobwe mbuli bwakali mulawu wamwendelezi kuti bagwisye umwi mwaange wasaluzigwa abantu.
Kuchindi eecho kwakali mwaange wakale mpewo utegwa Bbalabbasi.
Lino nibakabungana antomwe Payileti wakabambila kuti, “ngwani ngumuyanda kuti ndimwangunwide? Bbalabbasi na Jesu utegwa ngu Kkilisito?”
Wakalizi kuti bapeda Jesu kulinguwe nkambo kakwemuzya.
Awo nakakkede achuuno chabbetekelo, mwanakazi wakwe wakamutumina ijwi elyo lyakati, “utachiti chintu kumwalumi oyo utakwe kaambo. Nkambo ndakatazigwa loko sunu nkambo kaziloto nzindalota atala anguwe.”
Lino bapayizi bapati abendelezi bakasungilizya makamu abantu kuti bakumbile Bbalabbasi, akupegwa Jesu kuti akajiigwe.
Mwendelezi wakababuzya kuti, “Nguuli akati kababili ngumuyanda kuti ndimwangunwide?” bakaamba kuti, “Bbalabbasi.”
Payileti wakababuzya kuti niinzi nchinjelede kuchitila Jesu utegwa ngu Kkilisito? Bakamuvwiila boonse bakati, Ngagankaminwe.”
Mpawo wakamba kuti, “Nkambonzi, mbubiinzi mbwaachita?” Pesi bakompololesya kapati, “Mumugankamine.”
Lino Payileti nakabona kuti takwe chintu nchakali wajana, pesi kuti kunyongana kwakali kwatalika, wakabweza maanzi wasamba maboko kunembo lyamakamu abantu, akubambila kuti, tandikwe pe mulandu kubulowa bwamwalumi oyu. Amulibonene lwenu.”
Boonse bantu bakati, “Mbubo bulowa bwakwe abube kulindiswe abana besu.”
Mpawo wakabaangunwida Bbalabbasi, pesi wakawuma Jesu achimboko akumupeda kulimbabo kuti akagankaminwe.
Mpawo basilumamba abeendelezi bakabweza Jesu akumutola mukati kangánda yabwendelelezi bapati akubungania nkamu mpati yoonse yabasilumamba.
Bakamuzwatununa akumusamika bbaki lisalalisya.
Bakaluka musini wamvwa akumuzwatika amutwe wakwe, akumubika mufunko kukuboko kwakwe kwalulyo. Bakafugama aansi kunembo lyakwe akumuniaka, kabamba kuti, “Mwalemekwa Mwami waba Juda!”
Bakamuswida mate, alimwi bakabweza mufunko akumuuma mumutwe kabalokwindulula.
Lino nibakamuniaka, bakamuzwatununa bbaki lyabo akumuzwatika zisamo zyakwe, akumutola kuyomugankamina.
Awo nibakazwa aanze, bakajana mwalumi uzwa ku Sayilini utegwa Sayimoni, ngubakaangila kuti beende aamwi kuti anyumpule chiingano chakwe.
Bakasika kubusena butegwa Gologota, kachamba kuti, “Mbusena bwatupepe twamitwe.”
Bakamupa wayini uvwelene andulwe kuti anywe. Pesi nakalabila wakakaka kunywa.
Lino nibaka mugankamina, bakabaana zyakusama zyakwe akuuma chisolo,
alimwi bakakkala ani kabali kumulinda.
Atala amutwe wakwe bakabikka bulembo bumubeteka, bwamba kuti, “Ooyu ngu Jesu Mwami waba Juda.”
Kwakali basikubba bobile mbakagankaminwa aabo, umwi kuchimweensi aumwi kuchilisyo chakwe.
Aabo bakali kwinda enzila bakali kumutukila, kabatikinia mitwe yabo
kabamba kuti, “Iwe nuyomwaya ngánda ya Leza akwiyakulula mumazuba ataatu, lifutule omwini! do kuli Mwan a Leza, seluka achingano aawo!”
Munzila ikozyenie abalabo bapayizi bapati bakali kumuniaka kabala balembi abapati kabamba kuti,
wakali kufutula bamwi, pesi we takonzyi pe kulifutula. Ngu Mwami wa Izilayeli. Ngaseluke aachingano, alimwi tuyomusyoma.
Wakali kusyoma Leza, Leza ngamuvune lino, na Leza kayanda kumwangununa. Nkaambo wakali kwamba kuti ndimwana a Leza.”
Munzila ikozyenie abalabo basikubba mbakagankamidwe aabo abalabo bakamutukila.
Lino kuzwa kuchindi chahola lamusanu alimwi mudima wakasikila nyika yoonse kuyosika kuhola lyamusanu aane.
Nichakaba chiindi chamusanu mwaane, Jesu wakoompolola ejwi pati kaamba kuti, Eli, Eli, lama, sabakkatani?” Kazyamba kuti, Leza wangu Leza wangu, nkambonzi niwandisiya?”
Lino abo bakiimvwi mpawo bakazimvwa, bakaamba kuti, “ulikwiita Elayija.”
Mpawo umwi wakachijana akuyobweza nsisa akwizuzya awayini ulwela, wakisekka kumufunko, elyo wakamupa kuti ayinywe
Bayingi boonse bakati, mumuleke alikke, Tumubone na Elayija uleza na kuzomufutula.”
Mpawo Jesu wakalila lubo ajwi pati elyo wakapa muuya wakwe.
Amubone, chisitilizyo changánda ya Leza chakanduka muzimpanzi zibili kuzwa kujulu kusika aansi, anyika yakandendema, amabwe akaanduka.
Tubanda twakavunuka, amibili yabasalali bakali boona yakabusigwa,
Bakazwa mutubanda musule lyakubuka kwakwe, bakanjila mugunzi lisalala, akuboneka kubayingi.
Lino silumamba mupati abaabo bakali kulinda Jesu bakawubona muzuzumo azintu zyakachitika, bakayoowa baamba kuti, “Chamasimpe ooyu wali Mwana a Leza.”
Banakazi biingi bakali batobela Jesu kuzwa ku Galili kuti bamukutawukile bakali kulanga alaale.
Akati kabo kwakali Meli Magadalini, Meli banyina ba Jemusi a Jozefa, abanyina babana ba Zebbedi.
Lino nilyakaba goko, kwakasika mwalumi uzwa ku Alimatiya, utegwa Jozefu, wakali sikwiiya wa Jesu.
Wakayinka kuli Payileti akuyokumbila mutunta wa Jesu. Mpawo Payileti wakalayilila kuti awupegwe.
Jozefu wakabweza mutunta, wamuzambilila mulembo utenteema,
wakulazika mukabanda kakwe kapya nkakali wafokola mubbwe. Mpawo waka kkunkulisya ibbwe pati wasinka amulyango wenda.
Meli Magadalini amumwi Meli bakaliwo, bakalikkede kulubazu lyakabanda.
Buzuba bwakatobela bwakali buzuba bwinda bwakulibambila, bapayizi bapati abaFalisi bakali bungene antomwe a Payileti.
Bakali kwamba kuti, “Mwami, tuchiyeeya ulya silweno nakachili kupona, wakaamba kuti, “kwinda mazuba ataatu ndiyobuka alubo.'
Nkinkaako layilila kuti kabanda kakwe kalindwe kusikila kubuzuba bwatatu. Chimwi chindi ulabona basikwiya bakwe basika bazomubba akwambila bantu, 'Kuti wabuka kuzwa kubafu.'Alweeno lwakumamanino ngalulayinda lwakusanguna.”
Payileti wakabambila kuti, “mwinke mukalinde mbuli mbumukonzya.”
Mpawo bakiinka akuyochita kuti kabanda kalindwe, bakazilulula abbwe akubikka basikulinda.
Lino niyakayinda isabata, kakuya kubuchedo mubuzuba butanzi bwamviki, Meli magadalini awumwi Meli bakaza kuzolanga chibunda.
Amulange, wakaba muzuzumo mupati wanyika, nkambo angelo wamwami wakaseluka kuzwa kujulu, wakaza akukunkulisya ibbwe, akukkala alindilyo.
Chiiwa chakwe chakali mbuli lulabi, azyakusama zyakwe zyakalikutuba mbuli buluba bwatonje.
Balindizi bakandengenda akuyowa alimwi bakaba mbuli bantu bafwide.
Mu angelo wakazibya banakazi akwamba kuti kulimbabo, “Mutayowi, ndilizi kuti mulangula Jesu, wakagankaminwa.
Tawope okuno, pesi wabuka, mbuli mbwaakamba. Amuze mubone abusena Mwami mpakalilazikidwe.
Mwinke chakufwambana alimwi mwambile basikwiiya bakwe, 'wabuka kuzwa kubafu. Amubone, ulikunembo lyanu kuyaku Galili. Ámulange, ndamwambila.”
Banakazi bakazwa mukabanda chakufwambana kabala akuyoowa akukondwa kupati, alimwi bakachijana kuyowambila basikwiya bakwe.
Amulange Jesu wakabaswania akubambila kuti, “Mwapona!” Banakazi bakaza, bajana mawulu akwe akumukomba.
Mpawo Jesu wakabambila kuti, “Mutayowi. Amwinke mwambile bakwesu kuti bayinke ku Galili. Nkuko nkubayondibonena.”
Lino awo banakazi nibakalikwenda, Amulange, bamwi babalindizi bakayinka mugunzi akuyowambila bapayizi bapati zintu zyoonse zyakachitika.
Lino bapayizi nibakaswanana abapati akuyooma aabo ikkani eeli, bakapa mali nyiingi kuli basilumamba
akubaambila kuti, “Mwambe kuti kuti bamwi, 'Basikwiiya ba Jesu basika mansiku akubba mutunta wakwe nitwachilikoona.
'kuti na makani aya asika kumwendelezi, tulamukombelezya akugwisya makatazyo alimulindinywe.”
Mpawo basilumamba bakabweza mali akuchita mbuli mbubakalayililwa. Aya makani akamwayika kapati akati kama Juda alimwi akeendelela anembo nikuba asunu.
Pesi basikwiiya ibalkkumi awumwi bakayinka ku Galilii, kuchilundu oko Jesu nkwakabalayilila.
Mpawo nibakamubona, bakamukomba, pesi bamwi bakadoneeka.
Jesu wakaza kuli mbabo akwaambula abo akuti, “Nguzu zyoonse ndakazipegwa kujulu aansi.
Aboobo amwinke alimwi mukachite basikwiiya bamisyoobo yoonse. Mukaba bbabbatizye muzina lya Taata, lya Mwana, alya Muuya Uusalala.
Mubayiisye kulemeka zintu zyoonse nzindakamulayilila, amubone, ndilandinywe chiindi choonse, nikuba kusikila kumamanino.”
Aya ngingawo matalikilo a makani mabotu a Jesu Kilisito, Mwana wa-Leza.
Mbuli mbukulembedwe kuli Isaya musinsimi, “Mulange, ndatuma mutumwa kunembo lyabusyu bwake oyo ulolulamika nzila yako.
Ijwi lya oyo uwompolola munkanda, “Mubambe inzila yaMwami; mululamike inzila yakwe”.
Joni wakasika, kabbizya munkanda alimwi kakambawuka lubbizyo lwakusanduka. Akulekelelwa izibi.
Ichisi choonse cha Judiya abantu boonse baku Jelusalemu bakayinka kulinguwe. Bakabbizigwa anguwe mumulonga utegwa Jodani, bakalyamba zibi zyabo.
Joni wakali kuzwaata zizwaato zyaboya bwankamela alukumba lwachikumba muchibuno chakwe, nkabela wakali kulya insozi abuchi bwalusaka.
Wakambula wati, “Oyu uza musule lyangu ulanguzu kwiinda ndime, lukole lwambatata zyakwe nsikwe chelelo chakukotama ansi akuzyangununa.
Ndamubbizya amanzi, asi we uyomubbizya a Muuya Usalala”.
Zyakachitika mumazuba ayo Jesu wakazwa ku Nazaleta ya Galili, alimwi wakabbizigwa a Joni mumulonga utegwa Jodani.
Kachizwa biyo Jeso mumanzi, wakabona ijulu kalyanzana akujulika
alimwi Muuya kuseluka akukkala atala anguwe mbuli nziba. Ijwi lyakazwa kujulu kalyamba kuti, “Ulimwana wangu. Ndiboteledwe kapati anduwe”.
Nkabela Muuya wakamusungilizya kuya munkanda.
Wakali munkanda mazuba makumi ane, kalokusunkwa aSatani. Wakali abanyama balusaka, alimwi bangelo bakamugwasizya.
Lino musule Joni kalimwangwa, Jesu wakasika muGalilaya kakambawuka makani mabotu aLeza. Wakamba kuti, “Ichindi chazuzikizigwa,
alimwi bwami bwaLeza bwaba afwifwi. Musanduke musyome makani mabotu”.
Nakalibwenda kumbali alwizi lwaGlili, wakabona Sayimoni a Andilaya muzyalwanyina wa Sayimoni kabawala kanyandi mulwizi, nkambo bakali bazubi babaswi.
Jesu wakabambila kuti, “Kamuzuba, munditobele, alimwi ndilomuchita bazubi babantu”.
Akufwambana bakasiya tunyandi twabo mpawo bamutobela.
Elyo Jesu nakachilikuyobweda kuya kunembo, wakabona Jakobo mwana wa Zebbediya amuzyalwanyina wakwe Joni; bakali mubwaato kabaluka tunyandi.
Wakabayita alimwi bakasiya wisi Zebbediya antoomwe ababelesi mubwaato mpawo bamutobela.
Lino bakasika kuKkapenawume, alimwi kabuli bunsi bwaSabata, Jesu wakanjila muchikombelo wakuyisya.
Bakagamba kunjisyo yakwe, nkambo wakali kuyisya mbuli muntu ulanguzu utali mbuli balembi pe.
Mpawo awo mwalumi wakali amuuya mubi wakakwiila muchikombelo, kati,
“Tulanzi anduwe, Jesu waNazaleta? Waza kuzotunyonyona na? Ndilikwizi kuti nduwe ni. Nduwe Usalala Mwana wa-Leza!”.
Jesu wakakalalila dayimona kati, “Tedi zwa alimwi uzwe mulinguwe!”
Idayimona lyakamuwalila ansi mpawo lyazwa mulinguwe akukwiila kupati.
Bantu boonse bakagamba, akubuzyanya, “Kuti ninzi eechi? Ninjisyo impya ilanguzu Ukonzya kutanda madayimona na amuswilizye”
Alimwi mpuwo yakwe yakazula muchisi choonse chaGalilaya.
Musule lyakuzwa muchikomelo, bakayinka kunganda yaSayimoni a Andilaya, kabali antoomwe a Jakobo a Joni.
Lino banyinazyala baSayimoni bakalikuchiswa intutumanzi, alimwi bakamwambila Jesu atala amukayintu oyu.
Wakaza wakamujata aluboko, wamubusya; intutumanzi yakazwa, mpawo watalika kubakutawukila.
Igolezya izuba kalili lyabbila, baketa kulinguwe boonse bachiswa abakanjidwe amadayimona.
Ibantu bamunzi boonse bakabungana amulyango.
Wakaponya boonse bakalamalwazi asiyene-siyene akutanda madayimona miingi, asi takazumizya madayimona kwambula nkambo akalimuzi.
Wakabuka kuseni, kakuchisiya; wakayinka kusisikene kuyokomba.
Sayimoni ababo bakali anguwe bakamuyandula.
Bakamujana bamwambila kabati, “Bantu boonse balokukuyandula”.
Wakabambila wati, “Ngatuye kumbi, anze kumadolopo alafwifwi, kuti ndikakambawuke akulako. Ncindazwide anze obu”.
Wakayinka kuGalilaya yoonse, kakambawuka muzikombelo zyabo akutanda madayimona.
Sichipele wakasika kulinguwe. Kumukumbila; wakafugama wamba wati, “Kuti kuyanda, ulakonzya kundisalazya”.
Wakazula luzyalo, Jesu wakatandabika kuboko kwakwe wamuguma, kamba kuti, “Ndilayand. Kopona”
Mpawo awo chipele chakayinka, mpo wasalazigwa.
Jesu wakamulayilila changuzu mpo wamuti yinka.
Wakamwambila kuti, “Ube asimpe lyakuti tubuzyi naba omwe muntu, asi kuya, ukalitondezye kumupayizi, ukapayilile nkambo kakusalazigwa kwako, mbuli Mozesi mbwakalayilila, mbuli bukamboni kuli mbabo”.
Asi wakiinka watalika kwaambula kangunukide kamwaya ijwi, zyakachitisya kuti Jesu takachili kukonzya kunjila idolopo kangunukide, asi wakakkala anze mumyunzi. Nikuba bobo bantu bakachili kusika kulinguwe kabazwa kumasena asiyene-siyene.
Nakabola kuKkapenawumi nikwakiinda mazuba mache kwakamvwika kuti Jesu mwali mumunzi.
Bantu bingi bakabungana kwakuti takwe nikwachili busena, munganda nikuba kumulyango, Jesu kali kukambawuka ijwi kuli mbabo.
Kwakasika balumi bakanyampwide mwalumi wakayuminide mubili; kanyampwidwe abalumi bone.
Nibakabula mweenya wakuswena afwifwi anguwe nkambo kakuvula kwabantu, bakavumbula kaluli awo Jesu mpakabede nibakavumbula bakaseluzya bulo bwawaka yuminide mubili mpakabede.
Nakabona kusyoma lwabo, Jesu wakati kuli wakayuminide mubili, “Omwana, zibi zyako zyalekelelwa”.
Lino bamwi balembi bakekkede, bakayeya munyono yabo,
“Nkambonzi mwalumi oyu nambula obu? Utuka Leza alikke?”
Chakufwambana Jesu wakaziba mumuya wkwe nzibakali kuyeya mumyoyo yabo. Wakati kulimbabo, “Nkambonzi nimulikuyeya ezi mumyoyo yanu?
Nchechili chuuba kwamba kuti kumulwazi, “Walekelelwa zibi, na kuti bweza bulo bwako weende?”
Asi kuti muzibe kuti Mwana aMuntu ulamanguzu ano ansi enyika kulekelela zibi, wakati kuliwakayuminide mubili
“Ndati kulinduwe nyampuka, bweza bulo bwako, uye kunganda yako”.
Wakanyampuka chakufwambana wabweza bulo, wakazwa munganda kunembo lyabantu boonse, abobo boonse bakagamba bapabulumbu kuli Leza, bati, “Ezi tatuna zibona pe”.
Wakayinka lubo kunkomwe yalwizi, makamu abantu akamutobela, mpawo wakabayiisya.
Kayabweenda, wakabona Levi mwana wa Alufayewusi kakkede mutente lyabasimutelo wakati kulinguwe, “Nditobele”. Wakanyampuka wamutobela.
Jesu wakali kulya munganda yaLevi, abasimutelo abasizibi bakali kulya awe abasikwiiya bakwe, kwakali biingi abobo bakamutobela.
Balembi, bakali baFalisi, nibakabona Jesu kalikulya abasizibi, bakati kuli basikwiiya bakwe, “Nkamboonzi nalya abasimutelo abasizibi?”
Jesu nakamvwa obo wakati kulimbabo, “Bantu baponede mumubili tabayandi musilisi; asi bachiswa, mbibayanda musilisi. Tendazida kwiita baluleme asi basizibi”.
Lino basikwiiya ba Joni abaFalisi kali kulyimya kulya. Bamwi bantu bakasika kulinguwe, “Nkambonzi basikwiiya baJoni abaFalisi balalyiima, asi bako tabalyimyi pe?”
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Nkujana basikutambwa kubwinga balyiimya na sibwiinga nkalabo?” Nkachilabo sibwiinga, tabalyimyi.
Ayosika mazuba sibwiinga akubwezegwa kuzwa kulimbabo, ayo mazuba bayolyiimya.
Takwe usuma chigamba chamulembo mupya achizwato chikulukulu, chigamba chilakonzya kudeluka, chipya kuzwa kuli chachiindi, chiyodelukisya.
Takwe ubikka wayini mupya munkomo yachiindi wabona wayini ulabbalula inkomo mpawo zyoonse wayini a ziyonyonyoka. Wayini mupya ubikwa munkomo mpya.
Musabata Jesu wakayinda mumunda wamayila, basikwiiya bakabweza mayila.
Mpawo baFalisi bakati kulinguwe, “Langa nkambonzi basikwiiya nibalikuchita zintu zityola mulawo abuzuba bwaSabata?”
Wakati kulimbabo, “Temwakabala na kuti Davida nakabula akuba anzala - we abalumi mbakalabo -
mbakanjila munganda yaJehova Abbiyata nkali mupatiyizi mupati, akulya chinkwa chabukamu, chitazumizigwi kuligwa amuntu kupela kunze kwabapayizi, wakapa abalabo mbakalabo?”
Jesu wakati, “Sabata lyakalengelwa bantu, pepe bantu kulengelwa Sabata.
Aboobo, Mwana aMuntu Mwami, ku Sabata”.
Jesu wakanjila lubo muchikombelo, wakajana mwaalumi wakakokonyene kuboko.
Bantu biingi bakamulangisisya kuyanda kubona kuti ulamuponisya na mubuzuba bwa Sabata bamupe mulandu.
Jesu wakaambila mwaalumi wakakokonyene kuboko kuti, “Nyampuka uyimikile aakati kabantu aaba.”
Mpawo wakati kubantu, “Ncheechili chibotu, kuchita chibotu na chibi mubuzuba bwa Sabata; kuvuna buumi na kujaya?” Pesi bakawumuna.
Wakabalanga chakunyema, alimwi kawuside, nkaambo kakuyuma kwamyoyo yabo, wakati kumwaalumi ooyo, “Tandabika kuboko kwako. ” Mpawo wakatandabika, elyo kuboko kwakwe kwakaba kabotu.
Lino ba Falisi bakazwa aanze mpawo, antoomwe aba Heloda bakatanguna kulanguula nzila mbubanga balamujaya.
Mpawo Jesu, wakasosoloka abasikwiiya bakwe baya kulwizi, elyo makamu makamu abantu kuzwa kuGalilii, aku Judiya akabatobela.
Lino nibakamvwa nzyakali kuchita, bantu bayingi bakeza kuli nguwe kuzwa ku Jelusalema, Idumiya azisi zilimutala a Jodani azyeengelede Taya a Sidoni.
Nkaambo kamakamu aabantu wakaambila basikwiiya bakwe kuti bamubambile bwaato buniini afwiifwi, kuti akonzye kusosoloka aakati kabantu.
Nkaambo wakalikusilika bayingi, aboobo bakali aamalwazi balikuchundana kabaya kunembo kuti bamugume.
Kufumbwa myuuya mibi niyakamubona yakawida aansi kunembo lyakwe akoompolola, kuti, “Nduwe Mwana wa Leza. ”
Alimwi wakayilayila changuzu kuti itamudomboli kuti ngwani.
Wakatanta achilundu akwiita aabo mbakalikuyanda, alimwi bakeza kulinguwe.
Wakasaluuzya balikkumi ababili; (aabo mbakati mmbatumwa) kuti bakabe aamwi anguwe, alimwi kuti akabatume kukukambawuka,
akubapa ngunzu, zyakutanda myuuya mibi.
Aaba mbimbabo bali kkumi ababili mbakasaluuzya: Sayimoni, oyu wakamupa zina lyakuti ngu Pita;
Jemusi mwana wa Zebbediya, aJoni mwana wakwabo wa Jemusi, aba wakabawuzika kuti mba Bbowanejesi, nkukwamba kuti bana ba ndabi;
Andulo, Filipo, Bbatolomiya, Matayo, Tomasi, Jemusi mwana wa Alifasi, Tediyasi, a Sayimoni munkutwe
a Judasi Sikkaliyoti, nguwe wakazomuuzya.
Mpawo wakabweeda kumuunzi, alimwi makamu aabantu akamubunganina, aboobo basikwiiya bakwe anguwe tebakachili kujana chiindi chakulya pe.
Lino bang'anda yakwabo nibakamvwa zyalikuchitika, bakamulanguula, kabaamba kuti “Wapenga. ”
Balembi bakazwa kuJelusalema bakaamba kuti, “Unjidwe muuya mubi utegwa Bbelizabbeli,” akuti “Alimwi nguzu nzyatanzya myuuya mibi nzizyakwe Bbelizabbeli mwami wamyuuya mibi.”
Jesu wakabayita mpawo watanguna kwaambula ambabo muzikozyanio, “Satani ulakonzya biyeni kulitanda?
Na bwaami kabupambukene, bwaami oobo tabukonzyi kwiimikila.
Alimwi na tekwaba kumwvanana mung'anda, eeyo ng'anda tikonzyi kwiimikila.
Alimwi na Satani walikazya elyo kanzeene, takonzyi kwiimikila; nkokuti mamanino aakwe asika.
Pesi taakwe muntu ukonzya kunjila mung'anda yamwaalumi singuzu kuti abbe lubono lwakwe, atatanguna kumuzunda akumwaanga ooyo mwaalumi singuzu. Awo mpanga ulakonzya kubba lubono mung'anda eeyo.
Ndamwaambila kasimpe, zyoonse zibi akusampawula kwabantu kulalekelelwa,
pesi kufumbwa muntu usampawula Muuya Uusalala takonzyi kulekelelwa; ulaamulandu wachibi chitamani. ”
Jesu wakabaambila eezi, nkaambo bakalikwaamba kuti, “Ulaa muuya mubi.”
Mpawo banyina abakwabo bakasika. Kabayimvwi aanze, bakatuma umwi kuti amwiite.
Bantu bayingi bakalikkede kabamubunganide, alimwi bakamwaambila kuti, “Banyoko abanike bako balaanze baliikukulanguula.”
Wakabasandula wati, “Baama abakwesu mbaani? ”
Lino wakalanga aabo bakakkede kabamuzyungulukide wati, “Bakwesu abaama mbaaba!
Kufumbwa uuchita kuyanda kwaLeza nguumukwesu wangu abaama.”
Alimwi Jesu wakatalika kuyiisya kali kumbali aalwizi. Inkamu yabantu bakamuzyungulukide yakali mpati loko zyakuti wakanjila mubwaato, kuchitila kuti akonzye kusosolokela mumaanzi akukkala, bantu boonse bakalitobezezye lwizi kunkomwe.
Mpawo wakabayiisya zintu zyiingi kabelesya zikozyanio, alimwi mukuyiisya kwakwe wakati,
“Amuswiilizye, mulimi wakaya kukumiza mbuto yakwe.
Awo naakali kumiza mbuto, imwi yakawida munzila, mpawo tuyuni twakasika twiilya.
Imwi yakawida amwaala, aatakwe muse mwiingi. Yakamena kufwambaana, nkaambo muse wakali muche.
Pesi zuba nilyakabala yakapya, mpawo yakayuma nkaambo kamiyanda yakatabbide.
Imwi mbuto yakawida mumaamvwa, maamvwa akakomena asyanikizya matu aayo, aboobo teeyakakonzya kuzyala.
Imwi mbuto yakawida mumuse uvubide. Yakamena, akukomena mane yazyala michelo, imwi makkumi otatwe, imwi makkumi musanu alimwi, imwi mwaanda. ”
Lino wakati, “Ooyo ulaamatwi aakumvwa, ngamvwe.”
Lino Jesu naakaba alike, mbakali aabo antoomwe abasikwiiya bakwe balikkumi ababili bakamubuzya aatala azikozyanisyo eezyo.
Wakabaambila wati, “Insiswa ya bwami bwa Leza ilipedwe kuli ndinywe. Pesi kuli bamwi biyo bali kunze, zyoonse zyaambwa muzikozyanisyo,
kuchitila kuti, lyoonse kababona pesi kabatabonesesyi, alimwi kabamvwa lyoonse, pesi kabatamvwisisisyi; kansinga balikumvwa balikunosanduka kabalekelelwa zibi zyabo.”
Lino wakati kuli mbabo, “Ani sena tamulokumvwisisisya na chikozyanisyo eechi? Na kakuli boobo nga kulakonzeka biyeni kuti mumvwisisisye zimwi zikozyanisyo?
Mulimi uumiza mbuto nguwe uumiza jwi.
Bamwi bantu bali mbuli nzila, aawo mpulimizidwe jwi. Mpawo mbubalimvwa biyo, Satani wasika wabweza jwi lyali lyamizwa muli mbabo.
Bamwi, mbuli muse ulaamwaala mpuyakamizwa mbuto, balalimvwa jwi, mpawo, akufwambaana balalitambula chakubotelwa.
Pesi nkaambo tabajisi miyanda ibbide, balajata kwachiindi chiniini biyo. Nikwasika mapenzi nikuba kusyonsegwa nkaambo kajwi, balafwambaana kuwa.
Alubo bamwi, mbuli muse ulaamaamvwa muyakamizwa mbuto, balalimvwa jwi,
pesi masukusyo aanyika, kweenwa aabuvubi aziyandisyo zyazimwi zintu zyabuyo zilasika zyasyanikizya jwi, zyachita kuti litabi aamichelo.
Bamwi, mbuli muse uuvubide muyakabyalwa mbuto, balalimvwa jwi, balitambula, akuzyala michelo imwi makkumi otatwe, imwi makkumi musanu alimwi, imwi kusika mwaanda.”
Jesu wakati kuli mbabo, “Sena nga mweeta lambi kuti mulitibbike alusuwo, na kulibika muchinkuma chabulo? Ani nga tamulibiki atala aachibikilo chalyo na?
Nkaambo zintu zyoonse zisisidwe ziyooyubununwa, alimwi choonse chitibbikidwe chiyotibbulwa.
Kufumbwa ulamatwi akumvwa ngamvwe.”
Wakaya kunembo akubaambila kuti, “Amuchenjele loko nzimumvwa. Cheelesyo nchimubelesya anywebo muyoyelesegwa anchicho, nikuba kwindilila kulindinywe.
Nkaambo kufumbwa uujisi uyoopegwa zyiingi. Ooyo uutajisi, niziba nzyalaazyo uyoonyanzigwa.”
Alimwi wakati, “Mbobubede oobu bwami bwa Leza mbuli muntu uumiza mbuto aansi.
Mpawo uloona mansiku akubuka nibwacha, pesi mbuto ilamena akukomena, nikuba kuti tazi mbozichitika.
Muse awulike: ulamezya nseke zyamayila kusaanguna munsonga, kakutobela miyungi, mane miyungi yatuba.
Mayila mbaatuba biyo, ulabelesya chakunenzya, nkaambo chiindi chakutebula chasika.”
Alimwi wakati, “Sena niinzi nchitujnga tulachikozyanisya abwami bwa Leza, nakuti tubelesye chikozyanisyoonzi kubupandulula?
Buli mbuuli mbuto itegwa musitada, ni mbuto ndiini loko njobyala aansi.
Pesi niyabyalwa, ilakomena kwiinda zilimwa zyoonse zyamumuunda, kilaamitabi mipati izyakuti tuyuni tulakonzya kukala mumweenzule wayo.”
Jesu wakabaambila jwi kabelesya zikozyanisyo zyiingi mbuuli mbubalikumvwa,
mpawo taakwe nchaakabaambila pe katabelesezye chikozyanisyo. Pesi nakaba alike abasikwiiya bakwe, wakapandulula zyoonse.
Oobo buzuba, nilyakaba goko, wakati kuli mbabo, “Atuzubuke tuye mutala. ”
Bakasiya makamu makamu aabantu musule, bakamutobela, mubwaato mwakabede Jesu. Amwi maato akaliwo aalawo akamutobela.
Mbubakendeenda biyo kwakawunga guwo pati, alimwi mayuwe akalikukupila maanzi mubwaato, mane bwaato bwakasizule.
Jesu wakalilede kasegede musego, kusule mubwaato. Basikwiiya bakamubusya alimwi bakati kuli nguwe, “Omuyiisyi, sena tokwe nolikataazya nikuba kuti twaamba kufwa? ”
Wakabuka, wakalayilila guwo, alimwi wakati kumayuwe, “Umuna! Batama! ” Mpawo guwo lyakuumuna, mayuwe akayosa, kuumuna kuti zii!
Wakati kuli basikwiiya bakwe, “Nkamboonzi nimuyoowa boobu? Sena ambuli sunu tamunaba lusyomo na? ”
Bakayoowa loko alimwi bakabuzyania bati, “Ani ngwani ooyu, nkaambo guwo amayuwe zilamumvwa akumuswiilila?”
Bakazubuka lwizi baya kuchisi cha Jelasenesi.
Mpawaawo Jesu nakazwa mubwaato, mwaalumi wakanjidwe muuya mubi kazwa kuzibunda wakaza kuli nguwe.
Ooyu mwaalumi wakali kukkala kumawumbwe, alimwi katakwe naba umwi wakachili kukonzya kumwaanga, nikuba kuti wabelesya nsimbi.
Nkaambo chiindi chiingi wakanoonga waangwa nsimbi kumaboko akumawulu, pesi wakanoonga wazipasuula akutyola zyoonse nzyakanoonga waangwa aazyo. Takwe naba umwi wakali anguzu zyakumuzunda
Chiindi choonse sikati amansiku wakali kukwiila kumawumbwe amuzilundu akulichubbulula amabwe.
Lino naakabona Jesu kulekule, wakachijaana wakuwa bufugeme munsi lyamawulu aakwe, kunembo lyakwe.
Wakoompolola ajwi pati wati, “Uyaandanzi kulindime Jesu, Mwana wa Leza Mupati Kampatila? Ndakumbila muzina lya Leza kuti utandipenzyi pe! ”
Nkaambo Jesu wakali wati kuli nguwe, “Zwaa mumwaalumi oyu iwe nomuuya mubi!”
Lino Jesu wakabuzya kuti, “Nduweni izina lyako? ” Wakasandula wati, “Izina lyangu ndime Ligiyoni, nkaambo tulibayiingi. ”
Wakakombelezya Jesu kuti atabatandi pe kuzwa mubusena oobo.
Kwakali butanga bupati bwangulube bwakali kuchela aakalundu kali afwiifwi,
myuuya mibi yakakombelezya Jesu yati, “Tutandile mungulube; utuzumizye kuti tunjile mulinzizyo. ”
Wakayizumizya, elyo myuuya mibi yakazwa yaakunjila mungulube. Mweelwe uli zyuulu zibili wabutanga bwa ngulube zyakagwilimina kujenga zyaaliwalila mulwizi zyanikila
Aabo bakali kweembela ngulube bakachijanina kuyowaamba kudolopo amumyuunzi, lino bantu bakayinka kuyobona chakali chachitika.
Lino nibakasika kuli Jesu, bakamubona mwaalumi wakanjidwe ligiyoni wamyuuya mibi. Wakalikkede, kasamide, amizeezo yakwe yakali yaba kabotu. Eelyo bakayoowa.
Abo bakazibona bakaambila bantu azyakachitika kuli ooyu mwaalumi wakanjidwe muuya mubi, bakapandulula azyakachitika kungulube.
Mpawo bantu bakatanguna kumukombelezya Jesu kuti azwe muchisi chabo.
Lino Jesu nakaanjila mubwaato, mwaalumi wakanjidwe muuya mubi wakamukumbila kuti beende amwi.
Jesu wakamukakila, pesi wakati, “Kuya kumuunzi kuli bakulindinywe ukabaambile Mwami nzyaakuchitila, ambaakufwida luzyalo. ”
Eelyo mwaalumi ooyu wakeenda wakwaambila baku Dekkapolisi nzyakamuchitila Jesu. Mpawo bantu boonse bakagamba.
Lino Jesu naakazubuka lubo abwaato kuya mutala alwizi, bantu bayingi bakamubunganina kali kunkomwe yalwizi.
Lino umwi mweendelezi wachikombelo utegwa Jayilosi, wakaya nkukooko. Naakabona Jesu, wakawida kumawulu aakwe.
Mpawo wakamukombelezya chamoyo woonse wati, “Mwanaangu musimbi waamba kufwa, wenche kuza umubike maboko, ulasilikwa apone. ” Lino Jesu wakeenda awe.
Bantu bayiingi bakamutobela bamubunganina bamubika aakati.
Mpawo awo kwakali mwanakazi wakali kuchiswa kalobola kwaminyaka ilikkumi ayibili.
Wakafwaba kapati loko mukusilikwa abasilisi bayingi, alubo wakamana lubono lwake loonse. Nikuba boobo taakwe nakapona pe, bulwazi bwakayindilila.
Kali wamvwa impuwo zya Jesu, wakasika wanjila munkamu kusule lya Jesu wajata chisamo chakwe.
Nkaambo wakayeeya kuti, “Kufumbwa ndaguma chisamo chakwe ndilapona. ”
Mpawo awo bulowa bwakagama, alimwi wakamvwa mumubili wakwe kuti wapona bulwazi bwakwe.
Mpawo awo Jesu wakamvwa kuti nguzu zyamana mumubil wakwe. Wakachebukila musule wabuzya wati, “ani ngwani waguma chisamo changu? ”
Basikwiiya bakwe bakasandula bati, nga ulabuzya biyeni kuti, “ngwani wandiguma? ” Kubwene bantu bayiingi balikubunganidile bakubikkide akati.
Pesi Jesu wakachiliswini kalanguula oyo wakamuguma.
Lino mwanakazi olya mbwakalizi zyoonse zyakachitika alinguwe, wakaza kuli Jesu wawa kumawulu akwe, kazazama mukuyoowa, wamwaambila choonzyo chakachitika.
Lino wakamwaambila kuti, “Mwanaangu lusyomo lwako lwakuponia. Kuya muluumuno, waangunuke kuzwa mumafwabi ako.”
Lino Jesu kachaambula, kwakasika bamwi bantu bakazwa kung'anda yaJayilosi Muzulwidi wambungano bati, “uchimukatazizyaanzi Muyiisi, ” teemwanaako musimbi wafwa kale?.”
Jesu tatambwide pe ezizyakali kwaambuulwa, wakaambila Jayilosi kuti, “Syoma utayoowi pe. ”
Wakeenda aPita, Jemusi aJoni mukulana waJemusi, tewakazumizya bantu bayiingi pe.
Lino nibakasika kung'anda yamweendelezi wachikombelo, Jesu wakabona kunyongana, akuchundaana kwabantu balila akomooka kupati.
Mpawo wakanjila mukati wabaambila kuti, “Nkaambonzi nimunyongana akoomoka, Mwana tafwide pe uledebiyo? ”
Mpawo bakamuseka. Lino naakamana kubatandila anze boonse, wakabweza wisi amusimbi abanyina abasikwiiya mbakali abo, wanjila omo mwakali mwana.
Wakajata luboko lwamusimbi wamwaambila kuti, “Talita kkumi! ” (chaamba kuti, kasimbi buka! ”)
Mpawo awo musimbi wakanyampuka, weendeenda (wakali aminyaka ilikkumi ayibili). Alizeezi, bantu bakagambwa loko.
Wakabaambila malayilile mayumu akuti bataambili muntu atala azyakachitika, mpawo wakati amumupe chakulya.
Wakazwa awo mpawo waya ku chisi chakulimbabo, mpawo basikwiiya bakwe bakamutobela.
Lino buzuba bwa Sabata nibwakasika, wakatalika kuyiisya muchikombelo. Bantu bayiingi bakamumvwa kayiisya bakagamba. Bakabuzya kuti, “Ooyu mwaalumi wakazijana kuli njiisyo eez? i” “Mbusongoonzi mbwapedwe?” “Maleele alibuti aaya ngachita amaanza aakwe?”
“Ooyu teensi nguwena mubezi mwana wa Meli? Mwana wakwabo waJemusi, Josefa, Judasi aSayimoni? Bachizi bakwe teensi mbabo aaba mbitulabo na? Mpawo bakamubijilwa Jesu.
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Musinsimi tajani bulemu pe, kunze kwamuchisi, amung'anda mwazyalwa aakati kabasinzubo zyakwe. ”
Tewakakonzya pe kuchita malele, kunze kwakukumbila biyo bachiswa akubabikka maboko akubasilika.
Alimwi kutasyoma kwabo kwakamugambya. Wakeendeenda mugunzi eelyo kayabuyiisya.
Mpawo wakayita bali kkumi ababili wabatuma babili babili akubapa nguzu zyakuzunda myuuya mibi,
mpawo wakabaambila kuti tababwezi chintu mulweendo lwabo kunze, chakulya niiba nkomwe niiba mali mumikumba yanu kunze amufunko,
pesi basame nsangu pesi batabwezi zisamo zimbi.
Mpawo wakati kuibabo, “Nimuyoonjila mumuunzi mukkale mumo omo lumwi do mukazwe mugunzi eelyo.
Na kulibusena nkubakaka kumutambula nikuba kumuswiilizya, nimuyozwa mubusena oobo, mukasansamune lusuko kumawulu anu bukabe bukamboni atala lyambabo.”
Bakazwa baya kukukambawuka kuti bantu basanduke.
Bakaanda myuuya mibi miingi mpawo bakananika bachiswa bayiingi amafuta alimwi bakapona.
Mwami Helodi wakazimvwa eezi, nkaambo zina lya Mwami Jesu lyakali lyazibikana loko. Bamwi bakati, “Amwi ngu Joni Mubbabbatizyi wabusigwa kuzwa kubafu, nkikaako nguzu zyamalele nzizilikubeleka mulinguwe. ”
Bamwi bakati, “Ngu Elayija”. Alimwi bamwi bakati, “Musinsimi, nguumwi wabasinsimi bachiindi.”
Pesi Helodi naakamvwa obu wakati, “Joni mwaalumi oolya ngundakadunsula mutwe wakabusigwa kuzwa kubafu. ”
Nkaambo Helodi lwake ngwakali wapa nguzu kuti Joni aangwe, alimwi wakaangwa akubikwa muntolongo nkaambo ka Helodiyasi (muka Filipi mwanana wakwabo) ngwakali wakwata.
Nkaambo Joni wakanoonga waambila Helodi kuti, “Tachili chibotu kuti ukwate mukayintu wamwana wakwenu. ”
Lino Helodiyasi wakalijisi mfwindilili yakuyanda kujeya Joni, pesi tewakakonzya pe,
nkaambo Helodi wakali kumuyoowa Joni; wakalimwizi kuti muntu ululeme kali musalali, aboobo wakali kumutabilila. kumuswiilila kwakalikumunyongania loko, pesi wakalikumumvwa chiindi choonse kawangunukide.
Lino mweenya wakaba awo Helodi naakachita pobwe lyakuzyalwa kwakwe mpawo wakachita pobwe pati kachitila bapati abasilumamba bakwe, abeendelezi bapati bamu Galili.
Mpawo mwana musimbi waHelodiyasi nakasika wazyana, zyakabotezya Helodi abeenzu bakatambidwe kupobwe. Lino Mwami wakati kumusimbi, “Ndikumbile kufumbwa nchuyanda, ndilakupa.”
Mpawo wakamusyomezya achikonke wati, “Kufumbwa nchuyokumbila nichiba chipanzi cha bwami bwangu, ndilakupa. ”
Wakazwa waya kuli banyina wakwaamba kuti, “Ngandilakumbilaanzi? ” Banyina bakati, “Mutwe wa Joni Mubbabbatizyi”
Mpawo aawo wakanjila akufwabaana kuMwami achikumbilo chakwe wakwaamba wati: “Ndiyanda kuti lino, undipe mutwe waJoni Mubbabbatizya mukasuwo.”
Nikuba kuti eechi chakamuchisa loko mwami, pesi nkaambo kachikonke achikumbizyo, antoomwe abeenzu bakwe taakayanda kumukakila pe.
Mpawo wakafwambaana kutuma silumamba kuti akeete mutwe waJoni. Lino wakeenda wakudunsula mutwe waJoni muntolongo,
mpawo wawuleta mukasuwo wamupa musimbi oyo, mpawo musimbi, wakatola kuli banyina.
Nibakamvwa oobo, basikwiiya baJoni bakaza kuzobweza mutumba akuubaamba muchibunda.
Mmpawo baTumwa, bakamubunganina Jesu, bamwaambila zyoonse nzibakachita akuyiisya.
Lino nkaambo kakuti bantu bayiingi bakalikuza kabeenda kabatakwe nibajana chiindi chakuti balye, wakati kulimbabo, “Muzide okuno kusitikide mulyookezye. ”
Bakeenda muli chabochabo mubwaato bazubuka baya kutakwe bantu pe.
Lino bamwi bakababona nibakazubuka bakabaziba mpawo bakeenda amawulu kuzwa mumyuunzi yoonse bakubatangunina kusika.
Lino nibakasika kuchito Jesu wakabona makamu makamu abantu, wakabafwida luzyalo, nkaambo bakali mbuli mbelele zitakwe mweembeli. Mpawo wakatanguna kubayiisya zintu zyiingi.
Lino muchiindi eechi lyakali lyaba goko, basikwiiya bakwe bakaza kuli nguwe bakati, “Okuno nkubusena butakwe chintu, alubo chiindi chamana.
Baande bantu aba baye mumyuunzi izyungulukide munyika oomu bakalyulile chakulya.”
Pesi wakabasandula wati, “Mubape chakulya ndinywe. ” Bakati kuli nguwe, “Nga tulayinka na tukawule mikamu yachinkwa yiita myaanda yobile yama denari kuti tubape balye?”
Wakababuzya wati, “Mujisi zinkwa zingane? Mwiinke mukalange. ” Nibakalanguula bakati, “Tujisi zinkwa zili musanu abaswi babili.”
Wakabalayilila kuti baambile bantu boonse kuti bakkale muzibumga zibumga abwizu butete.
Mpawo bakakkala ansi muzibunga; muzibunga zyamyaanda azya makumi musanu.
Wakabweza zinkwa zili musanu abaswi babili, mpawo wakalanga kujulu, wakapa kulumba elyo wakakwamuna zinkwa mpawo wazipa kuli baikwiiya kuti bape bantu. wakakwamuna baswi babili mpawo wabapa boonse.
Bakalya boonse bakkuta.
Bakabwezelela bufwefwelenga bwazinkwa, abaswi bwakachala bazuzya zisuwo zili kkumi azibili.
Imweelwe wabaluumi bakalya wakali kusika kuzyuulu zili musanu.
Mpawaawo wakaambila basikwiiya bakwe kuti banjile mubwaato bazulule baye mutala, ku Betisayida, wakaambila bantu kuti bamwayike.
Nibakeenda, wakaya kuchilundu kuti akakombe.
Lino nilyakaba goko, bwaato bwakali akati kalwizi, we wakachaala alikke kunze.
Wakabona kuti kuti balokuzundaana aluuwo, nkaambo luuwo lwakabalwanisya. Achiindi chamansiku wakeenda atala ameenda, kaya kuli mbabo. Wakali wamba kubayinda kumbali.
Pesi nibakamubona keenda atala alwizi, bakayeeyanga ncheelo, bakoomba,
nkaambo boonse nibakamubona bakayoowa. Mpawo awo wakabaambuuzya wati, “Mujate moyo! Ndime. Mutayoowipe!”
Elyo wakatanta mubwaaato ambabo, mpawo luuwo lwakamana. Bakagambwa loko,
mbokunga tebakamvwisisisya pe atala azinkwa; myoyo yabo yakayumisigwa.
Lino nibakazubukila mutala, bakasika ku Jenesaleti bakaanga bwaato kunkomwe yalwizi.
Kabachizwa biyo mubwaato bantu batalika kumuziba Jesu.
Bakachijaana chisi choonse alimwi bakabweza bachiswa amalo akubatola oko kufumbwa nkubakamvwa kuti nkwabede.
Lino kufumbwa kumyuunzi nkwakaya, kumadolopo naanka kumabazu anyika bakalikubikka bachiswa muzisambalilo. Bakamukumbila kuti bajate chisamo chakwe, abaabo bakajata bakaponesegwa.
BaFalisi abamwi bayiisyi bamulawu bakali bazwa ku Jelusalema bakamubunganina
Mpawo bakabona bamwi basikwiiya bakwe kabanikulya chakulya amaboko “atasalali, ” nkukuti, atasambide.
(BaFalisi abaJuda boonse tabalyi chakulya kabatasambide maboko pe mbuli kuchiyanza chabo, nkaambo bajisi mbuli tunsiyasiya twabapati.
