Nibazwa kuzisambalilo ba Falisi tabalyi pe kabatasambide. Balalondola atumwi tunsiyansiya twiingi, tuli mbuli kusanzya nkomechi, nongo zyameenda azilongo nzikbalida.)
Lino baFalisi abayiisyi bamulawu bakabuzya Jesu bati, “Nkaamboonzi basikwiiya bako nibatalondoli tunsiyansiya twabapati, balalya kabatasambide?”
Wakabasandula wati, “Isaya wakasinsima kabotu aatala andinywe nibasikuupawupa; mbuli mbaakalemba kuti: 'Aba bantu bandilemeka amilomo yabo, pesi myoyo yabo ilikule andime.
Nkombyo zyabo tazikwe nchizyaamba, bayiisya milawu yabantu aziyanza zyabo.'
Mwakalekezya milawu yaLeza, mpawo mwajatisya ziyanza zyabantu. ”
Mpawo wakabaambila wati, “Mujisi nzila inembene yakusunzulusya mulawu waLeza akuubikka kumbali kuti mulondole kabotu tunsiyansiya twanu!
Mozesi wakati, 'Lemeka wuso abanyoko,' akuti 'kufumbwa muntu utukila wisi abayina, weelede kujeegwa.'
Pesi nywe mulati, 'Na muntu waamba kuli wisi abanyina, kuti “Kufumbwa zilibiyeni nzimwakagwasigwa kulindime ngu ‘Kkobbani’ (nkukuti, 'Nchilumbyo cha Leza',) -
elyo tamumuzumizyi kuti achitile wisi abanyina chimwi chintu.
Mulalobya ijwi lya Leza nkaambo katunsiyansiya twanu ntumwakabamba. Alimwi mulachita zintu zyiingi zili mbuli eezyo.”
Mpawo Jesu wakayita makamumakamu abantu wati kulimbabo, “Amundiswilizye, moonse, mumvwisisisye.
Takwe chili kunze amuntu chikonzya kumuninaania kuti chanjila mulinguwe. Chininaania muntu ncheecho chizwa mukati mumoyo wamuntu nchimuninaania.”

Jesu kali wasiya makamumakamu aabantu akunjila mung'anda, basikwiiya bakwe bakamubuzya atala achikozyano eechi.
Jesu wakati, “Tamunaaba akumvwisisisya pe? ” Tamubwene na kuti taakwe chinjila mumuntu chili kunze kwamuntu chinga chilamuninaania chanjila mukati mulinguwe, mbukunga
tachinjili mumoyo wakwe pesi muubula biyo mpawo chazwa kunze. ” Mukwaamba oobu Jesu wakasalazya zyakulya zyoonse.
Wakati, “Chizwa mumuntu nchichita kuti aninaane.
Nkaambo mukati ka myoyo ya bantu, muzwa mizeezo mibi, buyangwe, kubba, bujayi,
bwamu, bwaanka, luuni, lweeno, cheendwe, ibbivwe, kusinga, kulipunayizya abufubafuba.
Zibi eezi zyoonse zizwa mumoyo nzizininaania muntu.”
Wakanyampuka aabusena oobo akuya kuchlikiti cha chaTaya a Sidon. Wakanjila mung'anda alimwi tewakayanda kuti azibinkane kuti mpali amuntu naba omwe, nekuba boobo wakakachilwa kuyuba kuti bantu batamuboni.
Mpawaawo umwi mwanakazi wakali amwana wakanjidwe muuya mubi, mbakamvwa biyo aatala aJesu wakaza wawida kumawulu aakwe.
Mwanakazi oyu wakali wamusyobo waba Gilikki wakazyalilwa kuSiliya Fonisiya. Wakakumbila Jesu kuti atande muuya mubi uzwe mumwana wakwe.
Wakamwaambila wati, “Weelede kulekela bana kuti balye saansi. Nkaambo tachili kabotupe kubweza chakulya chabana mpawo usowele bankala. ”
Pesi wakamuvwiila wati, “Iiyi, Mwami, nekubaboobo alabo bankala balabwezelela bumbulumbulu bulosya bana munsi lyatafula.”
Mpawo wakamwaambila kuti, “Mbwasandula obo, enda biyo, muuya mubi wazwa kale mumwana wako. ”
Mpawo wakajoka kung'anda wajana mwana ulilede abulo, muuya mubi kali wazwa kale.
Lino Jesu wakazwa kubusena bwaTaya wakeenda wayinda muSidoni, katozya kulwizi lwaGalili mpawo wanjila muchilikiti chaDekkapolisi.
Ooku, bamwi bantu bakamweetela mwaalumi musinkematwi kali sichilimilimi, mpawo bakamukumbila kuti amubikke luboko lwakwe amuponisye.
Wakamubweza wakamugwisya mubantu biingi wamutola kumbali, wakamunjizya minwe mumatwi. naakaswida wamudompa alulimi.
Mpawo wakalungumana walanga kujulu, woompomoka wati kulinguwe, “Efata, ” nkukwaamba kuti, “Sinkuka! ”.
Nizyakachitwa eezi mwaalumi oolya akasinkuka matwi aakwe, lulimi lwakwe lwakaangunuka mpawo watanguna kwaambuula kabotu.
Wakabalayilila kuti bataambili bantu. Pesi nakanoonga wabalayilila oobu, bantu nibakayindilila loko kwaambuula azyakachitika.
Bantu bakazula kugamba kabaamba kuti, “Uchita kabotu loko muzintu zyoonse ulaponia basinkematwi abasichilimilimi.”
Kumazuba ayo, kwakaba alubo bantu bayingi loko, alimwi kabatajisi nekuba chakulya. Jesu wakayita basikwiya bakwe mpawo wakati kulimbabo,
“Ndamvwa lweetelelo amakani nkaambo bakendelela kunembo kabali ambebo kale kwamazuba otatwe alimwi kabatakwe nchebakalya.
Na ndabambila kuti kabaya kumyuunzi yabo katakwe nchebalya, bayoowizuka munzila. Bamwi babo bazwa musinzo mulamfu”.
Basikwiiya bakwe bakamusandula, “Nkukuli nkotuyojana chinkwa chizulide mubusena buyuminide buyokkutya bantu aba?”
Wakababuzya, “Mujisi zinkwa zyongane?” Bakamba kuti, “Musanu azibili”.
Wakalayilila makamu kuti akkale ansi. Wakabweza zinkwa musanu azibili, wakapa kulumba alimwi wakazikwamuna. Wakapa basikwiiya bakwe kuti babikke kunembo lyabo, alimwi bakabikka kunembo lyamakamu.
Aboobo bakala answi ziche, nakamana kupa kulumbila mbabo, wakalayilila basikwiiya kuti baabe azezi lubo.
Bakalya pele bakakkuta, pele bakabwezazelela bufwefwelenga bwakachala, insuwo mpati zilimusanu azibili.
Kwakachibe zyuulu zyoone zyabantu.
Mpawo wakabatuma kuti beende. Nibakamana bakanjila mubwaato abasikwiiya bakwe, alimwi bakaya kuchisi chaku Dayimanuta.
Mpawo baFalisi bakasika anze kumukanza. Bakakumbila zitondezyo zyakujulu, kuti bamusunke.
Wakagamba kapati wayoyela mukati wamba wati, “Nkambonzi izyalane eli niliyandula zitondezyo? Nchobeni ndamwambila kuti, takwe chitondezyo nchiyopegwa kuzyalane eli”.
Mpawo wakabasiya, wabweeda mubwaato lubo, akwiinka kulubazu lumbi.
Lino basikwiiya bakaluba kubweza chinkwa beni. Tebakachilikwe chinkwa nikuba chomwe mubwaato.
Wakabalayilila wakati, “Mube akulangila alimwi muchenjele kubumena bwama Falisi akubumena bwa Heloda”.
Basikwiiya bakabonisyana umwi awumwi, “Nkambo kakuti tatukwe chinkwa”.
Jesu wakaziziba ezi, wakati kuli mbabo, “Nkambonzi nimulikubonisyana akubula chinkwa? Sa tamuna kubona? Sa tamuna kumvwisya? Sa myoyo yanu ichilimiyumu?
Mula ameso, tamuboni na? Mulamatwi, tamumvwi na? Sa tamuyeyi?
Nindaka kwamuna zinkwa zilimusanu mumwelwe wamusanu wazyuulu, nzingane nsuwo zyakazwide zyabufwefwelenga bwazinkwa nzimwakabwezelela? Bakati kulinguwe, “Ikkumi azibili.
“Nindakakwamuna zinkwa zilimusanu azibili mumwele wazyuulu zine, nzingane nsuwo zyabufwefwelenga bwazinkwa nzemwakabweza?” Bakati kulinguwe, “Musanu azibili”.
Wakati, “Sa tamunakumvwisya na?”
Bakasika kuBetisayida. Bantu bankuko bakamwetela umwi mwalumi mofu alimwi bakakumbila Jesu kuti amugume.
Jesu wakajata mwalumi mofu ajanza, akumutola kumbali agunzi. Nakasikaswida aansi wakanda bulongo wakamunanika kumeso akwe akumubikka janza lyakwe, wakamubuzya, “Kuli nchwabona na?”
Wakalanga kujulu wakati, Ndabona balumi balangika anga minsamu ilokweenda.
Alimwi wakabikka lubo maanza atala ameso akwe, aboobo mwalumi wakabona, meso akwe akabweda, akubona zintu zyoonse chaantanganana.
Jesu wakamutuma wakati koya kumunzi wanu, “Utakunjili mudolopo”.
Jesu wakiinka abasikwiiya bakwe mugunzi lyaKayisala Filipo. Kabachili munzila wakabuzya basikwiiya bakwe, “Bantu bandamba kuti ndimeni?”
Bakamusandula bakati, “Joni muBbizyi. Bamwi baamba kuti Eliya, abamwi, nduwe umwi wabasinsimi”.
Wakababuzya, “Pele nywebo mundamba kuti ndimeni?” Pita wakati kulinguwe, “Nduwe Kilisito”
Jesu wakabachenjezya kuti batambili nikuba umwi atala anguwe.
Wakasanguna kubayiisya atala akuti Mwana Muntu uyofwabisigwa muzintu zyingi, alimwi uyokukakwa abapati akuba payizi bami akubalembi, akuyojayigwa, pele mumazuba atatu uyobuka.
Wakamba makani aya chaantanganana. Mpawo Pita wakamutola kumbali akumukalalila
Pele Jesu wakachebuka akulanga basikwiiya bakwe mpawo wakakalalila Pita wakati, “Kozwa kusule lyangu, Satani! Tubikkide miyeyo yako kuzintu zya-Leza, pele kuzintu zyabantu”.
Mpawo wakayita makamu abasikwiiya antoomwe, wakabambila kuti, “Na kulumwi uyanda kunditobela welede kulitakata lwakwe mwini, abweze chingano chakwe, akunditobela
Kufumbwa uyanda kufutula buumi bwakwe uyobuswekelwa, ayoyo usweekelwa bumi bwakwe akuyanda kwangu akujwi lyangu uyobujana.
Nimpindunzi njajana muntu kukuvuba nyika yoonse alimwi akuyoswekelwa buumi bwakwe?
Nchili muntu nchakonzya kupa kwinda buumi bwakwe?
Kufumbwa ufwa nsoni akaambo kangu amajwi angu muchibaka chamamambe achibi chazyalane, Mwana aMuntu uyowusigwa nsoni anguwe nakusika mubulemu bwaWisi antoomwe abangelo basalala”.
Wakati kulimbabo, “Nchobeni ndati kuli ndinywe, mpubali bamwi banu bayimvwi awa katakoyofwa banjila kabatana bona Bwami bwakujulu bwa-Leza busika kabuli anguzu.
Nikwakayinda mazuba alimusanu alimwi, Jesu wakabweza Pita, Jemusi aJoni wakeenda ambabo atala amulundu, lwakwe ambabo. Mpo wakasanduka kunembo lyabo.
Zyakusama zyakwe zyakangayima, zyakatubisisya kwiindilila loko kutuba kwiinda chintu chitubisisya munyika chinga chilakonzya kupenda chimwi.
Mpawo Elayija kali aMozesi wakalibonya kulimbabo alimwi wakalikwambula a Jesu.
Pita wakasandula akwamba kuti kuli Jesu, “Muyiisi, nchibotu kuba ano toonse, atuyake zilawu zyotatwe, chimwi chibe chako, chimwi chibe chaMozesi alimwi chimwi chibe cha Eliya”.
(Takalizi zyakwamba, nkambo wakali yowede.)
Ijoba lyakasika akubavumba. Mpawo ijwi lyakazwa mujoba,”Ooyu ngomwana wangu ngundiyandisya. Amumuswiilile”.
Aboobo, nibakalanga kumbali, bakabona kakutachikwe muntu akati kabo pesi Jesu alikke.
Nibakalikuya buseluka kuzwa achilundu, wakabalayilila kuti tabelede kubuzya kufumbwa omwe nzibakabona kusikila Mwana aMuntu akabuke kuzwa kubafu.
Mpo bakabamba twaambo twabo beni, pesi bakazuwisyana lwabo beni ninzi “Kubuka kuzwa kubafu” zyambaayi.
Bakamubuzya, “Nkambonzi balembi nibakati Eliya nguyelede kutalika kusika?”
Wakati kulimbabo, “Eliya ulelede kutalika kusika kuzobambulula zintu zyoonse. Lino nkaambonzi nikulembedwe kuti Mwana waMuntu nelede kufwabisigwa kuzintu zyiingi akunyonganisigwa?
Pesi ndamwambila kuti Eliya wasika, bakachita kufumbwa nzibayanda kuchita alinguwe mbuli mbukulembedwe atala anguwe”.
Mpawo nibakasika kuli basikwiiya, bakabona makamu abantu kabazyungulikide.
Mpo balembi bakali kukazyanya ambabo. Lino nibakabona Jesu, makamu woonse akagamba nibakamuchijanina bakamujuzya.
Wakabuzya basikwiiya bakwe, “Mulikukazyananzi ambabo?”
Umwi wakalinkamu wakasandula, “Omwiiyi, ndeeta mwana wangu kulinduwe ulamuuya umwiita kuti atambuulipe.
Umumana manguzu akumuwunsizya ansi akuzwa kkovu mumulomo, ngawayuma ntwiinyo, akuyuma mubili. Ndakabuzya basikwiiya bako kuti bamugusye asi bakakachilwa”.
Wakabasandula, “Mazyalane atasyomi, ndakkala andinywe kwachiindi chilibuti? Ndiyomukombelezya kuchiindi chilibuti? Mumweete kuli ndime”
Bakamweta mulombe kulinguwe. Kuchindi muuya nwakabona Jesu, mpawo awo lyakamuwisya lyamupa kugwigwima. Mulombe wakawida ansi akuzwa ikkovu mumulomo.
Jesu wakabuzya wisi, “Kwaba chiindi chilibiyeni kazichitikana?” Wisi wakati, “Kuzwa kachili mwanikenike”.
Chimuwisizya mumulilo kkana mumanzi akwezya kumujeyakuti kukonzya kuchita kufumbwa, tufwide luzyalo utugwasye”.
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Kuti kazikonzeka zyoonse zintu zilakonzeka kuliyoyo usyoma!”
Mpawo wisi wamwana wakalila akwamba kuti, “Ndimusyomi! kondigwasya akutasyoma kwangu!”
Jesu nakabona makamu kabachijanina, wakatanda myuuya mibi akwaamba kuti, “Nutambuli nutamvwi ndakwambila kuti, zwamulinguwe, utazobi nunjila lubo mulinguwe”.
Lyakalila akugwigwimya mulombe akuzwa mulinguwe. Mulombe wakalanga mbuli wakalifwide, biingi bakati,”Ulifwide”.
Pele Jesu wakamubeza aluboko wamunyampula, mulombe wakayimikila.
Jesu nakasika munganda, basikwiiya bakamubuzya chakusisikizya, “Nkambonzi nitwatalitanda?”
Wakati kulumbabo, “Ezi zyamisyobo oyu tazitandiki pesi akukomba”.
Bakeenda kuzwa awo akwiinda muGalilaya. Takalikuyanda kufumbwa kuti bazibe nkubakabede,
nakalikuyiisya basikwiiya bakwe. Wakati kulimbabo, “Mwanamuntu uyopendekezegwa mumaboko amuntu, alimwi bayomujeya. Natayobikwe kulufu, nikutakayinde mazuba atatu uyobuka kuzwa kubafu.
Pesi tebakazimvwisisisya pe nzyakali kwamba, alimwi bakalikuyowa kumubuzya.
Mpawo nibakasika kuKkapenamu. Mpawo nakanjila munganda wakababuzya, Mwalikwambanzi munzila?”
Pesi bakawumuna. Mbulikuti bakalibuya bukazyanya awumwi amwenzinyina kabali munzila atala akuti ngwani mupati.
Nakakkala ansi, wakayita basikwiiya bakwe bali kkumi ababili kabali boonse alimwi wakati kulimbabo, “Na kuli uyanda kuba wakusanguna, welede kuba wakumaninsizya kuli boonse akubalanda boonse”.
Wakabweza mwana munini wakamibikka akati kabo. Wakamubweza akumubikka amakwiko akwe alimwi wakati kulimbabo,
“Kufumbwa utambula mwana oyu muzina lyangu watambula ndime, kufumbwa oyo unditambula tatambuli ndime pesi utambula oyo wakandituma”.
Joni wakati, “Muyiisi, twabona umwi katanda badayimona munzina lyako alimwi twamukasya, nkaambo tatutobeli pe”.
Pesi Jesu wakati, “Mutamukasyi, mbulikuti takwe utakachite milimu mipati muzina lyangu alimwi mbulikuzwa awo bakambule kufumbwa zili atala andime.
Kufumbwa utakazyani andiswe ngwesu.
Kufumbwa ukupa nkomesi yamanzi kuti unywe muzina lyangu nkambo uzwa kwaKilisito, nchobeni ndamwambila kuti, takoyoyibulikilwa impindu yakwe.
Kufumbwa uchita banikenike bandisyoma kui bae, zinoli zibotu kulinguwe kuti abeze ibwe asungililwe munsingo yakwe alimwi awalwe mulwizi.
Naa kuboko kwako kwakubisizya, kudunsule. Nchibotu kunjila mubwami bwakubotelwa kwiinda kuba amaboko abili alimwi wakuwida mubbibi lyamulilo, kumulilo utazimi.
Munchali 44mutabikkilizidwe mu ULB. Amba kuti ichikoye chabo tachikoyofwa, alimwi mulilo tukoyozimwa.
Na kuulu kwako kwakuchita kuti ubisye, kudunsule. Nchibotu kunjila mubuumi bwakubotelwa kuli chilema kwiinda kuba amawulu abili alimwi wakuwida mubbibi lyamulilo.
Munchali 46 tabikkidwe pe mu ULB. Amba kuti ichikonye chabo tachikoyofwa, alimwi mulilo tukoyozimwa.
Na liso lyako lyakuchita kuti ubisye, ligusye. Nchibotu kunjila mubwami bwakujulu aliso limwi kwiinda kuba ameso abili wakuwisigilwa mubbibi lyamulilo,
kutayofwa kwachikonye chabo, mulilo tukoyozima.
Nkaambo moonse muyolungwa amunyo wamulilo.
Munyo mubotu, pesi kuti munyo wasapuka, ulachitwa biyeni kuti ube munyo lubo? Amube munyo nywebo nobeni, alimwi mube alumuno kuli umwi awumwi”.
Jesu nakazwa kubusena obo waya kuchisi chaku Judiya a kubusena bwamutala a mulongaJodani, alimwi bantu biingi bakaza lubo kulinguwe. Wakali kubayiisya lubo, mbuli mbakali wazibila kuchita.
Mpawo baFalisi bakaza kulinguwe kuzomusunka alimwi bakmubuzya kuti, “Chili mumulawu na kuti mwalumi aleke banakwe?” Wakasandula,
“Wakamulayilila buti Mozesi?”
Bakati, “Mozesi wakazuminina mwalumi kulemba lugwalo lwakulekana alimwi akumutanda”.
“Nkuyuma kwamyoyo yanu chakapa kuti alembe mulawo oyu”, Jesu wakabambila.
“Pele kuzwa kumatalikilo akulenga, 'Leza wakababumba, mwalumi amwanakazi'.
“Akambo kachechi mwalumi uyozwa kuliwisi abanyina
alimwi akakkale abanakwe, alimwi bobile bayooba nyama yomwe! Aboobo tabachili bobile pe, pele nyama yomwe”.
Aboobo Leza nzyaswanizya antoomwe, kutakabi muntu uzyaanzania”.
Awo nibakali mun'anda, basikwiiya bakamubuzya lubo aatala achechi.
Wakati kulimbabo, “Naba ani uleka mwanakazi akukwata umbi wamuchita bumambi.
Naa mukayintu waleka mulumi wakwe wakwatwa awumbi mwalumi, wachita bumambi”.
Mpawo bakeeta bana babo banini kulinguwe kuti abagume, pele basikwiiya bakabakalalila.
Pele Jesu nakazibona, tezyakamubotezya pe alimwi wakati kulimbabo, “Muzumizye bana mutabakasyi, nkambo bwami bwaLeza mbubwabo bali boobo.
Chakasimpe ndamwambila, naba ani utatambuli bwami bwaLeza mbuli mwana munini takonzyi kuyobunjila”.
Mpawo wakababweza bana mumanza akwe alimwi wabalongezya nakabikka maboko akwe alimbabo.
Nakatalisya lweendo lwakwe, umwi mwalumi wakachijana wazofugama kunembo lyakwe alimwi wabuzya, “Muyisi mubotu, ndichite buti kuti ndikajane buumi butamani?”
Jesu wakati, “Nkambonzi nuti ndimubotu? Tako pe mubotu naba umwi kunze kwaLeza alikke.
Ulizi milawo: 'Utajayi, utachiti bumambi, utabbi, utabejelezyi umwi, utabbi chakweenena, lemeka uso abanyoko.”
Mwalumimwakati, “Muyisi, zyoonse ezi zintu ndakazitibelezya kuzwa kandichili mukubusi”.
Jesu wakamulanga alimwi wamuyanda. Wakati kulinguwe, “Chintu chimwi nchobula. Weelede kuuzya zyoonse nzulazyo alimwi uzipe kubachete, elyo uyojana buvubi kujulu. Mpawo sika, unditobele”.
Pesi akaambo kamakani aya wakawusa kapati alimwi wakayinka kafwisya nsoni, nkambo wakali azintu zyiingi.
Jesu wakalangalanga mpawo wakati kulibasikwiiya bakwe, “Nchiyumu buti kubavubi kunjila mu bwami bwaLeza!”
Basikwiiya bakagamba kumajwi akwe.
Pesi Jesu wakabambila lubo, “Nobana, nchuubawuba kunkamela kuti yiinde mumpako yanaliti kwiinda muvubi kuti anjile mubwami bwaLeza”.
Bakagamba kapati alimwi baambilana kuti, “Ngwani unga ulakonzya kufutulwa?”
Jesu wakabalanga alimwi wati, “Kubantu tachikonzeki, pele kuli Leza chilakonzeka. Nkambo zintu zyoonse zilakonzeka a Leza”.
Pita wakatalika kwambula kulinguwe, “Boona, twasiya zyoonse twakutobela”.
Jesu wakati, “Nchobeni ndamwambila, takwe pe wasiya n'anda naa banyandumi naa bachizi naa banyina naa bana naa nyika akambo kandime alimwi akambo kavangeli,
utakabule kutambula zyiindulwidwe mwaanda munyika omuno lino: n'anda abanyandumi a bachizi a mamama abana anyika, mukupenzegwa, munyika utobela, buumi butamani.
Pele biingi balikumatangunino bayooba bakumamanino”.
Bakali mumugwagwa kabayabuya kuJelusalema, alimwi Jesu wakali kunembo lyab. Basikwiiya bakagamba, alimwi abaabo bakali kutobela musule bakayowa. Mpawo Jesu wakabweza bali kkumi ababili wabatola kumbali alubo watalika kubambila zizochitikana kulinguwe kuchiindi chitobela linolino.
“Amubone, tuyabuya kuJelusalema, alimwi Mwana waMuntu uyowabwa kubapayizi bapati abalembi.
Bayomupa mulandu walufu akumwaaba kulibamasi. Bayomusonsya, bayomuswida mate amubili, bayomuuma, alimwi bakamujeye. Pele kwiinda mazuba atatu uyobuka.
Jemusi a Joni, bana baZebbadi, bakaza kulinguwe bati, “Muyisi, tuyanda kuti mutuchitile kufumbwa nzituyomukumbila kulinduwe”.
Wakati kulimbabo, “Niinzi nchimuyanda kuti ndikamuchitile?”
Bakati, “Tuzumizye kuti tukkale anduwe mubulemu bwako, umwi kuchilisyo umwi kuchimwensi.”
Pele Jesu wakabasandula, “Tamuchizi nchimuli kukumbila. Mulakonzya na kunywa nkomechi njesikanywe naa kukakatila kulubbizizyo ndwesikabbizigwe andulo?”
Bakati kulinguwe, “Tulakonzya.” Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Nkomechi njesikanywe, muyoyinywa, alimwi lubbizizyo ndwesikabbizigwe andulo, anywebo muyolubbizigwa.
Pele utakakkale kuchilisyo kana kuchimwensi tensi ndime nensyambe pe, pele nkukwabaabo babambilidwe mbubo.”
Awo bamwi balikkumi nibakamvwa eecho, bakatalika kunyemena Jemusi a Joni.
Jesu wakabayita kulinguwe wati, “Mulizi aabo baambwa kuti mbendelezi babamasi balabeendelezya, alimwi basikutwe babo bakatondezya manguzu aabo alimbabo.
Pele tazikoyooba mbubo pe akati kanu. Naba ani uyanda kuba mupati akati kanu weelede kuba mupati mulanda,
alimwi naba ani uyanda kuba mutanzi akati kanu weelede kuba muzike waboonse
Nkambo Mwana aMuntu takazida kuzofutulwa pe, pele kufutula, alimwi akupa buumi bwakwe kukwangununa biingi.”
Bakasika kuJelikko. Nakazwa kuJelikko abasikwiiya bakwe amakamu makamu, mwana wa Timiyasi, Bbatimiyasi, moofu, wakalikkede kumbali amugwagwa.
Awo nakamvwa kuti Jesu muNazaleni, wakatalika koompolola wati, “Jesu Mwana waDavida, ndifwide luzyalo!”
Biingi bakamukasya mwalumi boofu, bamwambila kuti awumune. Pele wakompolola changuzu, “Mwana waDavida, ndifwide luzyalo!”
Jesu wakayimikila alimwi wabalayilila kuti bamwiite. Bakamwiita mwalumi moofu, bati, “Koyuma! Nyampuka! Ulikukwiita.”
Wakasowela ansi chikobela chakwe, wasotoka alimwi wasika kuli Jesu.
Jesu wakamusandula wati, “Niinzi nchuyanda kuti ndikuchitile?” Mwalumi moofu wakati, “Muyisi ndiyanda kubona.”
Mpawo Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Kuya. Lusyomo lwako lwakuponya.” Mpaawo wakabona lubo, alimwi wakamutobela mumugwagwa.
Nibakasika ku Jelusalemu kabali aafwiifwi aku Bbetipeji a Bbetani aku Chilundu chama Oliva, Jesu wakatuma basikwiiya bakwe bobile,
wakati kuli mbabo, “Amwiinke kugunzi lilikunembo lyenu, mbumutakanjile biyo, muyoojana mwana wembongolo waangidwe nkuko, uutanatantwa naba womwe muntu. Mukamwaangunune mumweete okuno.
Na kuli uyomubuzya kuti, “Muchitilaanzi oobu”? mukamwaambile kuti, ‘Mwami nguulikumuyanda alubo ulamuboozya aano muchiindi chifwiifwi.”
Bakayinka baakumujana mwana wedonki kumbali aamunzi, kaangidwe kumanjililo aamunzi. Nibakamwaangununa.
Bamwi bantu bakayimvwi mpawo bakabuzya kuti, “Muchitaanzi, nimwaangununa mwana wembongolo donki ooyu? ”
Bakasandula mbuli Jesu mbaakabaambilide, mpawo bantu bakabazumizya kuti beende.
Nibakamweeta mwana wembongolo kuli Jesu bakayala majansi amusana wakwe, Jesu wakakkala aalinguwe.
Bantu biingi bakayala milembo yabo mumugwagwa, bamwi bakayala matu ngibakatemene mumuunda.
Bakazulwide abakalimusule bakoompolola kabati, “Hossana! Ulilongezezedwe ooyo uza muzina lyaMwami.
Bulilongezegedwe ibwaami buyobuza ibwa taata wesu Davida! Hossana mujulu lyamajulu!”
Jesu wakanjila mu Jelusalema akwiinka ku Chikombelo bakalangalanga boonse busena, pele nkaambo kakuti lyakali lyaba goko, wakayinka ku Bbetani abalikumi aababili.
Buzuba butobela nibakaboola kuzwa ku Bbetani, wakali waba aanzala.
Mukubona mukuyu amatu aawo chakule, wakayinka kuti akabone kuti ulaamichelo na. Naakasika afwiifwi wabona matu luzutu kakutakwe michelo, kambo techakali chiindi chankuyu pe.
Elyo wakaambila mukuyu kuti, “Kutazoobi naba womwe uzoolya michelo kulinduwe. ” Basikwiiya baakwe bakamumvwa kawamba majwi aayo.
Naakasika mu Jelusalema, wakanjila muchikombelo mpawo wakatalika kwaandingania bakalikuula akuuzya oomo. Wakatonta matebuli aabasimuchincha mali ezyuuno zyabaabo bakalikuuzya nkwilimba.
Mpawo takwe naakazumizya naba omwe kuti abweze zyakalikuuzigwa mulubaya lwatempele.
Mpawo naakabayiisya wakati, “Tachilembedwe na kuti: `Ng'anda yangu iyotegwa ning'anda yakukombela kwamanyika wonse’? Pesi nywebo mwayichita ng'anda yabasikubba. ”
Bapati babapayizi abasimilawo bakaamvwa makani aya eelyo bakayandula nzila zyakumujaya aazyo, bakalikumuyowa nkaambo bantu biingi boonse bakaba aakugamba enjiisyo yakwe.
Nilyakaba igoko, bakazwa mudolopo.
Chifumofumo nkabayobweenda, bakabona mukuyu nkuuyumide kuzwa kumiyanda.
Pita wakayeeya mpawo wakati kuli Jesu, “Muyisi wangu langa! Mukuyu ngwakatukila wayuma!”
Jesu wakasandula kuti, “Amube aalusyomo muli Leza.
Ndimwaambila kasimpe kuti, na umwi wati kuchilundu, ‘Nkoya ukaliwalile mulwizi, ’ mpawo nkatadooneki mumoyo wakwe pesi nkasyoma kuti ezyo nzyawamba ziyochitika, ziyochitika mbubo.
Nkaako ndamwaambila kuti: Kufumbwa nchimuyookumbila mukukomba, amusyome kuti muyoochijana, mpawo chiyooba chanu.
Mpawo naa wayimikila kokomba, na nkowangilide umwi moyo, mulekelele, nkokuti Wuso wako ulikujulu akulekelele zibi zyako.
[“Nkambo kuti inywe nkamutalekeleli bantu balaamilandu kuli ndinywe, alakwe Wuso uulikujulu takoyoomulekelela milandu yenu”.]
Bakasika lubo kuJelusama. Eelyo Jesu naakayobweenda mulubuwa lwaChikombelo, bapayizi bapati, abayisyi bamulawu abapati bembungano bakeza kulinguwe.
Bakati, “Mumanguzu aani mochita zintu ziloobu? Alimwi ngwani ukupa inguzu zyakuchita zintu eezi? ”.
Jesu wakasandula kuti, “Ndiyobuzya mubuzyo womwe. Mundisandule, eelyo ndiyomwaambila kuti munguzu zyani mwendiikuchita zintu eezi.
Lubbabbatizyo lwaJohani, lwakalikuzwa kujulu na, nakuti lwakazwa kumuntu? Mundambile!”
Bakayizya aatala amakani aaya mpawo bakakazyania bati, “Nitwaamba kuti, ‘Luzwa kuzulu, ’ ulatubuzya kuti 'Nkamboonzi nimutamusyomi? ’
Pesi nitwaamba kuti, 'Luzwa kumuntu’.... ” bakayoowa bantu nkaambo muntu woonse wakalizi kuti Joni musinsimi mwinimwini.
Alimwi bakasandula Jesu kuti “Tatuzi pe.” Mpawo Jesu wakabaambila kuti, “Nsikomwaambila pe ambebo kuti manguzu aani ngechita aawo zintu eezi”.
Mpawo wakasanguna kubaambila maambila mbali wakati, “Mwaalumi umwi wakabyala misamu yamisansa. Wakayakila lubaya aalinjiyo, wakasya dindi lyakudinina nsansa, akuyaka ingaze yasikulinda. Alimwi wakajana kupa bamwi balimi mpawo wakaya kuchisi chimbi.
Muchiindi chakutebula wakatuma umwi wababelesi bakwe kuyoobweza michelo yamansansa.
Pesi balimi abo bakakumujata, akumuma, akumwaanda nkakutakwe nchakabweda aacho pe.
Wakatuma uumbi mubelesi; oyo mwaalumi bakamutulula mumutwe akumusampawula. Wakatuma uumbi, alubo oyo bakakumujaya.
Wakatuma bambi bingi; bamwi bakawumwa, bamwi bakajayigwa.
Kwakasyaala omwe biyo wakutuma, nkali mwana ngwaakali kuyandisya kapati. Wakamutuma nkali wakumaninsizya, wakati, “Bayomulemeka mwanaangu.”
Pesi balimi bakaambilana kuti, “Ooyu ngusimulya lukono. muze tumujaye, mpawo lukono luyoba lwesu.”
Nkabela bakamujata akumujaya, akumuwaalila anze aamuunda waminsansa.
Aboobo ulachita buti mwani muunda? Ulasika akujaya balimi akape bambi muunda wamisaansa.
Tamuna kwaabala na malembe: ‘Ibbwe lyakasowedwe abasikuyaka ndilyakazooba ibbwe lyachooko.
Mwaami ngwaakachichita eechi, mpawo chilabotezya kumenso eesu? ’”
Eelyo bakayanduula nzila yakumwaanga aayo nkaambo bakaziba kuti wakali kwaamba mbabo kumaambila mbali aaya. Pesi bakayoowa inkamu yabantu yakaliwo, nkaako bakamusiya mpawo bakeenda.
Muchiindi chitobela bakatuma bamwi baba Falisi aba Heloda kuli Jesu kuti bakamujate mumakani aakwe.
Bakasika kulinguwe bakati, “Muyisi, tulizi kuti ulimwaalumi ulaabulemu usyomekede. Topenzegwi abantu, nkaambo toswiilizyi makani aamuntu na kulanga chiwa chamuntu; pesi uyiisya nzila ya Leza mbuli mbiibede amubwini. Chileede na kutela kuli Kkayisala na pe? Tweelede kuti tubbadale na, naa kuti pe? ”
Pesi Jesu wakalizi kuupawupa kwabo. Jesu wakababuzya kuti, “Kaambonzi nimulikweezya kunditeya? ” Wakati, “Amundeetele nsiliva yanu alimwi ndiibone mbiibede.”
Elyo bakiiyeta nsiliva, alimwi wakababuzya kuti, “Mbubwani busyu obu? Alimwi ndizina lyani lilembedwe mpawo? ” Bakasandula kuti, “Nzizya Kkayisala. ”
Mpawo Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Amupe Kkayisala zyaKkayisala, alimwi mupe Leza izya Leza. ” Bakaba aakugamba aatala anguwe.
Mpawo ba Saduki, baamba kuti takwe bubuke, bakaza kulinguwe amubuzyo. Bakati,
“Muyisi, Mozesi wakatulembela kuti, 'Na mukulana wamulumi mpawo wasiya mwanakazi kabatakwe bana, mwaalumi weelede kukwata mukamufu mpawo babe abana bamukulana.'
Kwakali bana bachaalumi bali musanu ababili. Mutaanzi wakakwata mpawo wakafwa katasiide mwana naba womwe.
Wachibili wakakwata mukamufu, pesi alakwe wakafwa katasiide mwana. Chakaba mbubo akuli watatu.
Tawope akati kababa bali musanu ababili wakasiya mwana. Kumamanino, alakwe mwanakazi wakafwa.
Kububuke bwabafu, oyu mwanakazi uyooba wani? Mbunga boonse kabali musanu abatatu bakalimukwete.”
Jesu wakasandula kuti, “Tamuli mubulubizi na kambo malembe tamwaazi naa kuti manguzu aa Leza?
Bafu nibayoobuka, tabakoyookwata nikuba kukwatanisigwa; bayooba mbuli bangelo kujulu.
Lino mukwaamba atala abafu nibayoobuka temwakabala na muBbuku lyaMozesi, kuleezyo zyakachitika kuchiteyo, Leza mbakaambula kulinguwe, ‘Ndime Leza wa Abbulamu, Leza wa Ayizeki, alubo Leza wa Jakobo?'
Tali Leza wabafwide, pesi ngwababapona. Mulilubizizye kapati!”
Umwi wabayisyi bamulawo naakasika wakamvwa kabakazyania. Nkabwene kuti Jesu wakali wabapa nsandulo mbotu, wakabuzya Jesu kuti, “Nguuli mulawo mupati kwiinda imwi akati kamilawo yoonse? ” Jesu wakamusandula kuti,
“Ngooyu: ‘Amuswiilile, noma Izilayeli, Mwaami Leza wesu, Mwaami ngumwi.
Yanda Mwami Leza wako amoyo wako woonse, amizeezo yako yoonse, mpawo amanguzu aako woonse. ’ Wabili ngooyu:
‘Yanda mweenzinyokwe mbuli mboliyanda. ’ Tuwope mulawo mupati wiinda eeyi.”
Oyu mwaalumi wakasandula kuti, “Waamba kabotu omuyisyi, waamba kabotu kuti Leza ngumwi alubo takukwe umbi kunze kwakwe alike.
Kumuyanda amoyo wako woonse, akumvwisisisya kwako alubo amanguzu aako woonse, mpawo akuyanda simabambanwa wako mbuli mboliyanda nkubotu loko kwiinda zipayizyo. ”
Lino Jesu naakabona kuti wasandula chabuchenjezu, wakati kuli nguwe, “Tolikulepe a Bwami bwa Leza. ” Elyo kuzwa awo tawope naba omwe wakeezya kumubuzya iimbi mibuzyo.
Nkali kuyiisya Jesu mulubuwa lwatempele, wakabuzya mubuzyo wakati, “Nkamboonzi bayiisi bamulawo nibati Kilisitu mwana waDavida? We lwakwe
Devidi, kaambuzigwa a Muuya Uusalala, wakachaamba antanganana wakati: ‘Mwami wakati kuMwami wangu, kkala kukuboko kwachilisyo kwangu kusikila basinkondonyokwe ndibabike kunsi amawulu aako. ’
We lwakwe Devidi umwiita kuti ‘Mwami. ’ Ani inga ulaba mwana wakwe biyeni? ” Inkamu yabantu yaka muswiilizya chalumwemwe.
Naakalikuyiisya Jesu wakati, “Amubachenjelele bayiisi bamulawo balayandisya kweendeenda kabatungana mulongo kabajuzigwa kumasambalilo,
alubo akupegwa zyuuno zibotu mumambungano akulemekwa kapati aabungene bantu.
Balanyonyoona maanda abamukabafu kabakomba ankombyo ndamfu chakweebwa. Aaba bantu bayoopegwa chisubulo chipati.”
Jesu wakakkala kumbali lyachiykoobwedo chazituzyo mung'anda ya Leza; bantu nibakalikuwaala mali muchiyobweedo. Bavubi biingi bakalikuwala imali nyingi.
Pesi mukamufu muchete wakabika biyo tupeni tobile, tweelene aaseleni lyomwe.
Lino wakayita basikwiiya bakwe, wakati, Ndiikumwaambila kasimpe kuti, ooyu mukamufu wabika kwiinda boonse muchiyobwedo.
Boonse bapa mukweendelana abuvubi bwabo; pesi we, mubuchete bwakwe, wabika zyoonse nzyaalangilide mubuumi bwakwe kuti apone anzizyo.”
Awo Jesu nakali kweenda kuzwa mucikombelo, umwi wabasikwiiya bakwe wakati kuli nguwe, “Muyiisi langa imabwe aziyako zigambwa!”
Wakati kulinguwe, “Ulizibwene na iziyako zipati eezi? Takwe ibwe lyomwe litakasyale atala alimwi litakwe kwakukolomwedwa ansi”.
Awo nakakkala achilundu chama Oliva chilengene achikombelo, Pita a Jemusi a Endulu bakabuzya chakusisikizya,
“Twambile eezi zintu ziyochitikana lili? Niinzi chiyooba chitondezyo chazintu eezi kuti zyamba kuchitika?”
Jesu wakatalika kubambila, “Amukachenjele kuti kutakabi uyomwena.
Bangi bayoza muzina lyangu kabati, 'Ndime nguwe', pesi bayoyena bangi.
Chiindi nimuyomvwa inkondo ampuwo zyankondo, mutakalikatazyi; ezi zintu kuleede zikachitike, pesi mamanino anoli katanasika pe.
Nkaambo inyika iyobukilana enyika, abwami buyobukilana abwaminyina. Kuyoba kuteketa kwamasena mangi anzala zyiingi. Ezi matalikilo amachise akutumbuka.
Amukalinde. Bayomupeda kukubetekwa, alimwi muyowumwa muzikombelo. Muyoyima kunembo lyabendelezi abaami nkambo kangu, kuti bukabe bukamboni kuli mbabo.
Pesi makani mabotu ayotalika kukambawuka kunyika zyoonse.
Alimwi nibayomwanga akumupeda, mutakalikatazyi ikuti muyotyeni. Nkambo muchiindi echo nzimutakambe muyozipegwa; teensi ndinywe mutanowambule, pesi Muuya Usalala.
Mukulana uyoozya mwanike kulufu, a wisi kumwanakwe. Bana bayobukilana abazyali babo bakabatole kulufu.
Muyosungwa abantu boonse nkambo kazina lyangu. Pesi utajatilile mane kukabe kumamanino, oyo muntu uyofutulwa.
Nimuyobona chisesemyo chalunyonyoko kachimvwi mpuchitelede kwimikila (Oyo ubala ngamvwisye), abanolimu Judiya abachijile mumalundu,
akube kuti oyo uli achiluli changanda ataseluki kuya mun'anda naba kuti kuyotola chintu mukati,
ayoyo uli mulukuba atakabwedi kukutola chisamo.
Pesi maawe kuli babo balamada ababo banyonsya bana batete mumazuba ayo!
Amukombe kuti ezi zitakachitikani mumpeyo.
Nkambo ayo anoli mazuba akupengana kupati, atakabawo kuzwa kumatalikilo, awo Leza nakalenge nyika, kusikila lino, pe, nikuba kuti achiza alimwi.
Na kuti Mwami takafwiinsya mazuba, takwe mubuli walikuzofutulwa. Pesi nkaambo kababo basale abo basalala, wakafwiinsya mazuba.
Ino kuti umwi akatedi kulindime, 'Amulange, ngoyu Kilisito!' na kuti 'Amulange, ngulya!' mutakasyomi pe.
Nkambo kuyoba aba Kilisito bakubeja aba sinsimi bakubeja batakalibonye alimwi kuyoba zitondezyo azigambyo atakaboneke, na kuti chali chuba, basale.
Amukalindile! Ndamwambila zintu zyoonse kunembo lyachiindi.
Pesi musule lyamazuba akupenzegwa, zuba liyoba mudima, amweezi tukoyopa mumuni,
Nyenyezi ziyoloka kuzwa kujulu, alawo manguzu alikujulu ayoteketegwa.
Alimwi nibatakabone Mwana waMuntu kazamumayoba amanguzu a bulemu.
Alimwi uyotuma bangelo bakwe, uyobunganya aamwi basale bakwe kuzwa kumyuya yone, kuzwa kumamanino anyika kusika kumamanino ajulu.
Amwiiye chiiyo kuzwa kumukuyu. Awo ntabi niyisyukila matu, mwaziba kuti minza aswena.
Mbubobo, na kuti mwabona zintu kazchitikana, muzibe kuti waswena, afwifwi amilyango.
Nchobeni, ndamwambila, olu luzubo talukoyoyinda ezi zintu kazitana chitikana.
Ijulu anyika ziyoyinda, pesi majwi angu takoyinda pe.
Pesi buzuba obo achiindi, takwe muntu uzi, nikuba bangelo kujulu, na kuti Mwana, pesi kuti Taata.
Muchengele! Mulange, nkambo tamuzi kuti chiindinzi. Amwi malembe achiindi alembedwe muchiGilikki: Muchenjele! Mulange akukomba.
Zilimbuli muntu winka musinzo - wabusiya nganda yakwe wakwiibikka mumanza abalanda bakwe kuti bayibambe, umwi awumwi amulimu wakwe, wawabambila balinda nganda kuti amubuke.
Aboobo amuchenjele nkambo tamuzi kuti simalelo wanganda nabola kunganda; zilakonzya kuba goko, na kuti akati kamansiku, awo mukuku niwulila, na kuti bwacha.
Na kuti asike mpawawo, atakajani mulilede.
Nzindimwambila nywebo nditi kumuntu woonse: Linda!”
Lino kakutanasika mazuba abili kuya kupobwe lyakwindilila alyamikamu bwachinkwa chitakwe bumena. Mupati wabapayizi abalembi bakalangula inzila isisikene kuti ngabalamujata biyeni Jesu akumujaya.
Nkambo balikwamba kuti “kutabi muchindi chapobwe, kuti kutabi kunyongana akati kabantu”
Lino Jesu kalimu Bbetani mun'anda ya Sayimoni sichinsenda, kachili mukulya atafula, mwanakazi wakasika kulinguwe amunkuli watununkilizyo tudula loko, ooyo wakali wanadi. Wakapwaya munkuli akutila nadi amutwe wakwe.
Pesi kuli bamwi bakabijilwa. Bakambuzyana akati kabo kabati, “Wanyonywedanzi?
Tununkilizyo otu tweelede kuuzigwa ikwiinda myaanda itatu yamaseleni ikapegwe bachete”. Mpawo wakamukasya.
Pesi Jesu wakati, “Amumusiye alikke. Mumukatazizyanzi? Wandichitila chintu chibotu.
Bachete mulaabo kaale lyoonse, kufumbwa chindi nimwayanda mulakonzya kubachitila kabotu, tamukoyooba andime lyoonse pe. Wachita eecho nchakoonzya.
Wananika kale mubili wangu kuti ukazikwe.
Ndamwambila kasimpe kuti, kufumbwa makani mabotu nkwayookambawukwa munyika yoonse, eechi nchachita mwanakazi ooyu chinowambuulwa, mukumuyeya”.
Mpawo Judasi Isikkaliyoti umwi balikkumi ababili wakaya kubapayizi kuti akamupede kuli mbabo.
Lino bapayizi bapati nibamvwa oobo, bakabotelwa akumusyomezya kuti apege mali. Wakatalika kuyandula mweenya wakumupeda kuli mbabo.
Mubuzuba butaanzi bwachinkwa chitakwe bumena, lino nibakapayizya kabelele kapobwe lyakundilila, basikwiiya bakati kuli nguwe, “Nkokuli nkuyanda kuti tukabambilile kuti ukalye chakulya chapobwe lyakwindilila?”
Wakatuma basikwiiya babili akubaambila kuti, “Kamuya mugunzi, eelyo muyooswanana amwalumi unyampwide munkuli wameenda mumutobele.
Ooko nkwayojinka mun'anda mukamutobele mukati kuli munan'and, 'Muyisi wati, “Ilikuli yangu n'anda yabeenzu ooko nkundiyolinda ipobwe lyakwindilila abasikwiya bangu?”
Uyomutondezya n'anda mpati yamujulu ibambidwe kabotu. Mukatubambilile mumo”.
Mpawo basikwiya bakazwa bayinka mumunzi. Lino bakazijana zyoonse mbuli mbakabambila, eelyo bakambilila chakulya chapobwe lyakwindilila.
Nikwakaba golezya, wakaza abali kkumi ababili.
Aawo nibakali yeeme atafula akulya, Jesu wakati kasimpe ndamwambila kuti umwi wanu ngundilikulya aawe uyonduuzya.
Mpawo boonse bakawusaloko, alimwi awumwi wakati kuli nguwe, “Masimpe tensi ndime pe?”
Jesu wakasandula wakati kuli mbabo, “Nguumwi wabali kkumi ababili, ooyu wazwa kunika chinkwa lino mundido andime?”
Aboobo Mwana waMuntu uyoyinka mbuli mbukulembedwe atala anguwe. Pesi maawe kulooyo muntu wachitya kuti Mwana aMuntu awuzigwe chali kubota kumntu ooyo natakazyalwa”.
Aawo nibakachili kulya Jesu wakabweza chinkwa, wachilongezya, akuchikwamuna. Wabapa akwamba kuti, “Mubeze eechi ngumubili wangu”.
Alimwi wakabweza nkomechi, wapa kulumba, akukapa, eelyo bakanywa boonse.
Wakati kuli mbabo, “Oobu mbubulowa bwangu bwachizuminano, bulowa butilwa baangi”
Kasimpe ndamwambila kuti, nsikoyonywa limbi e ooyu muchelo wamasansa kusikila buzuba oobo nindiyoonywa mubwami bwaLeza”.
Mpawo nibakali kwiimba lwiimbo, bakazwa baya kuchilundu chaOlivisi.
Jesu wakati kuli mbabo, “Moonse muyoowa, mbuuli mbukulembedwe, 'Ndiyowuma mwembeli butanga buyomwayika'.
Pesi kandili ndabuka, ndilamwindila kunembo kuya kuGalili”.
Pita wakateedi, “Nikuba kuti boonse bawa pesi mebo pe”.
Jesu wakati kulinguwe, “Kasimpe ndakwambila, sunu iyii, mbubo busiku oobuno mukombwe kutana kokolika tubili uyondikaka tutatu.
Lino Pita wakati kuti kandeleede kufa ayebo, mezyo chikozyene.
Bakasika kubusena butegwa Gesemane, mpawo Jesu wakati kuli basikwiya bakwe, “Amukkale aawo nenchiya kukukomba”.
Wakabweza Pita, Jemusi a Joni, winka aabo, watalika kulilya akulikataazya.
Wakati kuli mbabo, “Muuya wangu wawusa loko, nikuba kusika kulufu. Muchaale aawa kamulindide”
Kabachiya kunembo, Jesu wakawida aansi akukomba kuti nichali kukonzeka chiindi echi chimwiinde.
Wakati, “Abba, Taata, kuti nduwe zintu zyoonse zilakonzeka. Gwisya nkomechi eeyi kuli ndime pesi kutabi kuyanda kwangu pe, asi kwako”.
Wakaboola, wakajana baloona, mpawo wakati kuli Pita, “Sayimoni, muloona na? Tamukonzyi kulindila hola lyomwe?
Mulindile akukomba kuti mutanjili mukusunkwa.
Lino wakazwa lwabili wakukomba majwi ngawonya.
Nakaboola lubo wakajana balokoona, nkambo meso aabo akali alema. Tebakaziba chakwamba kuli nguwe.
Wakaza kachitatu wakati kulimbabo, “Muchili koona na? Kwazulila! Chindi chasika. Amulange! Mwana aMuntu uli kuziigwa mumaanza abasizibi.
Munyampuke; tweende. Amulange, sikunduuzya waba afwifwi.”
Kachili kwambula, Judasi, umwi wabali kkumi ababili wakasika, ankamu mpati kabajisi mapanga amasumu, kuzwa kubapati babapayizi, abalembi, abaalu.
Lino sikumuuzya wakapa chitondeezyo, wati, “Ooyo ngundiyomyonta ngonguwe. Amumujate mumtole atamuchiji pe.”
Awo Judasi nakasika, mpawoawo wakaya kuli Jesu wati, “Muyisi!” Akumumyonta.
Mpawo bakabikka maboko alinguwe bamwaanga.
Pesi umwi wababo bakalimvwi wakasomona ipanga wakakwazula akudunsula kutwi kwamuzike wamupayizi mupati.
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Mwaza mbuli muyanda sikubba, amapanga, amasumu kuzondijata?
Aboobo ndali anywebo mazuba woonse akuyisya mun'anda yaLeza, temwakandisunga pe. Pesi eechi chachitika kuti malembe azuzikizigwe”.
Boonse mbakali aabo Jesu bakamusiya akumuchija.
Mwalumi munini, wakali samide mulembo luzutu uteentema ngwakali lipopode wakali kutobela Jesu.
Lino baalumi nibakamwanga wakasiya mulembo uteentema wachija kali chintanda.
Bakatola Jesu kumupayizi mupati. Bamubunganina bapayizi bapati, abaalu abalembi.
Lino Pita wakali buya butobela kulaale kulubaya kwamupayizi mupati wakakkala akati kabalindizi bakali afwifwi amulilo kuti akasalilwe.
Lino bapati babapayizi ankuta yoonse yaba Juda yakali kuyandula bukamboni bubi kuchita kuti bamutole kulufu. Pesi tebakabujana pe.
Eelyo biingi bakaleta bukamboni bwakubeja atala aanguwe, pesi bukamboni obu tebwali kuzuminina pe.
Bamwi bakayima akupa bukamboni bwakubeja atala anguwe; Kabati,”
Twakamumvwa kati, 'Ndiyomwaya n'anda yaLeza yakwa amaanza, mukati kwamazuba atatu ndiyoyiyaka imbi itachitwi amaanza”.
Nikuba boobo bukamboni bwabo tebwakazumina pe.
Mupayizi Mupati wakayimikila akati kabo wabuzya Jesu, “Tujisi nsandulo na? Ninzi eezi aaba balumi nzibapeda bukamboni atala anduwe?”
Asi we wakawumuna takwe nakasandula chintu pe. Alubo mupayizi mupati wakati wakamubuzya kuti, “Nduwe Kkilisito, Mwana wawulongezedwe?”
Jesu wakati, “Ndime! alimwi muyoomubona Mwana aMuntu ulikkede kululyo lwaluboko lwasinguzu akuboola amayoba akujulu.”
Mupayizi mupati wakadelula zisamo mpawo wati, “Sa tuchiyanda bukamboni?
Mwamvwa mbwamba chisapi. Muzeezo wanu ngwakutyeni?” Mpawo bakamupa mulandu welela lufu.
Bamwi bakatalika kumuswida mate akumuvumba busyu akumunabba akwamba kuti kuli nguwe, “Sinsima!” Basolooli bakamubweza akumuuma.
Eelyo Pita kachili munsi alubaya umwi wabalanda basimbi bamupayizi mupati wakaza kuli nguwe.
Nakabona Pita kali kuyota mulilo, wakalangisisya akwamba kuti, “Mwakali aamwi a Jesu muNazaleta”.
Pesi wakakaka akwamba kuti tandimuzi pe nikuba kumvwa atala anzinokwambuula anzizyo”. Lino wakazwa waya anze aamulyango. Alimwi malembe achindi alawungizya. Mpawo mukombwe wakokolika.
Pesi mulanda musimbi wakamubona mpawo watalika kwamba lubo kuti aabo balimwi mpawo, “Ooyu mwalumi nguumwi wabo!”
Lino wakakaka alubo. Nikwakayinda chindi chinini aabo bakalimvwi aawo bakati kuli Pita, kasimpe nduwe umwi wabo, nkambo alako uli muna Galiliyeni.”
Mukombwe mpawawo wakakokolika kachibili. Mpawo Pita wakayeeya majwi aaJesu ngakamwambila:
“Mukombwe kutana kukokolika kachibili, uyondikaka tutatu” alimwi wakawusa akulila.
Muchifumofumo, bapati babapayizi bakabungana abaalu abalembi abasilutwe babbooma lya Judiya. Bakamwanga bamutola. Akumupeda kuli Payileti.
Payileti wakabuzya kuti, “Nduwe Mwami waba Juda na?” Wakasandula kuti, “Wamba”.
Bapayizi bapati bakali kumutamikizya zintu zyiingi.
Alubo Payileti wakabuzya, “Tosanduli na?” Langa kuvula zintu zyiingi nzibali kukutamikizya!”
Pesi Jesu takwe naakamusandula, mpawo eecho chakamugambya Payileti.
Kuchindi chapobwe, Payileti wakaba angunywida umwi wabange, mwange ngubatanoli bakumbila.
Mpawo kwakali mwalumi utegwa Bbanabbasi muntolongo kalamwi abapati bakali amilandu yabujayi muchindi chalupapi.
Makamu akaza kuli Payileti mpawo bakatalika kukumbila kuti achite echo nchakali kunoonga wabachitila.
Payileti wakabasandula wati, “Muyanda kuti ndimwangunwide Mwami waba Juda na?”
We wakalizi kuti nkambo kabbivwe bapayizi bapati nchibakaaba Jesu kulinguwe.
Pesi bapayizi bapati bakasungilizya makamu kuti balilile kwangununwa kwaBbanabbasi.
Payileti wakasandula lubo wakati, “Mpoo ndichite biyeni aMwami wabaJuda?”
Bakawompolola lubo, “Ngagankaminwe!”
Payileti wakabambila kuti, “Mulandunzi ngwakachita?” Pesi bakayinkilila kunembo akoompolola kuti, “Amumugankamine”.
Payileti wakayanda kukutisika makamu, elyo wakabangunwida Bbanabbasi. Wakamupenzya Jesu mpawo wamupeda kuti akagankaminwe.
Basilumamba bakamutola bamunjizya mubbetekelo (alingawo maanda afulumende mapati), mpawo bakayita imbunga yabasilumamba.
Bakamubikka kunembo wantumbula Jesu, mpawo bakazinga musini wamaamvwa elyo bakamusamika.
Bakatalika kumuseka kabati, “Mwalemekwa, Mwami wabaJuda!”
Bakali kumumuma mumtwe atete mpawo bakamuswida mate. Bamufugamina akumukotamikila mitwe.
Nibakamana kumusonsya, bakamugwisya mulembo wantumbula mpawo bamusamika zisamo zyakwe, elyo bakamutola kuyomugankamina.
Umwi mwalumi, Sayimoni wakuSayilini, wakayabuza kuzwa kumunzi (wakali wisi wa Alekizanda a Lufusi), mpawo bakamwangila kuti amubwezele chiingano.
Basilumamba bakeeta Jesu kubusena butegwa Gologota (busenandululwa kutegwa, “Busena bwazipepe zyamyitwe”).
Bakamupa wayini ivwelengene andulwe, pesi takanywa pe.
Bakamugankamina mpawo bakaabana zisamo zyakwe bakasaana chisolo kuti basilumamba babone kuti umwi ulabweza chisamo chaali
Chakali chiindi chahola lyatatu nibakamugankamina.
Achikwankwani bakalemba mulandu ngubakamupa, bakati, “Mwami wabaJuda”.
Bakamugankamina aamwi ababbi babili, umwi kululyo lwakwe umwi kulumwensi lwakwe.
Malembi mabotu akale taakwe Makko 15: 28, (Malembe akazuzikizigwa akuti, “Wakabb. alikizigwa amwi abasikutyola milawo)
Abo bakali kwiinda nibakamubona bakali kutikinia mitwe kabati, “Iiwe! nokonzya kumwaya chikombelo mpawo akuchiyakulula mumazuba otatwe,
Livune useluke achingano!”
Munzila ikozyenie, bapati bapayizi bakati kumuniaka antoomwe abalembi, mpawo bakati, “Wakafutula bamwi, pesi takonzyi kulifutula.
Akube kuti Kilisito, Mwami wa Izilayeli, aseluka lino achingano ikuti tubone akusyoma.” Abalabo bakagankaminwa amwi anguwe bakamuseka.
Muhola lyamusanu alimwi, mudima wakazulila busena boonse kusikila kuhola lyamusanu aane.
Muhola lyamusanu aane Jesu wakalila ajwi pati wakati, “Eloyi, Eloyi, sabakkatani?” echi chipandulula kuti, “Leza wangu, Leza wangu wandisilaanzi?”
Bamwi babaabo bakayimvwi kumbali bakamvwa majwi akwe mpawo bakati, “Langa, ulikwiita Elija.”
Umwi wakachijana, wakanika nsinsa muwayini ilweela, wachibikka atete, mpawo wakamupa kuti anywe. Mwalumwi oyu wakati, “Atubone naa Elija ulaza kuzomwangununa.”
Elyo Jesu wakalila ajwi pati mpawo wafwa.
Isila lyachikombelo lyakadeluka muzipanzi zibili kuzwa kujulu kusika ansi.
Elyo mupati wabasilumamba balimwaanda wakayimvwi kalangide Jesu naakabona kuti wafwa munzila eyi, wakati, “Masimpe mwalumi oyu wali Mwana waLeza.”
Kwakaliko alimwi banakazi bakali kweebela chakule. Akati kabo kwakali Maliya Magadalini, Maliya (bayina a Jemusi mwanike a Josesi) mwalumi walikutegwa Josesi lino utegwa Jozefu muli Makko 6: 3. Izina liti Josefu lyiimikilila mbuli mbulyakali kwaamba muchiHebbulu, mpawo izina liti Josesi lyiimikilila mbuli mbulyakali kwaambwa muchiGilikki, mpawo a Salume.
Nakali muGalili bakalikumutobela mpawo akuchita milimu yakwe. Alimwi banakazi bayingi abalabo bakali kumusindikila ku Jelusalema.
Nilyakaba golezya, nkambo kakuti lyakaliZuba lya Mabambe, nkuukuti, izuba lilimusanu abuzuba butegwa Sabata,
Jozefu waku Alimatiya wakasika aawo. Wakali kulemekwa kali umwi wabapati bachisi wakali kulindila bwaami bwaLeza. Wakayinka chabulemu kuli Payileti mpawo wakakumbila mutunta waJesu.
Payileti chakamgambya kuti Jesu wakali wafwa kale; wakayita mupati wabasilumamba bali mwaanda mpawo wakabuzya kuti kulinguwe Jesu wafwa.
Elyo Payileti nakaziba kuzwa kumupati wabasilumamba balimwaanda kuti Jesu wafwa, wakuupa Jozefu mutunta.
Jozefu wakawula mulembo utentema wakamwangununa achingano, wamuvungilizya amulembo utentema, mpawo wamulazika muchiyumbwe chamumpako yabbwe. Elyo wakatendelesya bbwe wajala mulyango wachumbwe.
Maliya Magadalini a Maliya bayina a Josesi bakakubona busena Jesu mbwakalazikwa.
Nibwakamana buzuba butegwa Sabata, Meli Magadaleni, Meli banyina aJemusi, a Salome bakawula tununkilizyo kuti bayinke kuyoonanika mutumba wa Jesu.
Chifumo fumo mubuzuba butaanzi bwamviki, zuba mbulyakapasula buyo bakayinka kuchibunda.
Alimwi kabacheenda munzila bakabuzyania umwi awumwi kuti, “Nguni uutakatugwisizye bbwe kuzwa kumulyango wachibunda? ”
Pesi balange buyo, bakabona bbwe lyakali pati oko, kaligwisizigwe kale.
Nibakanjila muchibunda, bakabona mwaalumi mukubusi kasamide chisamo chituba, kakkede kululyo, mpawo bakagamba a kuyoowa.
Wakati kulimbabo, “Mutayoowi. Mulanguula Jesu mu Nazeleta, wakagankaminwa aachiingano. Tawo pe aano, ulibukide! Amulange aabusena mpubakamubikide.
Pesi kamuya, mukaambile basikwiiya bakwe a Pita kuti, ulazulula kunembo lyanu kaya ku Galilii. Nkukonya muyoomubona, mbuli mbwakaamwaambilide,”
Mbubakazwa muchibunda; kabatalika kuchijaana bakalikuteketa kabagambide. Taakwe nchimbakaambilana pe nkaambo bakali yoweede.
[Malembe mayingi aakutanguna abukamboni bwachiindi mubbuku lya Maakko Chandano 16. munchali 9 kusika ku 20 taawo pe. ] Mubuzuba butaanzi bwamviki, naakabuka, wakasanguna kulitondeezya kuli Meli Magadalena, ooyo ngwakagwisya myuuya mibi ili musanu ayiibili.
Wakayinka wakwaambila aabo bakali anguwe, aabo bakali komookaakulila.
Pesi nibakamvwa kuti Jesu muumi akuti wamubona, tebakasyoma pe.
Nikwakiinda zintu eezi, wakalibonia muzila zisiyene kuli babili, nibakalikuyobweenda kuya kumyuunzi.
Bakayinka kuyowambila basikwiya boonse, pesi taakwe nibakabasyoma
Mukweenda kwachiindi Jesu wakalibonia kulibali kkumi awumwi nibakali kulya; wakabakalalila mukutasyoma akuyuma kwamyoyo yabo, nkaambo bakakaka kuzuminina aabo bakamubona naakabuka.
Wakaamba kuti kulimbabo, “Kamuya munyika yoonse alimwi mukakambawukile zilengwa zyoonse.
Kufumbwa uusyoma akubbapatizigwa uyoofutulwa, pesi kufumbwa uutasyomi uyoopegwa mulandu.
Alimwi zigambyo eezi ziyoobatobela boonse basyoma: Bayootanda myuuya mibi muzina lyangu. bayoowambuula mumilaka mipya.
Bayoojata nzoka amaboko aabo, alimwi nibayoonywa chijaya, tachikwe kuyoobachisa pe, bayoobika maanza aabachiswa, alimwi bachiswa bayoopona.”
Mpawo Mwami naakamana kubaambila, wakatolwa kujulu mpawo wakakukkala kuluboko lwalulyo lwa Leza.
Mpawo basikwiiya bakazwa akuyookambawuka koonse koonse, alimwi Mwami wakabeeleka aabo akusiimya jwi lyakwe azitondeezyo zyakali aandilyo.
Biingi bakatola mulimu wakubikka antoomwe zintu zyakazuzikizigwa akati kesu,
mbuli mbuzyakayinzigwa kizosika kulindiswe abaabo kuzwa chiindi bakali bakamboni alubo kabali bala bejwi.
Chakabaanga nchibotu kulindime ambebo - nkaambo ndakachita mfunkununo izulide aatala azeezyo zyakachitika kuzwa kumatalikilo - kuti ndikulembele lugwalo, webo nomusongo Tiofilasi.
Kuti uzibe choonzyo aatala azintu nzuwakayiisigwa.
Mumazuba aHelodi mwami waku Judiya, kwakali umwi mupaizi wakalikutegwa Zekaliya, wakali kwakulubazu lwa Abija. Mukayintu wakwe Elizabeti alubo wakali walunyungu lwa Aaloni.
Bakaliluleme boonse kunembo lya Leza, kabalemeka milawu yoonse anzyatalide Mwami.
Pesi tebakalikwe mwana pe nkaambo Elizabetji wakali ngomwa, alubo bakali bachembaala boonse mulechi chiindi.
Lino kwakasika aachiindi Zekkaliya mpakali mubuliwo bwa Leza, kalikuchita milimu ya bupayizi mbuli mumabambe aakwe.
Mbuli munzila yachiyanza yakusala mupayizi utabeleke, wakali wasaligwa achisolo kuti anjile muchikombelo cha Leza kuti akatente tununkilizyo.
Choonse chibunga chabantu chakali kukomba aanze kuhola eelyo tununkilizyo nitwakali kutentwa.
Mungelo wa Mwami wakalibonia kuli nguwe alimwi wakayima kubbazu lyakululyo lyachipayililo,
Zekaliya, naakamubona wakateketa nkaambo kuyoowa kwakamujata.
Pesi mungelo wakati kulinguwe, “Utayoowi, Zekaliya, nkaambo nkombyo yako yamvwika. Mukako Elizabetki ulakuzyalila mwana mulombe. Uzomuuzika kuti ngu Joni
Uyooba aakukondwa akusekelela, alubo banji bayoobotelwa akuzyalwa kwakwe.
Nkaambo uyooba mupati kubusyu bwa Mwami. atazonywi wayini na zinywigwa zilula, alubo unozwide Muuya Uusalala kuzwa mwida lyabanyina.
Biingi bana ba Izilayili bayobweeda ku Mwami Leza wabo.
Uzoya kunembo lya Mwami mumuuya amumanguzu aa Elija. Uzoochita eezi kuti azosandule myoyo yamataata kuti ibweede kubana babo, kuchitila kuti batalemeki mulawu bazoyende mubusongo bwabaluleme - kuchitila kubambila Mwami bantu babambilidwe nguwe.”
Zekaliya wakati kumungelo.”Ndilaziziba biyeni eezi? Nkaambo ndachembaala abanangu bachembaala.”
Mungelo wakamusandula wati kulinguwe, “Ndime Gabbuliyeli, wiima mububewo bwa Leza. Ndatumwa kuti ndizowambule aanduwe, ndikweetele majwi mabotu aaya.
Langa, uyowumuna, tokoyokonzya kwaambula pe, kuyosika zikachitike zintu eezi. Eezi zyachitika nkaambo taakwe niwasyoma majwi aangu, ayoozuzikizigwa muchiindi cheelede.”
Lino bantu bakalikulinda Zekaliya, bakagamba kuti nkaambonzi naatola chiindi chilamfu chiloobu kachili muchikombelo.
Pesi naakazwida aanze takachili kukonzya pe kwaambula. Bakakubona kuti wakabona chilengaano nakali muchikombelo. Wakalikwaambuula katondeeka biyo muchuumunizi.
Chiindi chakumana kwamulimu wakwe nichakasika wakabweeda kung'anda yakwe.
Musule lyamazuba aaya, mukayintu wakwe Elizabeti wakajata da. Wakalisisa kwamyeezi musanu. Wakaamba kuti,
“Eechi nchaandichitila Mwami naakandilanga wandimvwida luzyalo kuti andigwisye mawuse kunembo lyabantu.
Mumweezi wamusanu awumwi, mungelo Gabbuliyeli wakatumwa kuzwa kuli Leza kuya kudpolopo lyaku Galilii litegwa Nazaleta,
kuya kuli nakalindu wakatangidwe kumwaalumi wakalikutegwa Jozefu. Wakali walunyungu lwa Devidi, alubo pzina lyamusimbi lyakali Meli.
Wakasika kulinguwe wati, “Wapona iwe noopedwe luzyalo lupati. Mwami uli aayebo.”
Pesi wakanyonga kapati amajwi aamungelo alwimwi wakagamba kuti nkujuzigwa kulibiyeni ooku.
Mungelo wakati kulinguwe, “Utayoowi, Meli, nkaambo wajana luzyalo kuli Leza.
Langa uzoojata da uzoozyale mwana mulombe. uzomuuzika zina lyakuti, 'Jesu'.
Unooli mupati alubo unoyitwa kuti Mwana wa Simajulu. Mwami Leza uyomupa chuuno chabwami bwa syanyinakulu Devidi.
Uzooyendelezya ng'anda ya Jakobo mane kukabe kutamani, alimwi bwami bwakwe tabukozoomana pe.
Meli wakati kumungelo, “Ziyoochitika biyeni eezi nkaambo nsinaziba mwaalumi pe?”
Mungelo wakatgi kulinguwe, “Muuya Uusalala uzoosika kulinduwe, alubo nguzu zya Simalelo zizoosika alinduwe. Aboobo ooyo uusalala uutazozyalwe uzootegwa Mwana wa Leza.
Langa munakwenu Elizabeti ulaada lyamwana mulombe mubuchembele bwakwe, lino wanba mumweezi wamusanu awumwi, ooyo wakalikutegwa ningomwa.
Nkaambo taakwe chimukachila pe Leza.
Meli wakati, “Langa ndimulanda waMwami, azibe kulindime mbuli majwi aako.” Mpawo mungelo wakamusiya.
Mpawo mumazuba aayo Meli wakanyamnpuka watgozya kubusena bwazilundu, kudolopo lya Judiya.
Wakanjila mung'anda ya Zekaliya wakujuzya Elizabeti.
Aawo Elizabeti naakamvwa kujuzya kwa Meli, mwana wakali mwida lyakwe wakasotoka, mpawo Elizabeti wakazuzigwa aMuuya Uusalala.
Wakoompolola ajwi pati wati, “Ulilongezezegwe iwe akati kabamwi banakazi, alubo ulilongezezegwe muchelo weda lyako.
Nkamboonzi nikchachitika kuti banyina aMwami wangu basike kulindime?
Nkaambo langa, majwi aako akundijuzya naanjila mumatwi aangu mwana uulimwida lyangu wasotoka alukondo.
Aboobo ulilongezezegwe ooyo uuyoosyoma kuti kuyooba kuzuzikizigwa kwazintu eezi nzyaakambilwa kuzwa kuMwami.”
Meli wakati moyo wangu ulalumbayizya Mwami,
alubo muuya wangu ulalumbayizya Leza mufutuli wangu.
Nkaambo wakalanga chiimo chaansi chamulanda wakwe. Nkaambo amulange, kuzwa lino mazyalane woonse ayondiijta kutghi ndili longezezegwe.
Nkaambo ooyo wandichitila zintu zipati, alimwi zina lyakwe lilasalala.
Luzyalo lwakwe luyoozulila kuzwa kuzyalane kuya kulilimbi zyalane kuli aabo bamuyoowa.
Wakatondeezya nguzu ejanza lyakwe; wakasansaanya aabo balisumpula aatala amizeezzo yamyoyo yabo.
Wakagwisya bana babaami kuzwa kuzyuno zyaabo alimwi wakasumpula aabo bali aachiimo chilaansi.
Wakakutya basinzala azintu zibotu, pesi bavubi wakabaanda kabatakwe chintu.
Wakapa lugwasya kuli Izilayeli mulanda wakwe, kuti ayeeye kutondeezya luse
(mbuli mbakaamba kuli basikale besu) kuli Abraham alunyungu lwakwe.”
Meli wakakkala a Elizabeti kwamyeezi yotatwe mpawo wabweda kung'anda yakwe.
Lino chakasikachiindi chakuti Elizabeti atumbuke aboobo wakatumbuka mwana mulombe.
Basimabambanwa antoomwe abasinzubo zyakwe bakamvwa kuti Leza wakamutondeezya luzyalo, mpawo bakabotelwa aamwi anguwe.
Mpawo mubuzuba bwamusanu aatatu bakasika kuzopalula mwana. Bakalikuyanda kumuuzika kuti “Zekaliya” zina lyawisi.
Pesi banyina bakasandula bati “Pe. ulayitwa kuti ngu Joni.”
Bakati kulinguwe, taakwe pe kuluzubo lwesu loonse ulazina eeli.”
Mpawo bakaambuula awisi anzila yakutondeeka kababuzya kuti uyanda kuti mwana awuzikwe zina lili.
Wisi wakakumbila aakulembela, mpawo wakalemba kuti, “Izina lyakwe ngu Joni.” Boonse zyakabagambya eezi.
Mpawaawo mulomo wakwe wakajulika mpawo lulimi lwakwe lwakaangunuka. Wakaambula akulumbayizya Leza.
Kuoyoowa kwakabasikila boonse bakalikukkala afwiifwi ambabo. Impuwo yoonse eeyi yakazula kumalundu achisi cha Judiya.
Boonse bakazimwa bakazibamba mumyoyo yabo, kabati, “Ooyu mwana uzooba nyamaanzi?” Nkaambo kuboko kwa Leza kwakali aanguwe.
Wisi Zekaliya wakazula Muuya Uusalala mpawo wakasinsima, kati,
“Atembawulwe Mwami, Leza wa Izilayeli, nkaambo wasika kuzogwasya alimwi weeta lufuko kubantu bakwe.
Wakatunyampwida lwija lwalufutuko mung'anda yamulanda wakwe Devidi,
mbuli mbakaambula amilomo yabasinsimi bakwe basalala bakale.
Ulatufutula kuzwa kulibasinkondoma akulibaabo batusulide.
Uzoochita eezi mukutondezya luzyalo kumataata esu akuyeeya chizuminano chakwe chisalala,
chikonke nchaakachita kuli Abbulahamu taatesu.
Wakakonka kuti swe, nitwakafutgulwa kuzwa kumaanza abasinkondoma, tuzomubelekele kaututayoowi pe,
mubusalali amubululami kunembo lyakwe mumazuba esu woonse.
Iyii, anduwe, nomwana, uzoyitwa kuba musinsimi waSimajulu, nkaambo uzoyhinda kunembo lya Mwami koyabubamba nzila, kobambila bantu mukusika kwakwe,
kupa luzibo lwalufutuko kubantu bakwe akulekelelwa kwazibi zyabo.
Eezi zizoochitika nkaambo kaluzyalo lwa Leza wesu, nkambo mukuyozwa kwazuba uzoosika kuzotugwasya,
likabamunikile bakkede mumudima amumweenzule walufu. Uyoochita eezi kuti akazulwide mawulu eesu munzila yaluumuno.”
Lino mwana wakakomena wasima mumuuya, alimwi wakakkala munkanda kuyoosika buzuba mbwakalitodeezya kuli Izirayeli.
Lino mulayo mazuba, kwakasika akuti oyo siza Agasitasi wakatamuna mulumbe kulayilila kuti kubalwa kwachitwe kwabantu boonse bapona munyika.
Oku kwakali kubalwa kutanzi kwakachitwa chiindi kkwiniliyasi nakali mwendelezyi wa Siliya.
Aboobo muntu woonse wakiinka kudolopo lyakwe kuti akalembesye kubalwa
Josefa alakwe wakinka atala kuzwa ku Galile, kuzwa kudolopo lya Nazaleta, kuya kuJudiy, kuya kudolopo lyaDavida, oyo utegwa Betelehema, nkaambo wakali wang'anda a lunyungu lwaDavida.
Wakayinka ooko kuti akalembesye aantomwe a Meli, ooyo ngwakatuminide alumwi wakali aatambu.
Lino kwakasika kuti biyo nibakachiliko oko, ichindi chakasika chakwe kuti atumbuke mwana wakwe.
Wakatumbuka mwana mulombe, mwana mutanzi wakwe, alimwi wakamuputila mumalembo akasala malamfu alimwi wamulazika muchata, nkaambo tekwakalikwe busena bulabo munga'nda yabenzu.
Kwakaliwo bembeli mubusena obo bakalikukkala mumyuunda, kabalo kulinda butanga bwabo mansiku.
Mungelo wamulami wakaboneka kuli mbabo, alimwi abulemu bwaMwami bwaka yubununwa alimbababo, alimwi bakazula akuyowa kupati.
Mpawo mungelo wakamba wakati, “Mutayowinkambo ndamwetela makani mabotu ayo atazo yete kukondwa kupati kubantu boonse.
Sunu mufuli wazyalilwa ndinywe mudolopo lyaDavida nguKKilisto mwami!
Echi nchichitondezyo chitakapegwe kuli ndinywe. Mulojana mwana kaputilidwe mulembo likasalaalimwi kalede luchaata.”
Mpawo mpawo kwakaliwo antomwe abangelo biingi loko bazwa kujulu, kulumbaizya Leza alimwi kabati,
“Bulemu kuli Leza usumpukide, alimwi ngakube luumuno munyika akati kabantu amwi amoyo ngwaboteledwe.” Amwi malembo achiindi achi Greeki alakupeleta kusiyenesiyene oko kubona kwaamba kwamabala abili akonzya kwaamba zilikumamanino amabala mache a muchala 14, yabili nkili njiyandisigwa. Kubona kwaamba nkoku.” chiyandisisyo chibotu kubantu kana akati kabantu alumwi awoyo we (LEZA) ngwabo teledwe
Kwakaba kuti awo bangelo kabali bayinka kuzwa alimbabo kuya kujulu, bembeli bakati kuli umwi awumwi, “ngatwiinke lino ku Betelehema alimwi tukabone echi chintu chachitika, echo Mwami nchatuyubnwida.
Bakafwambanina nkuko alumwi bakujana Malia, Josefa, amwana oyo wakalede muchata
Kuzwawo abo nibakabamubona, bakazibisya ezyo zimbakali babuzigwa bo atala amwana.
Boonse abo bakamvwa bakagamba kuli zezyo zyakambwa abembeli.
Pesi Maliya wakali kuyeya a makani ngakali wamvwa, wakalondolawo mumoyo wakwe.
Bembeli bakabweda kabalumbaizya akutembawula Leza kuli zyoonse ezyo zibakamvwa akubona, mbuli mbubaka mbilwa.
Elyo kwakiinda mazuba masanu aatatu, elyo nakabalulwa, wakuzikwa wategwa Jsu, izina ndyakapedwe amungelo musule katana mintwa mwida
Elyo ilangililwa mweelwe yamazuba akulisalazya kwabo nakiinda, mbuli mumulawo waMozesi, bo bakamweta kuchikombelo kuJelusalema kulomupeda kumwaami.
Mbuli mbukulembedwe mumulawu wamwami, “woonse mwana mulombe ujula ida ulo bikkwa kumbali kuMwami.”
Abobo bakapa chipaizyo mbuli ezyo zyakambidwe mumulawu wamwana, “inziba zibili nabana bankuilimba.
Amubone kwakali mwalumi muJelusalema ula zina litegwa Simiyoni, alumwi oyo mwalumi wakali luleme a kulipeda. Wakali kalangilila kumbilizigwa kwabaIzilayeli, alubo muuya usalala wakala tala anguwe.
Zyakali zyayubununwa kuli nguwe amuya usalala kutitakozobona lufu katanakubona uNanikidwewaMwami.
Kazulwidwa aMuuya, Simiyoni waka sika muchikombelo. Elyo bazyali bakanjizya mukati mwana Jeso, kulo muchitila mbuli chiyanza chabo chamulawo.
Wakamubweza mumaboko aakwe alimwi walumbaizya Leza, alimwi wakati,
“Lino leka mulandawako ayiinde mulumuno, mwami, mbuli ijwi lyako.
Nkaambo menso angu abona lufutuko lwako,
olo mbwakambilwa abuliwo bwabantu boonse.
“Mumuni wachiyubunuzyo kuli bamasi alimwi bulemu kubantu bako izilayeli.”
Wisi abanyina, bakagambilwa aatala azintu zyakalikwaambulwa aatala amwana wabo.
Simiyoni wakabalongezya mpawo wakati kuli banyina, “Amulange mwana ooyu ulisalidwe kuti kube kuwa akusumpulwa kwabamwi bantu biingi muli Izirayeli achitondeezyo chikakidwe -
alimwi ipanga liyoyasa muuya wako - kuchitila kuti myoyo myiingi ikayubununwe.”
Musinsimi mwanakazi uutegwa Ana wakaliwo. Wakali mwana musimbi waFanuwelo kuzwa kumukowa wa Asha. Wakali wapona amulumi wakwe minyaka ili musanu ayibili kuzwa kubusimbi bwakwe.
Alimwi wakali mukamufu kwamwinyaka ili makumi musanu aatatu atune. Takwe nakazwide muchikombelo pesi wakali kubelekela kulyimya a kukomba mansiku, asikati.
Kuli ndilelyo wola wakaswena afwifwi kuli mbabo almwi wakatalika kupa kulumba kuli Leza, alimwi wakambula alubo aatala amwana kubantu boonse abo bakali kulindila kufutulwa kwaJelusalema.
Eelyo aabo boonse nibakamanisya nzibakeelede kuchitambuli mulawo wamwami, bakabweeda ku Galilii, kudolopo lyabo lya Nazaleta.
Mwana wakakomena alimwi wakasima, kuyungizya mubusongo, alimwi luzyalo lwaleza lwakali aanguwe
Bazyali bakwe bakali kwiinka munyaka umwi awumwi ku Jelusalema kupobwe lya kwindilila.
Awo nakaba aminyaka kkumi ayibili, bakabweda lubo mbuli chiindi chachiyanza chabo kupobwe.
Nibakakkala mazuba azulide aa pobwe, bakabweda kumunzi. Pesi mulombe Jeso wakasyala ku Jelusalema alimwi bazyali bakwe tebakazipe.
Bakayelela kuti wakali akabunga ako nkibakayobwenda aako, mpawo bo bakenda musinzo wazuba limwi. Mpawo bakasanguna kumulangula akati kanzubo zyabo abeenzinyina.
Eelyo nibakamubula, bakabweda ku Jelusalema alimwi bakatalika kumuyandula nkuko.
Zyakachitika kuti musule lyamazuba aatatu bakasanguna kumuyandula mung'anda ya Leza, kakkede akati kabayisyi, kalokubaswilizya akubabuzya mibuzyo.
Boonse bakamumvwa bakagamba kukumvwisisisya kwakwe akunsandulo zyakwe
Elyo nibakamubona bakakankabala. Banyina bakati kulinguwe, “Mwanaangu, nkambonzi nwatujata enzila eyi? Langa, wuso andime twalikukuyandula achakutankalinkana.”
Wakati kulimbabo, “Nkambonzi nimwalikundiyandula? Temwazi na kuti ndeelede kuba mungánda yandeende?”
Pesi bo tebakamvwisisya nzyakalikwamba awayo majwi.
Elyo wakabweda kumunzi kulimbabo kuNazaleta alimwi wakali kulibombya kuli mbabo. Banyina bakalondola zyoonse ezi mumoyo wabo.
Pesi Jeso wakaya kunembo akukomena mubusongo a muchiimo, alimwi wakayungizya kuluzyalo kuli Leza aku bantu
Mumunyaka wakkumi amusanu mubweendelezi bwa Tibeliyasi Kkayisala - aawo Pontiyasi Payileti nakali mwendelezyi waku Judiya, Heloda kali mwendelezyi waku Galilii, mwana wakwabo Filipo kali mweendelezi wachisi chaku Ituliya a Tilankonitis, a Lisaniyasi kali mwendelezyi waku Abilene,
kuzwa kubupayizyi bwa Anasi aKkefasi - ijwi lya Leza lyakasika kuli Joni mwana wa Zakaliya munkanda.
Wakeenda muzisi zyoonse zizyuungulukide Joodani kakambauka lubbabbatizyo lwakusanduka akulekelela kwazibi.
Mbuli mbukulembedwe mubbuku lyamakani aIsaya musinsimi, “Ijwi lyasikompolola munkanda, 'Amubambenzila yamwami, amululamike nzila zyakwe
Yonse mimpata iyozuzukizigwa, a zilundu zyoonse atulundu tuyoba ansi amigwagwa ipilingene iyo lulamikwa, amasen aatabambinkene ayooyakwa akuba migwagw,
bantu boonse bayoobona lufutuko lwa Leza.'”
Mpawo Joni wakati kumakamu akalikuza kuzo bbabbatizigwa anguwe, “Nywebo nobana bachipile! ngwani wakamuchenjezya kuti muchije kuzwa kubukali bulokuza?
Aaboobo, muzyale michelo mibotu iitondezya kusanduka alimwi mutataliki kwaamba mukati kanu, “Tula Abulahamu kali taata wesu; mbundamwambila kuti Leza ulakonzya kusumpula bana ba Abulahamu kuzwa kumabwe aya.
Alino kaleba kalibikidwe kale kumiyanda yamisamu. Aboobo kufumbwa musamu utazyali muchelo mubotu ulawugonkela kunsi akuuwalila mumulilo.”
Alimwi makamu akendelela kunembo akumubuzya bakati, “Niinzi mpawo nzitutachite?”
Wakasandula akuti kulimbabo, “Na kulumwi uujisi twakuzwata tubili, uleelede kwabana amuntu utakwe ayooyo ujisi chakulya ayiite mbobo.”
Abasimutelo abalabo bakaza kuzo bbabbatizigwa, akwamba kuli nguwe kuti, “Muyisi, niinzi nchitweelede kuchita?”
Wakati kulimbabo, “Mutakabwezi mali nyiingi njimutabuzizigwe kubweza.”
Bamwi basilumamba abalabo bakamubuzya, bakati, “Aniswe ninzi nchitweelede kuchita?” Wakati kulimbabo, “Mutakabwezi mali kufumbwa kulumwi changuzu, alimwi mutakapenzyi omwe chakubeja. amukakutisikane amiholo yanu.”
Lino bantu nibakachili kulindila chakupekezya kusika kwa Kkilisto boonse bakali kugamba mukati kamooyo yabo aatala aJoni, kutii ngunguwe Kkilisto.
Joni wakasandula wakati kuliboonse, “Imebo lwangu ndamubbabbatizya amanzi, pele kulumwi ulobuza ulanguzu kwiinda ndime, aboobo nsikonzyi nikuba nkwangununa misungo yansangu zyakwe. Uyomu bbabbatizya aMuya Uusalala antomwe amulilo.
Kajisi pologwe yakupupuluzya mujanza lyakwe chakusalazya lubuwa lwakwe akubunganya bbali munganda yakwe. Pele uyowumpa buungu amulilo alimwi mulilo tukoyoozima pe.”
Mubwingi bwakumusumpula Joni wakalikwambula makani mabotu kubantu.
Alimwi Heloda kali mwendelezyi wakazumizigwa kukukwata mwanakazi wamwana wakwabo Helodiyasi azyoonse zintu zibi Heloda nzyakachitide,
wakayungizya ezi kulimbabo boonse, akujalila Joni muntolongo.
Lino nichakasika chiindi aawo bantu boonse bakabbabbatizigwa Jesu alakwe wakabbabbatizigwa, nibakachili kukomba, majulu akajulika,
aMuuya Uusalala muchimo chamubili wakaza mbuli nziba, alimwi jwi lyakazwa kujulu “Ulimwana wangu ngwendiyandisisya. Ndabotelwa anduwe.”
Mpawo Jesu naakatalika mulimu wakwe wakali amyaaka yakuzyalwa makumi aatatu. Wakali mwana mulombe (mbuli mbukwakaklikuyelelwa) kuti Josefa mulombe waHeli,
mwana waMatati, mwana waLevi, mwana Melichi, mwana wa Janayi, mwana waJosefa.
Josefa wakali mwana wa Matatiyasi, mwana wa Amos, mwana wa Naumi, mwana wa Esili, mwana wa Nagayi,
mwana wa Mati, mwana wa Matatiyasi, mwana wa Simiyoni, mwana wa Josekki, mwana wa Juda.
Joda wakali mwana waJowanani, mwana wa Lesa, mwana wa Zelubbabbeli, mwana wa Salatiyeli, mwana wa Neli,
mwana wa Melikki, mwana wa Elimadamu, mwana wa Eli,
mwana wa Joshuwa, mwana wa Eliyeza, mwana wa Jolimu, mwana wa Matati, mwana wa Levi
Levi wakali mwana wa Simiyoni, mwana wa Juda, mwana wa Josefa, mwana wa Eliyakim, mwana wa
Meliya, mwana wa Mena, mwana Matata, mwana wa Natani, mwana wa Davida,
mwana wa Jese, mwana wa Obbeti, mwana wa Bbowazi, mwana wa Salimoni, mwana wa Nasiyoni.
Nashoni wakali mwana wa Aminadabu, mwana Adimini, mwan wa Alini, mwana wa Heziloni, mwana wa Perez, mwana wa Juda,
mwana wa Jakkobo, mwana wa Isakka, mwana wa Abbulamu, mwana wa Tela, mwana wa Nawoli,
mwana wa Selugi, mwana wa Lewu, mwana wa Pelegi, mwana wa Ebba, mwana wa Shela.
Sila wakali mwana wa Kkayinani, mwana wa Alipazada, mwana wa Semu, mwana wa Nowa, mwana wa Lameki,
mwana wa Metusela, mwana wa Inoki, mwana wa Jaledi, mwana wa Mahalaleli, mwana wa Kkayini,
mwana wa Inosi, mwana wa Seti, mwana wa Adamu, mwana wa Leza.
Mpawo Jesu, kazwide Muuya Uusalala, wakaboola kuzwa kumulonga wa Jodani, wakazulwidwa a Muuya kuya munkanda
ooko nkwakaakusunkwa mazuba makumi one adyabbulosi. Takwe nchakalya mumazuba aayo, kumamanino achiindi echo wakaba aanzala.
Dyabbulosi wakati kulinguwe. “na kana koli mwana wa Leza lailila ibwe eli libe chinkawa.”
Jesu wakamusandula wati, “Zililembedwe, 'Muntu taponi achinkwa luzutu pe.”'
Mpawo dyabbulosi wakazulida Jesu akutomudenzya bwaami boonse bulanyika muchindi chinini.
Mpawo dyabbulosi wakati kulinguwe, “Ndilapa nduwe bwendelezi boonse abulemu mbuli mbundakabupegwa, alimwi ndilakonzya kupa kufumbwa ngundiyanda.
Kuti mpawo, na wafugama akundikomba, zilaba zyako.”
Pesi Jesu wakamusandula wati, “Zililembedwe, 'Ulelede kukomba Mwaami Leza wako, akumumanina milimu yakwe.”'
Mpawo dyabbulosi wakatola Jesu ku Jelusalema akumubikka ansonge yakaluli katempele, akumwambila kuti, “Na koli mwana wa Leza liwaalile, aansi kuzwa aawa.
Nkaambo kulilembedwe kuti, 'Uyolailila bangelo bakwe atala andinywe, kuti bakukwabilile,
mpawo bayokunyampula amaboko aabo, kuchitila kuti utakaligubbuli.'”
Nakamusandula Jesu wakati, “Kulaambidwe kuti, 'Utabiki Mwami Leza wako kumisunko.”
Mpawo diyabbulosi nakamana ku sunka Jesu, wakeenda wakamusiya kusikila chiindi chimbi.
Jesu wakabweda ku Galillaya munguzu zyamuuya, a makani atala anguwe akazulila mukati kachisi chizyungulukide.
Mpawo wakasanguna kuyisya muzikombelo zyabo alimwi wakalumbaizigwa aboonse.
Nakasika ku Nazaleta nkwakakomenezegwa, a mbuli muchiyanza, wakannjila muchikkomnbelo muzuba bwa sabata wakayimikila akubala chakompolola.
Mabhuku amunsinsimi Isaya akapegwa mumaboko akwe. Wakajula bhuku akujana ndawu yakalembedwe kuti.
“Muuya wa Leza uli aalindime, nkaambo wakandinaanika kuti ndaambe makani mabotu kuli bafwaba, wakandituma kuzowamba lwaangunuko kuli aabo baangidwe akuzobonia batakuboni, kwangununa aabo baadyaminizigwe,
kuzowamba munyaka wa Luse.”
Nakajula mabhuku, wakapa lubo kuli baka bungene kabakkede aansi. Menso aboonse bakali muchikombelo kamulangide.
Wakatalika kwambula ambabo, “Sunu eli jwi lyazuzikizigwa mukumvwa kwanu.”
Boonse awo bakambula zibotu atala anguwe akugamba majwi aakwe alumbayizigwa akalikuzwa mumulomo wakwe, bakali kuti, “Ooyu temwana wa Josefa na?”
Wakati kulimbabo, “Chamasimpe muyowaamba kasimpi aaka kulindime, musilisi liponye omwini. Kufumbwa nzitwakamvwa nzuwakachita mu Kapenawumu, ita zikozyenie akudolopo lyakulindinywe.
Pele wakati, “Nchobeni ndamwambila kuti takwe musinsimi utambulwa mudolopo lyakwe.
Pele mukasimpe ndamubuzya kuti kwakali bamuka bafu biingi mu Izilayeli muchiindi cha Elayija, ijulu nilyajalwa kwaminyaka iitatu amyeezi iilamusanu awumwi alimwi nzaala mpati yakasika munyika.
Pele Elayija taakwe nakatumwa nikuba kuli umwi wabo, pele kuli Zalafati mu Sidoni, kulimukamufu ukkala nkukooko.
Kwakali bali aazipele biingi mu Izilayeli kwamazuba a Elisya musinsimi, pele takwe nikuba umwi wakali salazidwe kusiya Namani muSayilini.”
Boonse bantu muchikombelo bakazula kuyoowa nibakamvwa zintu eezi.
Bakabuka bamutanda kuti azwe mudolopo akumuizya atala akalundu idolopo lyabo nkulyakayakilidwe nkumbali kulundu, kabayanda kuti bakamutontele aansi.
Pesi wakayinda akati kabo waya kuli bumbi busena.
Alimwi wakeendelela akuya ku Kkapenamu, idolopo lilimu Galilii, alimwi wakasanguna kubayiisya atala aSabata.
Bakagamba enjisyo yakwe, nkaambo wakali kwambula changuzu.
Lino muchikombelo kwakali mwaalumi wakali aamuuya mubi wadayimona, alimwi wakalila akoompolola ajwi pat,
“Aah! Niinzi nzitwelede kuchita anduwe, Jesu waku Nazareta? Wasika kuzotujaya na? Ndilizi kuti nduweni - Uusalala wa Leza!”
Jesu wakamutukila dayimona, akwaamba kuti, “Utaambuli zwa mulinguwe. Aawo dayimona nakamuwisya mwaalumi aakati kabo, wakazwa mulinguwe, alimwi telyakamuchisa abunini.
Boonse bantu bakagamba, alimwi bakaliswini kwambula atala anzizyo umwi awuumwi. Bakat, “Musyobo nzi wamabala ali obu? Wakulayilila myuuya mibi chabwendelezi anguzu alimwi yazwa.”
Alimwi makani mabotu akatalika kuyanzala kumabazu woonse akuchisi.
Mpawo Jesu wakazwa muchikombelo, alimwi wakanjila mung'anda ya Sayimoni. Lino banyinazyala ba Sayimoni bakalikuchiswa akupya mubili, alimwi bakabakombelezezya kuli nguwe.
Mpawo wakayimikila kunembo lyamwanakazi akukalalila kupya kwamubili, alimwi bwakamusiya bulwazi. Mpawo, wakanyampuka akutalika kubakutawukila.
Mpawo zuba nilyakabbila, bantu bakamwetela Jeso boonse bakali aamalwazi asiyenesiyene wakabika maboko akwe kuli boonse akubaponia.
Madayimona alawo akazwa kubayingi babo, kalikulila kaamba kuti, “Uli Mwana wa Leza!” Jesu wakakalalila ma daimona alimwi akutazumizya kuti uaambule nkaambo akalizi kuti ngu Kkilisto.
Lino nibwakasika buzuba bwakulyokezya, wakaya kubusena buumwide. Makamu abantu akalikumulanguula akasika nkwaakabede. Bakeezya kumukasya kuti atazwi pe akati kabo.
Pele wakati kulimbabo, “Ndilelede alimwi kukambawuka ijwi atala abwami bwa Leza kumadolopo miingi, nkaambo aka nkikambo nkindakatuminwa.”
Alimwi wakeendelela kukambawuka muzikombelo zyoonse zyamu Judiya.
Lino kwakachitika kuti bantu nibakabungene munsi aJeso akuswilila jwi lya Leza, awo nakimvwi kulubbazu lwalwizi lwa Genesareti.
Wakabona maato obile kagwisigilwe kunkomwe ya lwizi. Basikuzuba nswi bakali bazwa mulingawo bakali kusanzya tunsabwe twabo.
Jeso wakanjila mulilimwi lya bwaato, ilyakali lya Sayimon, akumukumbila kuti aligwisye kuzwa mumanzi kwamusinzo mufwifwi anyika. Alimwi wakakkala ansi akuyiisya bantu anze abwaato.
Awo nakamana kwambuula, wakati kuli Sayimoni, “Bweeza bwato ububike mumanzi uwaale mansabwe kuti uche.”
Sayimoni wakasandula wati, “Mwaami, twabeleka busiku boonse pesi takwe nchitwajata, pesi mujwi lyako, ndilawala mansabwe.
Lino nibakachita oobo, bakabungika nswi nyinji, a nsabwe zyabo zyakalikudeluka.
Mpawo bakobola benziina bakali muli bumwi bwaato kuti baboole akuzobagwasya. Bakasika akuzuzya maato obile, alimwi batalika kubbila.
Aboobo Sayimoni Pita, nakachibona wakawida kumawulu aJeso wamba, “Kozwa kulindime nkaambo ndimwaalumi uuchita zibi, Mwami.”
Nkaambo wakagamba, aboonse mbakali aabo, kunswi nzibakajata eezyo nzibakatola.
Eechi chakabikkilizya Jemusi a Joni, bana ba Zebediya, bakali basimulimunyina a Sayimoni. Jeso wakati kuli Sayimoni, “Utayoowi nkaambo kuzwa sunu kuya kunembo uyozuba bantu.”
Nibakeeta maato aabo kunze, bakasiya zyoonse akutomubela.
Chakachita kuti nakali kuli limwinya dolopo mwaalumi wakazwide chipele wakali mo. Elyo nakamubona Jeso, wakawida kubusyu bwakwe akumukumbila, wati, “Mwaami, kuti wayanda kondi salazya.”
Mpawo Jeso wakatambika janza lyakwe wamujata, wati “Ndilayanda kosalala.” Mpawaawo chipele chakamusiya.
Wakamulayila kuti atawambili naba omwe, mpawo wakamwambila kuti, “Yinka munzila yako, ukalitondezye kumupayizyi ukatuule chipayizyo chakusalazigwa kwako, mbuli mbwakalailila Mozesi bube bukamboni kuli mbabo.”
Pele impuwo atala anguwe yakiinka kule, elyo makamu abantu akasika antoomwe kuti amvwe kuyisya kwakwe akuponisigwa kumalwazi aabo.
Pesi we wakanoonga waya kumasena asisikene kuyookomba.
Kwati limwi zuba kuli eecho chiindi naakali kuyiisya, kwakali baFalisi abayisyi bamulawu bakali kkede aawo, bakazwide kumasena miingi amu Galili, Judiya aku Jelusalema. Nguzu zya Mwami zyakali anguwe zyakuponia.
Nkabela bamwi baalumi bakaza babwezede umwi mwaalumi aabulo wakayuminide mubili, bakayandula nzila yakumunjizya mukati kuti bamubike aansi kunembo a Jeso.
Tebakajana nzila yakumweeta mukati akambo kamakamu, lino bakinka aachiluli chang'anda baseluzya mwalumi achiluli abulo bwakwe, akati lyabantu kunembo lya Jeso.
Naakabona lusyomo lwabo, Jeso wakati, “Yomwaalumi zibi zyako zyalekelelwa.”
Lino balembi bamulawu aba Falisizi bakatalika kubuzya bakati, “Ngwani oyo waambula chakusampawula ngwani ukonzya kulekelela zibi kunze kwa Leza alikke?
Pesi Jeso wakabona mbubakali kuyeeya, wakasandula wati kuli mbabo, “Nkaamboonzi nimulibuzya mumyoyo yanu?
Nchichili chuuba kwaamba kuti, 'Zibi zyako zyako zyalekelelwa akwaamba kuti nyampuka uyende?'
Pele kuti mukazibe kuti mwana wamuntu ulaanguzu aanyika zyakulekelela zibi, ndati kuli nduwe, “Nyampuka bweza bulo bwako uye kung'anda yako.”
Mpawaawo wakabuka kunembo lyabo wabweza bulo bwakwe mpaakalede. Mpawo wakiinka kung'anda yakwe, kayabulumbayizya Leza.
Boonse bakagamba mpawo balumbaizya Leza. Bakazuzigwa buyoofu bati, “Twabona zintu zyiindilide sunu.”
Musule lyazezi zyakachitika, Jeso wakazwa wayinka eelyo wakabona simutelo uutegwa Levi kakkede aatente lyabasimutelo. Wakati kuli nguwe, “Nditobele.”
Mpawo Levi wakabuka wamutobela wasiya zyoonse musule.
Nkabela Levi wakachitila Jesu pobwe pati mung'anda yakwe, kwakaliko basimutelo biingi abantu bakakkede aabo aatafula kuti balye ambabo
pesi ba Falisi bakalikutongawukila basikwiiya bakwe kabati, “Nkaamboonzi nalya abasimutelo abasizibi?”
Jesu wakabasandula wati, “Bantu batachiswi tabayandi musilisi, pesi luzutu aabo bachiswa.
Tendakazida baluleme pesi aabo basizibi kuti basanduke.”
Bakati kulinguwe, “Basikwiiya ba Joni bakalikulyiimya kulya akukomba abasikwiiya baba Falisi bachita mbubo. Pesi basikwiiya bako balalya akunywa.”
Mpawo Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Mpali na uukonzya kwaamba kulibasikutambwa kupobwe kuti balyiimye chakulya sikukwata kachiliwo?
Pesi buzosika buzuba aawo sikukwata natazo bwezwe kuzwa kulimbabo, kumazuba aayo bazolyimya.”
Lino Jesu wakaamba chikozyanisyo kulimbabo. “Taakwe naba omwe uudelula chigamba chachisamo chipya akuchibelesya aachisamo chikulukulu. Kuti wachita oobo uladeluula chisamo chipya. Lino chigamba chizwa kuchisamo chipya tachikonzyi kweelela kuchisamo chikulukulu.
Taakwe uubika wayini mupya muchibikilo chachiindi. Kuti wachita oobo wayini mupya ulabbalula chibikilo. Lino wayini ooyo uyoofusuka alimwi chibikilo achilacho chilanyonyooka.
Pele wayini mupya welede kubikwa muchibikilo chipya chakubikila wayini.
Taakwe naba omwe uunywa wayini mukulukulu uuyanda kunywa wayini mupya, uwamba kuti wachiindi ulimbubo.
Lino zyakachitika muSabata awo Jesu nakalikuyabweenda akwiinda akati kamyuunda yazilyo, alimwi basikwiya bakwe bakabweza nseke zyazilyo, kabapukapuka akati kamaboko abo, akulya.
Pele bamwi babaFalisi bakati, “Nkaamboonzi nimuchita chitali mumulawu mubuzuba bwaSabata?”
Wakasandula Jesu wakati, “Sa tamunabala eezyo nzyakachita Davita awo naakaba aanzala, mwini ambakali abo?
Wakanjila mung'anda yaLeza alimwi wabweza chinkwa chisalala mpawo walya chisela, alimwi wapa chimwi kuli baabo mbakalabo kuti balye, nikuba chakalimumulawu luzutu kuti bapayizi abalikke bachilye.” Mpawo wakati kulimbabo,
“Mwana a Muntu ngoMwami waSabata.”
Zyakachitika kuti imwi Sabata wakanjila muchikombelo chamaJuda wayisya bantu. Mumoomo mwakali mwalumi wakali akuboko kwachilisyo kwakayumide.
Balembi bamulawo abaFalisi bakamulangisisya kuyanda kubona kuti ulaponya umwi na muSabata, kuti bamujanine kaambo kakumupa mulandu.
Pele wakalizizi nzibakali kuyeeye alimwi wakati kumwalumi wakali akuboko kuyumide, “Nyampuka mpawo wiimikile akati kaboonse.” Aboobo wakanyampuka wayimikila aawo.
Jesu wakati kulimbabo, “Ndamubuzya, chili mumulawu na muSabata kuchita bubotu na bubi kuvuna buumi na kujaya?”
Mpawo wakalangalanga kuli boonse wasikuti kumwaalumi, “Tandibika luboko lwako.” Wakachita mbubo, alimwi lwakatalamuka.”
Pesi bakazula kunyema abasikwaambilana kuti bamuchite buti Jesu.
Zyakachitika mumazuba aayo mpakayinka kuchilundu kukukomba. Wakiinkila kunembo mansiku woonse mukukomba kuli Leza.
Nibwakacha, wakayita basikwiya bakwe kulinguwe, alimwi wakasala bali kkumi ababili, aabo mbakati mbatumwa.
Mazina abatumwa mbaba Sayimoni (oyo ngwakati Pita) a mukulana wakwe Endulu, Jemusi, Joni, Filipu, Bbatolomiyo,
Matayo, Tomasi, Jemusi mwana wa Alufiyasi, Sayimoni walikutegwa muZiloti,
Judasi Sikkaliyoti, wakazoba sikwaaba Jesu.
Pele Jesu wakaseluka kuzwa kuchilundu ambakali aabo mpawo wiimikila antandabale amakamu mapati abasikwiya bakwe a bantu biingi bazwa kuJudiya a kuJelusalema akunkomwe yalwizi lwaTaya a Sidoni.
Bakaza kuzoswiilila kulinguwe akuponesegwa zilwazi zyabo. Bantu bakali kukatazigwa amyuuya mibi bakaponesegwa abalabo.
Woonse wakali munkamu wakali kweezya kumuguma nkambo manguzu akuponya akali kuzwa mulinguwe, alimwi wakabaponya boonse.
Mpawo wakalanga kulibasikwiiya bakwe alimwi wati, “Mulilongezedwe nywebo nobachete, nkambo bwami bwaLeza mbubwanu.
Mulilongezedwe nywebo nimufwa nzala, nkambo muyokkutisigwa. Mulilongezedwe nimulila lino, nkambo muyooseka.
Mulilongezedwe nywebo nimuyosulwa abantu, alimwi bayomusaamika akumusampawula, akaambo kaMwana waMuntu.
Mukabotelwe mubuzuba oobo akusotoka mulukondo, nkambo chakasimpe muyooba ampindu mpati kujulu, nkaambo basikale babo bakajisi basinsimi munzila ilibobu.
Pele chabija kulindinywe nibavubi, nkaambo mwatambula kale luumbulizyo lwanu.
Chabija kulindinywe nimukkusi lino, nkaambo muyooba anzala, chabija kulindinywe nimuseka lino, nkaambo muyolila akukwiila muchindi chitobela.
Chabija kulindinywe na woonse muntu kawamba bubotu andinywe, nkaambo mbubo basikalebabo mbubakabajisi basinsimi bakubeja.
Pele ndati kulindinywe nimulikuswilizya, yanda basinkondonyokwe alimwi muchite zibotu kulimbabo bamusula.
Mulongezye baabo bamutuka alimwi mukombele aabo bamusukuusya.
Kuli wooyo ukuuma seya mupe lubo alimbi. Na umwi muntu wabweza chibaki chaajulu utamwiimi chakunsi.
Pa kumuntu woonse uukukumbila. Na umwi muntu wabweza chintu chako utamwaambili kuti achiboozye kulinduwe.
Mbuli mboyanda kuti bantu bakuchitile weelede kubachtila ayebo mbuboobo.
Na wayanda luzutu aabo bakuyanda mbulumbuunzi buli kulinduwe? Nkaambo nikuba abasizibi balabayanda aabo babayanda.
Na wachitila kabotu aabo bakuchitila kabotu, zikugwasyanzi? Nkaambo abalabo basizibi balazichita eezyo.
Na kogwasya biyo aabo bakonzya kukubweedezya nzuwabapa, chikugwasyayi? Nkaambo basizibi abalabo balapa basizibinyina, kuti bajane mpindu ikozyenie.
Pesi muyande basinkondonyokwe mubachitile zibotu. Mupegwe mutalangili kupegwa lubo aboobo mpindu yenu iyooba mpati alimwi muyooba bana ba Simajulu, nkaambo we lwakwe uli aaluyando nikuba akulaabo batakwe luyando abasizibi.
Mube aaluzya nkaambo Wuso alakwe ulaaluzyalo.
